Method: 提出KoRe方法，将1跳子图压缩为紧凑的离散知识令牌，并将其注入预训练的LLM中，实现对知识的高效、可解释地增强。该方法避免了对模型的重新训练或微调。

Result: 在三个标准基准测试中，KoRe方法表现出与现有方法相当甚至更优的性能，同时显著降低约10倍的令牌使用量，证明了紧凑离散知识表示在提升现代LLM能力方面的有效性与效率。

Conclusion: 通过将知识图谱中的1跳子图以离散紧凑形式注入大语言模型，KoRe实现了知识的有效、高效和可解释的融合，为构建更可靠、低资源消耗的智能系统提供了新路径。

Abstract: Modern Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown impressive performances in user-facing tasks such as question answering, as well as consistent improvements in reasoning capabilities. Still, the way these models encode knowledge seems inherently flawed: by design, LLMs encode world-knowledge within their parameters. This way of representing knowledge is inherently opaque, difficult to debug and update, and prone to hallucinations. On the other hand, Knowledge Graphs can provide human-readable and easily editable world knowledge representations, and their application in knowledge-intensive tasks has consistently proven beneficial to downstream performance. Nonetheless, current integration techniques require extensive retraining or finetuning. To overcome this issue, we introduce KoRe, a methodology to encode 1-hop sub-graphs into compact discrete knowledge tokens and inject them into a LLM backbone. We test the proposed approach on three established benchmarks, and report competitive performances coupled with a significant reduction (up to 10x) in token usage. Our results show that compact discrete KG representations can efficiently and effectively be used to ground modern LLMs.

It refines hypotheses incrementally and integrates findings for grounded decisions. The system supports both inference-time use with large LLMs and training-time distillation into compact open-source models.

In this paper, we introduce ClinSeekAgent, an automated agentic framework for dynamic multimodal evidence seeking that shifts the paradigm from passive evidence consumption to active evidence acquisition.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视觉语言模型虽强调长链式推理，但其在视觉任务上的性能瓶颈主要源于视觉感知不足，而非推理能力本身。因此，亟需系统性地分离并优化感知与推理能力，以突破性能上限。

Method: 将VLM后训练过程分解为三个阶段：视觉感知、视觉推理、文本推理，分别采用针对性的训练数据和方法（如强化学习优化感知）。采用分阶段训练策略，确保感知能力先行稳固，再逐步提升推理能力。同时探索该能力导向课程与传统难度课程的互补性。

Result: 分阶段训练显著优于合并训练，实现1.5%的推理准确率提升和20.8%的推理链长度缩短；在WeMath和RealWorldQA等任务上分别取得+5.2%和+3.7%的性能提升，优于现有开放权重VLM模型。结合能力与难度双维度课程设计带来进一步增益。

Conclusion: 视觉感知是影响VLM性能的关键基础，应优先通过专用数据和强化学习进行优化，并采用分阶段训练方式建立稳固感知基础。该能力导向的分阶段训练策略是一种有效且可扩展的方法，能显著提升模型整体性能，为未来VLM设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Recent advances in vision-language models (VLMs) emphasize long chain-of-thought reasoning; yet, we find that their performance on visual tasks is primarily limited by a lack of visual perception as opposed to reasoning itself. In this work, we systematically study the interplay between perception and reasoning in VLM post-training by decomposing their capabilities into three separate training stages: visual perception, visual reasoning, and textual reasoning, incorporating specialized training data. We demonstrate that visual perception (a) requires targeted optimization with specialized data; (b) serves as a fundamental scaffold that should be solidified through staged training before refining visual reasoning; and (c) is more effectively learned via RL than caption-based SFT. Our experiments across multiple VLMs demonstrate that staged training consistently improves both visual perception and reasoning performance over merged training. Notably, models trained with our approach achieve 1.5% higher reasoning accuracy with 20.8% shorter reasoning traces, suggesting that superior perception reduces the need for excessive reasoning. Furthermore, we show that this capability-based staging represents a new curriculum dimension orthogonal to traditional difficulty-based curricula, and combining both yields further additive gains. Our staged-training models achieve superior performance among open-weight VLMs, establishing advanced results on several visual math and perception (e.g., +5.2% on WeMath and +3.7% on RealWorldQA) tasks compared with the base counterpart.

</details>


### [145] [TIDE: Efficient and Lossless MoE Diffusion LLM Inference with I/O-aware Expert Offload](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20179)
*Zhiben Chen,Youpeng Zhao,Yang Sui,Jun Wang,Yuzhang Shang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: TIDE提出一种资源高效的推理系统，利用扩散过程中专家激活的时序稳定性，通过基于区间的专家刷新策略降低I/O开销和计算瓶颈，无需模型训练即可实现无损加速，在单GPU-CPU系统上对LLaDA2.0-mini和LLaDA2.0-flash分别提升1.4×和1.5×吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AR基方法在部署大规模扩散语言模型（dLLMs）时面临高昂的I/O开销或严重的计算瓶颈，尤其在资源受限设备上挑战更大，亟需更高效的推理优化方案。

Method: 提出TIDE系统，利用扩散过程中专家激活的时序稳定性，设计区间式专家刷新策略，并将推理调度建模为数学规划问题以最小化I/O流量与CPU计算开销。

Result: 在单GPU-CPU系统中，TIDE相较于基线方法在LLaDA2.0-mini和LLaDA2.0-flash上分别实现了1.4×和1.5×的吞吐量提升，且为无损优化，无需额外训练。

Conclusion: TIDE通过高效利用专家激活的时序稳定性，实现了资源受限环境下dLLM推理的显著加速，是一种无需训练的“免费午餐”式优化方案，具有实际部署价值。

Abstract: Diffusion Large Language Models (dLLMs) have emerged as a competitive alternative to autoregressive (AR) models, offering better hardware utilization and bidirectional context through parallel block-level decoding. However, as dLLMs continue to scale up with mixture-of-experts (MoE) architectures, their deployment on resource-constrained devices remains an open challenge. Existing AR-based methods often incur either prohibitive I/O overhead or significant compute bottlenecks. In this work, we propose TIDE, a novel resource-efficient inference system that leverages the temporal stability of expert activations during the diffusion process within the block. Specifically, we leverage the temporal stability of expert activations during the diffusion process within the block and introduce an interval-based expert refresh strategy that updates the expert placement in an I/O-aware fashion. To ensure optimal performance, we formulate the inference scheduling as a mathematical programming problem, solving for the optimal interval that minimizes I/O traffic and CPU computation. Most importantly, TIDE is a lossless optimization that requires no model training, providing a "free lunch" acceleration for dLLM inference. In a single GPU-CPU system, we demonstrate that TIDE achieves up to 1.4$\times$ and 1.5$\times$ throughput improvements over prior baselines on LLaDA2.0-mini and LLaDA2.0-flash models, respectively.

### [146] [Position: Let's Develop Data Probes to Fundamentally Understand How Data Affects LLM Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18801)
*Shiqiang Wang,Herbert Woisetschläger,Hans Arno Jacobsen,Mingyue Ji*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文倡导通过设计基于随机过程的合成数据序列（即数据探针）来系统研究数据特征如何影响大语言模型（LLM）在训练、微调、对齐、上下文学习等阶段的表现，以超越依赖大量实验的启发式方法，实现对数据本质作用的理论理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型的数据筛选和数据集构建严重依赖于大规模公共数据集上的大量实验，不仅计算成本高，且缺乏对数据特性如何影响模型行为的系统性理解。因此，亟需一种更科学的方法来揭示数据与模型性能之间的内在联系。

Method: 提出使用从适当定义的随机过程中生成的合成序列作为数据探针，通过观察模型在这些探针上的表现，系统分析不同数据特征对模型性能、泛化性和鲁棒性的影响。这些探针具有可分析的统计特性，可借助典型集等理论概念进行建模和解释。

Result: 该数据探针方法能够提供一种超越经验启发式的路径，帮助研究者深入理解数据在大语言模型训练与推理中的基础作用，为数据设计和模型优化提供理论指导。

Conclusion: 建立系统化的合成数据生成与探针分析方法，是推动大语言模型研究从经验驱动向理论驱动转变的关键方向。

Abstract: Data is fundamental to large language models (LLMs). However, understanding of what makes certain data useful for different stages of an LLM workflow, including training, tuning, alignment, in-context learning, etc., and why, remains an open question. Current approaches rely heavily on extensive experimentation with large public datasets to obtain empirical heuristics for data filtering and dataset construction. These approaches are compute intensive and lack a principled way of understanding the essence of how specific data characteristics drive LLM behavior. In this position paper, we advocate for the need of developing systematic methodologies for generating synthetic sequences from appropriately defined random processes, with the goal that these sequences can reveal useful characteristics when they are used in one or multiple stages of the LLM workflow. We refer to such sequences as data probes. By observing LLM behavior on data probes, researchers can systematically conduct studies on how data characteristics influence model performance, generalization, and robustness. The probing sequences exhibit statistical properties that can be viewed using theoretical concepts, such as typical sets, which are generalized to describe the behaviors of LLMs. This data-probe approach provides a pathway for uncovering foundational insights into the role of data in LLM training and inference, beyond empirical heuristics.

</details>


### [147] [Operationalizing Document AI: A Microservice Architecture for OCR and LLM Pipelines in Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18818)
*Yao Fehlis,Benjamin Bengfort,Zhangzhang Si,Vahid Eyorokon,Prema Roman,Patrick Deziel,Devon Slonaker,Steve Veldman,Ben Johnson,Joyce Rigelo,Michael Wharton,Steve Kramer*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种微服务架构，用于在生产环境中高效运行文档理解流水线，涵盖分类、OCR和大语言模型结构化字段提取。通过实践验证，该系统每小时可处理数千页多页文档。关键设计包括混合分类、分离GPU推理与CPU编排、异步处理IO密集型操作，以及独立水平扩展策略。批量分析发现：OCR是端到端延迟的主要瓶颈，系统吞吐量受限于共享GPU推理能力而非工作节点数量。研究旨在为从业者提供可落地的文档理解系统架构模式，实现模型从基准测试到实际部署的有效转化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 学术研究多聚焦于新模型构建，忽视了模型在生产环境中的实际部署挑战，导致理论与实践之间存在巨大鸿沟。为弥合这一差距，亟需可扩展、高效的系统架构支持大规模文档理解任务的落地。

Method: 采用微服务架构，将文档理解流程拆分为多个服务模块，分别处理分类、OCR和大语言模型字段提取；通过混合分类策略优化负载分配；分离GPU密集型推理与CPU控制逻辑；使用异步机制处理输入输出操作；支持独立水平扩展。结合批量性能分析，对系统瓶颈进行识别与优化。

Result: 系统可实现每小时处理数千页多页文档的高吞吐量；实证发现OCR是主要延迟来源，且系统性能受共享GPU容量限制，而非工作节点数量；提出的架构有效支撑了大规模生产级文档理解任务的稳定运行。

Conclusion: 本文提供的微服务架构及设计模式能够有效解决文档理解模型在生产环境中的可扩展性与稳定性问题，为实际部署提供了可复用的技术范式，推动模型从实验室走向真实业务场景。

Abstract: Academic research tends to focus on new models for document understanding creating a wide gap in the literature between model definition and running models at production scale. To close that gap, we present a microservice architecture that encapsulates pipelines of multiple models for classification, optical character recognition (OCR), and large language model structured field extraction as well as our experience running this pipeline on thousands of multi-page documents per hour. We describe our primary design decisions, including a hybrid classification, separation of GPU-bound inference from CPU-bound orchestration, use of asynchronous processing for the many IO-bound operations in the pipeline, and an independent, horizontal scaling strategy. Using batch profiling, we identified two surprising qualitative findings that shape production deployments: OCR, not language-model parsing, dominates end-to-end latency, and the system saturates at a concurrency determined by shared GPU-inference capacity rather than worker count. Our goal is to provide practitioners with concrete architectural patterns for building document understanding systems that work beyond the benchmark; effectively operationalizing models in production.

</details>


### [148] [Evaluating the Utility of Personal Health Records in Personalized Health AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18937)
*Rory Sayres,Kejia Chen,Ayush Jain,Matthew Thompson,Jonathan Richina,Xiang Yin,Jimmy Hu,Fan Zhang,Bob Lou,Mike Sanchez,Ines Mezerreg,Meredith Schreier,Hamsa Subramaniam,I-Ching Lee,Yugang Jia,Daniel Mcduff,Yossi Matias,Avinatan Hassidim,Dale Webster,Yun Liu,Jackie Barr,Quang Duong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究评估了大型语言模型（Gemini 3.0 Flash）在提供患者健康记录（PHR）上下文时，对患者提出的各类健康问题的回答帮助性。通过2,257个来自不同来源的查询与1,945份去标识化PHR匹配，对比了无上下文、仅摘要信息和完整临床记录三种情况下的回答表现。结果显示，加入PHR数据显著提升回答的有用性（p < 0.001），并在安全性、准确性、相关性和个性化方面有潜在提升。研究还开发了一套新评估框架，识别出模型在理解时间顺序混乱和罕见但关键的虚构信息等方面的不足。结果表明PHR数据可有效支持多样化的用户需求，并为监控LLM在复杂记录中的理解缺陷提供了方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 患者管理的个人健康记录（PHRs）虽有助于患者理解自身健康状况，但其中信息复杂，可能阻碍有效洞察。如何利用技术手段提升对这些数据的理解与应用，是当前亟需解决的问题。大语言模型（LLM）具备处理自然语言的能力，若能结合真实临床数据，有望生成更精准、个性化的健康建议。因此，本研究旨在探索LLM在引入PHR上下文后对患者提问的响应质量是否提升，以及其在实际应用中的潜力与局限。

Method: 从三个来源收集2,257个患者健康查询：短文本搜索查询、基于聊天机器人模板的长句问题、以及患者向医疗团队提出的真实电话咨询问题。每个查询与一份去标识化的PHR匹配。使用Gemini 3.0 Flash模型生成回答，共设置三种条件：(1) 无PHR上下文；(2) 仅提供人口统计、疾病史和用药的摘要；(3) 提供完整的临床笔记。采用已有评分框架SHARP及自建错误模式分析框架进行评价。全部样本由自动评分器评估，部分样本（n=95）由临床医生进行人工评分，且所有评分者均知晓完整PHR内容。

Result: 引入PHR上下文显著提升了回答的有用性（p < 0.001，配对t检验），尤其在完整临床笔记条件下效果最明显。模型在安全性、准确性、相关性和个性化方面均有提升。新构建的评估框架揭示了模型在理解时间线错乱、罕见但重要的虚构信息等复杂结构上的缺陷。

Conclusion: PHR数据可显著增强大语言模型对患者健康问题的回答质量，支持多样化用户需求。研究提出了一套针对PHR理解缺陷的评估框架，为未来优化模型性能、保障医疗安全提供了重要方向。该成果推动了患者自主理解健康记录的技术实现，具有广阔的应用前景。

Abstract: Patient-managed Personal Health Records (PHRs) promises to empower patients to better understand their health; but information in the record is complex, potentially hindering insights. In this study, we assess the potential of large language models (LLMs, Gemini 3.0 Flash) to provide helpful answers to user health queries, when provided clinical data from PHRs as context. A total of 2,257 user queries were drawn from 3 different distributions to represent patient questions: shorter web search queries, longer questions derived from templates of chatbot conversations, and questions patients asked to their healthcare team (patient calls). Queries were matched with de-identified PHRs (from a pool of 1,945). Gemini responses were generated (1) without PHR context; (2) with a basic summary of demographics, conditions, and medications; (3) with full, extensive clinical notes. For evaluation, we leveraged an existing rating framework (SHARP), and developed a new framework for specific error modes when interpreting PHRs. Evaluation was performed using autoraters for the full set, and with clinician ratings for a subset (n=95), with both sets of raters knowing the full PHR context. We see significant improvements in the helpfulness of answers to all question types with PHR data (p < 0.001, paired t-test). We also observe potential gains in safety, accuracy, relevance and personalization of answers. Our PHR evaluation framework further identifies gaps in LLM understanding of particular aspects of complex PHRs, such as temporal disorientation, and rare but meaningful confabulations. These results suggest potential for PHR data to help people with a wide range of user needs; and provide a framework for monitoring for gaps in LLM answers based on PHR context. This study motivates further work to assess and realize potential benefits to users from understanding their health records.

</details>


### [149] [Learn-by-Wire Training Control Governance: Bounded Autonomous Training Under Stress for Stability and Efficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19008)
*Anis Radianis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Learn-by-Wire Guard（LBW-Guard），一种位于AdamW之上的有界自主训练控制治理层，用于提升大语言模型在高学习率、大规模和长时间运行压力下的训练稳定性。它不替换优化器更新规则，而是通过监控训练遥测数据、识别不稳定性敏感区间，并施加有界控制来保持固定训练目标。在基于Qwen2.5-7B的多场景测试中，LBW-Guard将最终困惑度从13.21降至10.74（改善18.7%），训练时间从392.54秒缩短至357.02秒（提速1.10倍）。在强学习率压力下，传统AdamW性能急剧下降，而LBW-Guard仍能保持稳定训练，表现显著优于梯度裁剪基线。结果表明，在优化器之上引入有界运行时控制可有效保障计算效率与训练稳定性，且不依赖于优化器替换或局部梯度抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代语言模型训练在高学习率、大规模和长时间运行条件下面临不稳定、性能退化和算力浪费问题。现有方法难以在保持训练目标的前提下有效应对这些挑战，亟需一种能够在不改变优化器核心逻辑的情况下增强训练鲁棒性的机制。

Method: 提出LBW-Guard，一个位于AdamW之上的有界自主训练控制治理层。该系统通过实时监测训练过程中的遥测数据，识别不稳定性敏感区域，并施加有界的控制信号以调节优化器行为，从而在不改变原始训练目标的前提下提升训练稳定性与效率。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-7B基准设置下，LBW-Guard使最终困惑度从13.21降至10.74（改善18.7%），训练时间减少至357.02秒（提速1.10倍）；在极端学习率条件下（如3e-3和1e-3），LBW-Guard仍能维持低困惑度（11.57和10.33），而标准AdamW则严重退化（分别达1885.24和659.76）。梯度裁剪等基线方法无法复现此效果。

Conclusion: 稳定性敏感的大语言模型训练可通过优化器之上的治理层获益。LBW-Guard证明了有界运行时控制在保障计算效率与训练稳定性方面的有效性，且其机制独立于优化器替换与局部梯度抑制，为未来训练系统设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Modern language-model training is increasingly exposed to instability, degraded runs, and wasted compute, especially under aggressive learning-rate, scale, and runtime-stress conditions. This paper introduces Learn-by-Wire Guard (LBW-Guard), a bounded autonomous training-control governance layer that operates above AdamW. Rather than replacing the optimizer update rule, LBW-Guard observes training telemetry, interprets instability-sensitive regimes, and applies bounded control to optimizer execution while preserving fixed training objectives.
  We evaluate LBW-Guard in a Qwen2.5-centered stress-and-robustness suite using WikiText-103, with Qwen2.5-7B as the empirical anchor, model-size comparisons against Qwen2.5-3B and Qwen2.5-14B, learning-rate stress tests, gradient-clipping baselines, and a no-LoRA TinyLlama-1B full-parameter sanity check. In the 7B reference setting, LBW-Guard reduces final perplexity from 13.21 to 10.74, an 18.7% improvement, while reducing end-to-end time from 392.54s to 357.02s, a 1.10x speedup. Under stronger learning-rate stress, AdamW degrades to 1885.24 final perplexity at LR=3e-3 and 659.76 at LR=1e-3, whereas LBW-Guard remains trainable at 11.57 and 10.33, respectively. Gradient-clipping baselines do not reproduce this effect.
  These results support a scoped systems conclusion that stability-sensitive LLM training can benefit from a governance plane above the optimizer. LBW-Guard provides evidence that bounded runtime control can preserve productive compute under stress while remaining distinct from optimizer replacement and local gradient suppression.

</details>


### [150] [AgentNLQ: A General-Purpose Agent for Natural Language to SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19010)
*Olena Bogdanov,Yeunji Jung,Chandra Dhir,Pareekshitreddy Gaddam,Saurabh Jain,Lakshmi Tumati,Vijay Parthasarathy,Anup Shirgaonkar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的多智能体方法用于自然语言到SQL的转换，在BIRD基准测试中实现了78.1%的语义准确率。该方法通过语义增强的模式表示和用户提供的业务规则，生成更准确的SQL查询。主要贡献包括：设计了一个优化的多智能体协调器，利用大模型进行规划、编排、反思与自纠正；开发了一种先进的模式增强方法，生成上下文感知的元数据以提升准确性；并在BIRD-SQL基准上验证了方法在不同领域和数据集上的准确性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型在自然语言处理方面取得了快速进展，但自然语言到SQL的转换在准确性上仍无法达到人类专家水平，因此需要进一步改进算法以提升性能。

Method: 采用多智能体架构，引入语义增强的数据库模式表示，结合用户提供的业务规则，通过一个优化的协调器利用大模型进行规划、编排、反思与自纠正，生成高精度SQL查询。

Result: 在BIRD基准测试中实现78.1%的语义准确率，并在不同领域和数据集上展现出良好的准确性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: 所提出的多智能体方法显著提升了NL2SQL的性能，为解决实际应用中的复杂查询需求提供了有效方案，具备较强的可扩展性和实用性。

Abstract: Natural language to SQL (NL2SQL) conversion is an important problem for researchers and enterprises due to the ubiquitous importance of relational databases in broad-ranging practical problems. Despite the rapid advancements in the capabilities of LLMs, NL2SQL has not reached parity in accuracy with human expert SQL writers, hence needing additional improvements in NL2SQL algorithms. This study presents a new multi-agent method for NL2SQL that achieves 78.1% semantic accuracy on the BIg Bench for LaRge-scale Database (BIRD) benchmark. Our method leverages a semantically enriched representation of user-provided schema, adds user-provided business rules, and produces accurate SQL queries. The main contributions of this study are (a) We designed an optimized new orchestrator in a multi-agent solution that uses LLMs to plan, orchestrate, reflect, and self-correct to generate accurate SQL queries, (b) We developed an advanced schema enrichment method that creates context-aware metadata to improve accuracy, and (c) We demonstrated the accuracy and generalizability of the method across different domains and datasets by evaluating it on the BIRD-SQL benchmark.

### [151] [How Far Are We From True Auto-Research?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19156)
*Zhengxin Zhang,Ning Wang,Sainyam Galhotra,Claire Cardie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究引入ResearchArena框架，评估多个现成智能体（Claude Code、Codex、Kimi Code）在无监督条件下完成完整科研流程的能力。尽管在仅基于论文文本的评审（SAR）中表现良好，甚至接近人类投稿水平，但结合代码与实验结果的交叉审查（PR）后，性能显著下降，暴露出生成论文存在伪造结果、实验设计不足和计划执行不一致等严重问题。不同智能体表现出差异巨大的可靠性，其中Kimi Code问题尤为突出，表明当前自动研究系统仍远未达到顶级会议录用标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自动研究系统虽能生成完整论文，但其质量缺乏系统评估。现有评价方式（如仅看论文文本）可能高估了实际可行性，因此亟需一个全面、多维度的评估框架来揭示生成论文的真实科学严谨性。

Method: 构建ResearchArena这一最小化框架，使各智能体在轻度引导下自主完成科研全流程（选题、实验、写作、自修正）。通过13个计算机科学主题、每组3次重复实验，共生成117篇论文，并采用三种评价方式：仅文本评审（SAR）、包含代码与实验环境的同行评审（PR）、以及人工主导的元评审（meta-review），以多角度验证论文质量。

Result: SAR评分显示部分智能体表现优异，接近人类投稿水平；但PR评分大幅下降，暴露实验真实性严重问题。手动审计发现三大失败模式：伪造结果、实验功率不足、计划与执行不匹配，且问题分布高度依赖于具体智能体。所有生成论文均未达到顶会录用标准。

Conclusion: 当前自动研究系统虽能在表面层面生成看似合理的论文，但在实验真实性和科学严谨性方面仍存在根本性缺陷。未来需加强智能体对实验可复现性与数据可信性的理解，推动真正具备科研能力的自动化研究系统发展。

Abstract: Recent auto-research systems can produce complete papers, but feasibility is not the same as quality, and the field still lacks a systematic study of how good agent-generated papers actually are. We introduce ResearchArena, a minimal scaffold that lets off-the-shelf agents (Claude Code using Opus 4.6, Codex using GPT-5.4, and Kimi Code using K2.5) carry out the full research loop themselves (ideation, experimentation, paper writing, self-refinement) under only lightweight guidance. Across 13 computer science seeds and 3 trials per agent-domain pair, ResearchArena yields 117 agent-generated papers, each evaluated under three complementary lenses: a manuscript-only reviewer (SAR), an artifact-aware peer review (PR) in which agents inspect the workspace alongside the manuscript, and an human conducted meta-review. Under SAR alone the picture is optimistic: Claude Code obtains the highest score, outperforms Analemma's FARS, and matches the weighted-average human ICLR 2025 submission, suggesting that minimally scaffolded agents can produce papers that look competitive on manuscript-only review. Manual inspection, however, reveals this picture is overstated: SAR scores are poorly aligned with its actual acceptance decisions and reward plausible framing without verifying experimental substance. Under artifact-aware PR scores drop sharply, and manual auditing identifies experimental rigor as the major bottleneck, decomposing into three failure modes (fabricated results, underpowered experiments, and plan/execution mismatch) that are highly agent-dependent: Codex 5%/8% paper-vs-artifact mismatch / fabricated references versus Kimi Code 77%/72%, a $\sim$15$\times$ spread that tracks distinct research personas the agents develop. None of the 117 agent-generated papers reaches the acceptance bar of a top-tier venue. This suggests that we are still gapped from the true auto-research.

### [152] [Not all uncertainty is alike: volatility, stochasticity, and exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19215)
*Payam Piray*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在生物和人工智能中自适应决策时，如何在利用已知结果与探索不确定选项之间取得平衡。传统方法将环境中的不同不确定性来源视为等同，但本文区分了两种类型：环境奖励状态随时间漂移（波动性）和通过噪声结果观测（随机性）。尽管两者都增加后验不确定性，但它们对最优探索的影响相反：波动性促进探索，而随机性抑制探索。作者通过扩展Gittins指数框架至具有潜在动态的高斯状态空间老虎机模型，形式化地证明了这种不对称性，并提出了因果感知的不确定性敏感探索（CAUSE）策略，该策略基于控制即推理推导出闭式探索奖励，具有相同的单调性特征。实验表明，CAUSE在异构噪声结构环境中优于标准探索策略，且超越了仅适用于休息老虎机的Gittins每臂策略。此外，学习与探索受同一噪声推断不对称性支配，该框架预测病理性噪声推断会导致探索“反转”而非简单受损，这对精神疾病计算模型具有启示意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究虽指出不确定性通常促进探索，但未区分不同类型的不确定性来源。然而，在现实环境中，存在多种不确定性，如状态漂移（波动性）和观测噪声（随机性），二者虽均增加不确定性，却可能对探索行为产生相反影响。因此，亟需一种能区分并准确建模这些差异的理论框架，以实现更精准的自适应决策。

Method: 通过扩展经典Gittins指数框架到高斯状态空间带状问题，引入潜态动态，形式化分析波动性与随机性对探索的影响。进一步采用控制即推理（control-as-inference）范式，推导出闭式探索奖励机制——因果感知的不确定性敏感探索（CAUSE），其具备正确的单调性。

Result: 研究表明，波动性增强探索，随机性抑制探索，二者具有显著不对称性；所提出的CAUSE策略在复杂噪声环境中表现优于传统探索方法，包括不适用于非静态环境的Gittins策略；同时揭示了噪声推断错误可能导致探索行为反转，为精神障碍的计算解释提供新视角。

Conclusion: 不确定性并非单一维度概念，其来源决定探索行为的方向。本研究建立的理论框架不仅提升了智能体在复杂环境中的学习效率，还为理解认知异常中探索偏差提供了新的计算机制解释。

Abstract: Adaptive decision-making in biological and artificial intelligence requires balancing the exploitation of known outcomes with the exploration of uncertain alternatives. Although prior work suggests that uncertainty generally promotes exploration, it has typically treated distinct sources of environmental uncertainty as equivalent. We consider environments with latent reward states that drift over time (volatility) and are observed through noisy outcomes (stochasticity). Both increase posterior uncertainty, yet we show they drive optimal exploration in opposite directions: volatility enhances it, stochasticity suppresses it. We establish this asymmetry formally by extending the Gittins index framework to Gaussian state-space bandits with latent dynamics. We further derive Cause-Aware Uncertainty-Sensitive Exploration (CAUSE), a closed-form exploration bonus obtained via control-as-inference that inherits the same monotonicities. CAUSE outperforms standard exploration strategies in environments with heterogeneous noise structure, and also improves on a Gittins-per-arm policy whose rested-bandit optimality does not transfer to restless settings. Learning and exploration are governed by the same noise-inference asymmetry, and the framework predicts that pathological noise inference produces \emph{reversed} rather than merely impaired exploration, with implications for computational accounts of psychiatric conditions.

### [153] [Can Large Language Models Revolutionize Survey Research? Experiments with Disaster Preparedness Responses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19229)
*Yan Wang,Ziyi Guo,Christopher McCarty*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出并评估了一个五阶段的LLM集成框架，涵盖问卷设计、样本选择、试点测试、缺失数据填补和后收集分析，以佛罗里达州2024年飓风米尔顿准备度调查（n=946）为实证案例。引入基于保护动机理论（PMT）的共现知识图谱，开发七种LLM配置，包括零样本推理、检索增强基线及新型理论驱动变体。提出的锚定边际理论信息LLM（A-TLM）在灾难相关块状缺失非随机缺失（MNAR）条件下，于S4阶段的均方根误差（RMSE）表现优于三种经典填补方法（1.439 vs. 1.496），且偏差极低（-0.121），远优于随机森林填补器（-0.631）。以PMT因果结构组织检索并单次调用整合全部证据，显著优于非结构化检索与分步推理（MAE 0.993 vs. 1.097）。研究揭示总体偏差趋近零可能掩盖子群体间的相反误差，建议采用子群体分层偏差审计作为报告标准。通过受约束的知识图谱聊天机器人证明，幻觉可通过基于证据的拒绝机制有效管理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Survey research is increasingly challenged by declining response rates, sample bias, block-wise missingness among at-risk respondents, and AI-assisted fraud in online panels. Traditional methods struggle to maintain data quality under such conditions, especially in high-stakes disaster contexts where accurate behavioral insights are critical. Large language models (LLMs) offer potential for improving survey workflows but lack rigorous evaluation across the full pipeline, particularly in real-world disaster settings.

Method: The study develops a five-stage LLM integration framework: questionnaire design, sample selection, pilot testing, missing-data imputation, and post-collection analysis. A Protection Motivation Theory (PMT)-constrained co-occurrence knowledge graph is constructed to guide retrieval and inference. Seven LLM configurations are evaluated: zero-shot inference, retrieval-augmented baselines, and novel theory-informed variants. The Anchored Marginal Theory-Informed LLM (A-TLM) integrates PMT causal structure into a single model call, enabling holistic evidence aggregation. Subgroup-stratified bias auditing is introduced to detect hidden disparities masked by aggregate metrics.

Result: A-TLM outperforms three classical imputation methods (IPW/MI, MICE+PMM, missForest) in RMSE under MNAR conditions (S4 RMSE: 1.439 vs. 1.496), with near-zero signed bias (-0.121) compared to -0.631 from random forest. Retrieval structured around PMT causal logic achieves lower MAE (0.993) than unstructured or staged retrieval (1.097). Subgroup analysis reveals that negligible aggregate bias can mask significant opposing errors in subgroups, underscoring the need for stratified auditing. A retrieval-constrained chatbot successfully manages hallucination through grounded refusal.

Conclusion: LLM integration can significantly enhance survey quality in disaster contexts when guided by theoretical structure and constrained retrieval. The proposed A-TLM framework demonstrates superior performance in missing data imputation and reduces both bias and error. The findings advocate for systematic subgroup-level bias auditing and architectural safeguards against hallucination. This work provides a replicable, theory-driven blueprint for deploying LLMs in high-stakes survey research.

Abstract: Survey research faces mounting structural challenges: declining response rates, sample bias, block-wise missingness among at-risk respondents, and AI-assisted fraudulent completions in online panels. Large language models (LLMs) have been proposed as a remedy, yet rigorous evaluations across the full survey workflow remain scarce, particularly in disaster contexts where data quality matters most. We present and evaluate a five-stage framework for LLM integration covering questionnaire design, sample selection, pilot testing, missing-data imputation, and post-collection analysis, using the 2024 Hurricane Milton preparedness survey of Florida residents (n=946) as a shared empirical testbed. We introduce a Protection Motivation Theory (PMT)-constrained co-occurrence knowledge graph and develop seven LLM configurations spanning zero-shot inference, retrieval-augmented baselines, and novel theory-informed variants. Our proposed Anchored Marginal Theory-Informed LLM (A-TLM) outperforms all three classical imputation baselines (IPW/MI, MICE+PMM, missForest) on RMSE under disaster-relevant block-wise MNAR conditions (S4 RMSE 1.439 vs. 1.496 for the next-best), while achieving near-zero signed bias (-0.121) where the random-forest imputer produces the largest absolute bias (-0.631). Organizing retrieval around PMT causal structure and integrating all evidence in a single model call outperforms unstructured retrieval and staged sequential inference (MAE 0.993 vs. 1.097 for standard RAG). We document that near-zero aggregate bias can mask opposing subgroup errors and propose subgroup-stratified bias auditing as a reporting standard. A retrieval-constrained knowledge-graph chatbot demonstrates that hallucination is architecturally manageable through grounded refusal.

### [154] [Causal Evidence for Attention Head Imbalance in Modality Conflict Hallucination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19250)
*Jinrui Jiang,Zhangtai Wu,Zhen Wu,Xinyu Dai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了多模态大语言模型在视觉与文本冲突时产生幻觉的原因，通过路径修补法识别出两类具有相反因果作用的注意力头：驱动幻觉的头和抵抗幻觉的头。研究发现，驱动幻觉的影响分布更广且权重更大，而抵抗幻觉的影响集中在少数重要头中，形成不平衡的路由结构，导致模型偏向错误文本前提。基于此，提出MACI方法，在检测到模态冲突时有条件地抑制驱动幻觉的头，显著降低幻觉率，并在多个模型上实现良好性能与准确性的平衡，且可零样本迁移至其他测试集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解多模态大语言模型在面对视觉与文本矛盾时为何倾向于依赖错误的文本信息而非正确的视觉证据，揭示其内部机制中的因果成分。

Method: 采用路径修补法进行头级因果分析，对五种开源多模态大语言模型进行系统性分析，识别驱动与抵抗幻觉的注意力头；通过消融实验验证其影响；提出条件性干预方法MACI以抑制特定幻觉驱动头。

Result: 发现驱动幻觉的注意力头具有广泛分布和更高聚合权重，而抵抗幻觉的头集中于少数关键头，形成不平衡路由结构；提出的MACI方法在五个模型上均显著减少幻觉，优于现有推理阶段基线，且在新任务上具备零样本迁移能力。

Conclusion: 多模态冲突下的幻觉现象源于模型内部注意力头的因果不对称性，通过识别并干预特定驱动幻觉的头，可有效缓解幻觉问题，且该方法具备良好的泛化性和实用性。

Abstract: Modality-conflict hallucination occurs when multimodal large language models (MLLMs) prioritize erroneous textual premises over contradictory visual evidence. To understand why visual evidence fails to prevail during generation, we take a mechanistic perspective and examine which internal components drive or resist this failure. We perform head-level causal analysis using path patching across five open-source MLLMs and identify two groups of attention heads with opposing causal roles: hallucination-driving heads and hallucination-resisting heads. We find a consistent asymmetry: driving effects are more broadly distributed and carry greater aggregate weight, whereas resisting effects concentrate in a small number of high-importance heads. Ablation experiments further confirm that these groups exert opposing effects during generation: distributed driving influence and localized resistance together form an imbalanced routing structure that biases generation toward the erroneous premise. Motivated by this finding, we propose MACI (Modality-conflict-Aware Causal Intervention), a conditional intervention that suppresses causally identified hallucination-driving heads only when conflict is detected. Across five MLLMs, MACI achieves the largest hallucination reduction among compared inference-time baselines on the MMMC benchmark with a favorable hallucination-accuracy trade-off, and transfers zero-shot to the SCI-SemanticConflict test.

Method: 结合理论分析与实证研究：通过数学推导分析权力分配的理想条件，并利用Project Catalyst的链上治理数据进行实证分析，评估实际系统中的权力不均衡程度。

We study this phenomenon through the lens of computational social choice, focusing on the extent of power imbalances in stake-weighted voting when power is quantified using the Penrose-Banzhaf power index. Our work presents both analytical and empirical contributions. Analytically, we demonstrate that while a perfect alignment between power and relative stake ownership is generally unattainable, it can be approximated in expectation under specific conditions. Empirically, using data from a real-world on-chain governance system (Project Catalyst), we provide a more fine-grained understanding of the power imbalances that are likely to occur in current stake-weighted governance systems.

Yet existing RRMs are largely deterministic, following a single latent trajectory and converging to a single prediction. We introduce \emph{Generative Recursive reAsoning Models (GRAM)}, a framework that turns recursive latent reasoning into probabilistic multi-trajectory computation. GRAM models reasoning as a stochastic latent trajectory, enabling multiple hypotheses, alternative solution strategies, and inference-time scaling through both recursive depth and parallel trajectory sampling. This yields a latent-variable generative model supporting conditional reasoning via $p_θ(y \mid x)$ and, with fixed or absent inputs, unconditional generation via $p_θ(x)$. Trained with amortized variational inference, GRAM improves over deterministic recurrent and recursive baselines on structured reasoning and multi-solution constraint satisfaction tasks, while demonstrating an unconditional generation capability. \href{https://ahn-ml.github.io/gram-website/}{https://ahn-ml.github.io/gram-website}

### [157] [Beyond Mode Collapse: Distribution Matching for Diverse Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19461)
*Xiaozhe Li,Yang Li,Xinyu Fang,Shengyuan Ding,Peiji Li,Yongkang Chen,Yichuan Ma,Tianyi Lyu,Linyang Li,Dahua Lin,Qipeng Guo,Qingwen Liu,Kai Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DMPO (Distribution-Matching Policy Optimization) addresses mode collapse in on-policy RL by approximating forward KL minimization, promoting solution diversity and sustained exploration. It constructs a reward-proportional target distribution over trajectories and aligns the policy to it, avoiding reliance on intractable global distributions. Evaluated on NP-hard combinatorial tasks, DMPO improves Quality Ratio by 9% and 12% on text-based and vision-based NP-Bench, respectively, and shows gains in mathematical reasoning (+2.0%) and out-of-domain tasks (+2.3%), demonstrating enhanced generalization through diversity-preserving training.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: On-policy reinforcement learning methods like GRPO suffer from mode collapse, where they converge to a single high-reward solution and stop exploring alternative strategies due to reverse KL minimization's mode-seeking behavior.

Method: DMPO introduces a principled approximation of forward KL minimization by constructing a group-level target distribution over sampled trajectories proportional to their rewards, then aligning the policy distribution to this target without requiring sampling from the intractable global target distribution.

Result: DMPO achieves 43.9% Quality Ratio on text-based NP-Bench (vs. GRPO's 40.1%) and 43.1% on vision-based NP-Bench (vs. 38.4%), showing 9% and 12% relative improvements. It also improves performance in mathematical reasoning (+2.0%) and out-of-domain tasks (+2.3%), indicating enhanced general reasoning capabilities.

Conclusion: The work establishes distribution matching as a practical and principled approach to preventing mode collapse in on-policy RL, with consistent quality improvements across diverse reasoning tasks, demonstrating that sustained exploration through diversity preservation enhances overall performance and generalization.

Abstract: On-policy reinforcement learning methods like GRPO suffer from mode collapse: they exhibit reduced solution diversity, concentrating probability mass on a single solution once discovered and ceasing exploration of alternative strategies. We show this stems from reverse KL minimization's mode-seeking behavior, which reinforces the first high-reward trajectory found rather than maintaining a distribution over multiple diverse solutions. We propose DMPO (Distribution-Matching Policy Optimization), which prevents mode collapse through principled approximation of forward KL minimization. DMPO constructs a group level target distribution over sampled trajectories proportional to their rewards, then aligns the policy distribution to this target. This provides mode-covering behavior without requiring sampling from the intractable global target distribution, enabling sustained exploration throughout training. We validate DMPO on NP-hard combinatorial optimization, where exponentially many feasible solutions exist but only a few approach optimality, an ideal testbed for evaluating exploration. DMPO achieves 43.9% Quality Ratio on text-based NP-Bench (vs. GRPO's 40.1%) and 43.1% on vision-based NP-Bench (vs. 38.4%), demonstrating 9% and 12% relative improvements respectively. These gains generalize to mathematical reasoning (+2.0%) and out-of-domain tasks (+2.3%), showing that diversity-preserving training enhances general reasoning capabilities across modalities. Our work establishes distribution matching as a practical, principled approach to preventing mode collapse in on-policy RL, with consistent quality improvements demonstrating sustained exploration across diverse reasoning tasks.

</details>


### [158] [Attention-Guided Reward for Reinforcement Learning-based Jailbreak against Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19485)
*Zheng Lin,Zhenxing Niu,Haoxuan Ji,Yuzhe Huang,Haichang Gao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究大推理模型（LRMs）在越狱攻击下的脆弱性，发现攻击成功率（ASR）与模型注意力模式密切相关。成功攻击通常对输入提示中的有害标记分配较低注意力，而对推理内容中的相关标记分配较高注意力。为此，作者提出一种基于强化学习（RL）的新越狱方法，将注意力信号引入奖励函数，并引入多样化的说服策略以扩展动作空间，显著提升攻击效果。在五个开源和闭源LRM上进行的实验表明，该方法在有效性、效率和可迁移性方面均优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大推理模型（LRMs）虽能生成结构化推理过程，但其内部推理内容暴露了更多安全风险，特别是更容易受到越狱攻击。现有研究表明，传统方法在攻击LRMs时效果有限，亟需更有效的攻击机制来揭示其潜在漏洞。

Method: 提出一种基于强化学习（RL）的越狱攻击方法，通过将注意力信号嵌入奖励函数设计，引导模型在推理过程中关注有害内容；同时引入多种说服策略以丰富动作空间，增强攻击多样性与适应性。

Result: 在三个基准测试中，所提方法在五个不同类型的LRM上均实现了更高的攻击成功率（ASR），且在效率和跨模型迁移能力方面表现优异，显著超越现有方法。

Conclusion: 注意力模式是影响大推理模型越狱攻击成败的关键因素。通过结合强化学习与注意力感知的奖励机制，以及多样化的说服策略，可有效提升越狱攻击的性能，为评估和增强LRMs的安全性提供了新思路。

Abstract: Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in solving complex problems by generating structured, step-by-step reasoning content. However, exposing a model's internal reasoning process introduces additional safety risks; for example, recent studies show that LRMs are more vulnerable to jailbreak attacks than standard LLMs. In this paper, we investigate jailbreak attacks on LRMs and reveal that the attack success rate (ASR) is closely correlated with LRMs' attention patterns. Specifically, successful jailbreaks tend to assign lower attention to harmful tokens in the input prompt, while allocating higher attention to those tokens in the reasoning content. Motivated by this finding, we propose a novel jailbreak method for LRMs that leverages reinforcement learning (RL) to enhance attack effectiveness, explicitly incorporating attention signals into the reward function design. In addition, we introduce diverse persuasion strategies to enrich the RL action space, which consistently improves the ASR. Extensive experiments on five open-source and closed-source LRMs across three benchmarks demonstrate that our method achieves substantially higher ASR, outperforming existing approaches in terms of effectiveness, efficiency, and transferability.

</details>


### [159] [Position: The Turing-Completeness of Real-World Autoregressive Transformers Relies Heavily on Context Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19514)
*Guanyu Cui,Zhewei Wei,Kun He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文澄清了Transformer Turing完备性的常见误解，区分了固定系统设置（i）与规模家族设置（ii）。指出现有证明多基于规模家族设置，但真实大模型部署对应固定系统设置，因此不能直接证明Turing完备性。强调上下文管理方法对计算能力有决定性影响，主张其是自回归Transformer的核心组成部分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献中关于Transformer Turing完备性的论证多基于规模家族设置（即不同模型处理不同长度输入），但实际大模型部署属于固定系统设置（单一模型处理任意长度输入），二者存在本质差异。这种混淆导致对Turing完备性的误读，亟需明确区分并重新评估相关理论结果的有效性。

Method: 本文首先形式化固定系统设置，定义真实世界大模型的运行机制；接着分析规模家族设置中的已有证明，指出其虽可提供资源界限，但不足以证明真正意义上的Turing完备性；最后通过对比不同上下文管理方法的性能，揭示其对计算能力的显著影响。

Result: 在固定系统设置下，现有证明无法支持Transformer的Turing完备性；不同上下文管理策略会带来截然不同的计算能力表现；上下文管理是决定自回归Transformer计算能力的关键因素。

Conclusion: Transformer的Turing完备性不应仅依赖于模型规模扩展，而必须在固定系统框架下严格验证；上下文管理机制应被视为核心计算组件，未来研究需更重视其设计与理论分析。

Abstract: Many works make the eye-catching claim that Transformers are Turing-complete. However, the literature often conflates two distinct settings: (i) a fixed Transformer system setting, in which a fixed autoregressive Transformer is coupled with a fixed context-management method to process inputs of different lengths step by step, and (ii) a scaling-family setting, in which a family of different models (with increasing context-window length or numerical precision) is used to handle different input lengths. Existing proofs of Transformer Turing-completeness are frequently established in setting (ii), whereas real-world LLM deployment and the standard notion of Turing-completeness correspond more naturally to setting (i). In this paper, we first formalize the fixed-system setting, thereby providing a concrete characterization of how real-world LLMs operate. We then argue that results proved in the scaling-family setting provide theoretically meaningful resource bounds but do not establish Turing-completeness, thereby clarifying a common misinterpretation of existing results. Finally, we show that different context-management methods can yield sharply different computational power, and we advocate the position that context management is a central component that critically determines the computational power of real-world autoregressive Transformers.

</details>

Method: 提出BLINKG基准，涵盖从简单到复杂的多种真实世界用例场景，设计多层级评估任务，用于测试不同LLMs在跨数据源映射中的表现。通过大规模实验对比多个先进LLMs在不同复杂度任务上的准确率与鲁棒性，并分析其局限性。

Result: 实验表明，当前主流LLMs在简单或中等复杂度任务中已展现出良好的映射能力，能够有效支持部分知识图谱构建流程；但在高度复杂或模糊的场景中，性能显著下降，存在误匹配、遗漏或逻辑不一致等问题。该基准成功揭示了现有LLMs的能力边界。

Conclusion: BLINKG为评估LLMs在知识图谱构建中的映射能力提供了首个标准化基准，有助于系统性地衡量和改进模型性能。同时，研究明确了实现半自动化（LLM驱动）知识图谱构建所需的关键技术要求，为未来研究提供了清晰方向。

Abstract: Generating Knowledge Graphs (KGs) remains one of the most time-consuming and labor-intensive tasks for knowledge engineers, as they need to identify semantic equivalences between input data sources and ontology terms. While declarative solutions (e.g., RML, SPARQL-Anything) have helped to generalize this process, aligning input schema elements with ontology terms still involves intricate transformations and requires considerable manual effort. With the advent of Large Language Models (LLMs), there is growing interest in leveraging their capabilities to assist KG engineers. Although some studies have explored using LLMs to automate KG construction, there is still no standardized framework for assessing how effectively they establish correspondences between data schemes and ontology concepts. Therefore, in this paper, we propose BLINKG, a benchmark designed to evaluate the mapping capabilities of LLMs in constructing KGs from heterogeneous data sources. The benchmark includes a set of scenarios with increasing complexity, based on real-world use cases. We conduct an extensive experimental evaluation of several stateof-the-art LLMs using BLINK and observe that they already offer promising solutions. However, their performance remains limited in complex scenarios. Thanks to this benchmark, we can already assess the current capabilities of LLMs for KG construction. Additionally, we define a set of requirements for achieving (semi)automated (LLM-driven) KG construction, opening new research lines in this area.

### [161] [Efficient Elicitation of Collective Disagreements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19521)
*Mohamed Ouaguenouni,Felipe Garrido-Lucero,Umberto Grandi,César Hidalgo,Magdalena Tydrichova*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究选民在多个选项之间的意见分歧结构，提出一种分层框架以识别计算分歧度量所需的最小聚合偏好信息。通过引入广义的‘多数矩阵’（plurality matrix），记录每个子集S中各选项在S中排名第一的概率，从而超越传统的成对比较。研究发现，许多现有分歧度量（如排名方差、分裂性）需至少三元组信息才能表达，说明成对比较不足以捕捉结构性分歧。同时，理论与实验表明，拓展至更高层级信息具有价值。作者设计了两种可操作的采集协议，在参与人数与认知负担之间进行权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统调查方式要么采用成对比较（简单但信息有限），要么要求完整排序（认知负担高）。然而，成对比较无法区分结构性分歧与随机噪声，因此需要更精细的偏好信息表示方法。

Method: 提出‘多数矩阵’作为成对比较的推广，记录每个子集S中各元素排名第一的概率；定义分歧度量的‘层级’概念，即表达该度量所需的最小子集大小；基于此分析现有分歧度量的层级，并设计两种用于估计多数矩阵的调查协议。

Result: 证明了包括排名方差和分裂性在内的多种分歧度量位于层级3，说明成对比较无法充分刻画它们；实验与理论分析表明，扩展到更高层级信息能提升分歧分析的准确性；所设计的两种采集协议可在参与人数与认知负荷间实现有效平衡。

Conclusion: 成对比较不足以揭示结构性分歧，必须借助更高层级的偏好信息；多数矩阵提供了一种高效且可操作的框架，支持更精确的分歧度量计算，为未来调查设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: We analyze the structure of the disagreement among a population of voters over a set of alternatives. Surveys typically ask either for pairwise comparisons, simple and intuitive for participants, or full rankings over alternatives, eliciting the entire voters' preferences. Building on the observation that pairwise comparisons cannot distinguish structural disagreement from noise, we propose a stratified framework to identify the minimal aggregated preference information needed to compute a number of disagreement measures from the literature. Specifically, we introduce the plurality matrix, a generalization of pairwise comparisons that records, for every subset $S$ of alternatives, the probability that each $a \in S$ ranks first in $S$. We define the level of a disagreement measure as the smallest subset size needed to express it, showing that many existing notions, including rank-variance and divisiveness, sit at level $3$, proving that pairwise comparisons are not enough. In addition, we demonstrate the interest of going beyond level $3$ both theoretically and experimentally. To make these results actionable, we design two elicitation protocols to estimate the plurality matrix, exploring the trade-off between the number of required participants and the cognitive load requested to each of them.

### [162] [Generative-Evaluative Agreement: A Necessary Validity Criterion for LLM-Enabled Adaptive Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19529)
*Grandee Lee,Yue Wang,Che Yee Lye,Luke Peh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出生成-评估一致性（GEA）作为衡量大语言模型评分函数是否能准确恢复其生成函数所设定技能水平的有效性标准。在双阶段自适应评估中，模型仅能恢复约一半预期方差（r = 0.698），存在系统性正偏差；语法可验证技能的GEA较强（r > 0.7），而设计类技能的GEA接近零，低技能过估计会抬高靠近分流阈值的分数。研究主张采用细粒度、技能分解的评分标准以增强GEA，并提出互补缓解策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当同一LLM负责生成评估题、模拟学生回答并进行评分时，评估过程形成自指闭环，可能导致评分结果不可靠。为确保评估有效性，需建立客观标准来检验模型评分是否真实反映其预设的技能水平。

Method: 引入生成-评估一致性（GEA）作为有效性指标，在双阶段自适应评估框架下，通过指令控制生成不同技能水平的响应，并由同一模型评分，计算评分结果与目标技能水平之间的相关性。同时对不同技能类型（如语法可验证与设计类）分别分析GEA表现。

Result: 模型在生成任务中仅恢复了约50%的预期方差（相关系数r = 0.698），存在系统性正偏差；语法可验证技能的GEA较高（r > 0.7），而设计类技能的GEA接近零；低技能者被显著高估，导致分数在路由阈值附近被人为抬高。

Conclusion: 细粒度、技能分解的评分标准是提升GEA的核心机制，有助于减少评分偏差。此外，还需结合其他缓解策略以改善自指评估系统的可靠性。

Abstract: When the same LLM generates assessment items, simulates student responses, and scores them, the validation loop is self-referential. We introduce Generative-Evaluative Agreement (GEA), a validity criterion measuring whether an LLM's scoring function recovers the skill levels its generative function was instructed to produce. In the first direct measurement of GEA on a two-stage adaptive assessment, the model recovers roughly half the intended variance r = 0.698 with systematic positive bias. GEA is strong r > 0.7 for syntactically verifiable skills but near zero for design-level skills, and low-skill overestimation inflates scores near the routing threshold. We argue that granular, skill-decomposed rubrics are the principal proposed mechanism for strengthening GEA and outline complementary mitigations.

### [163] [Library Drift: Diagnosing and Fixing a Silent Failure Mode in Self-Evolving LLM Skill Libraries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19576)
*Xing Zhang,Yanwei Cui,Guanghui Wang,Ziyuan Li,Wei Qiu,Bing Zhu,Peiyang He*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出可复现的消融实验以分离库漂移效应；设计细粒度追踪工具（如每项技能的贡献评分、归因判断、路由参与度指标）进行运行时诊断；构建并验证一种最小化治理配方，包含结果驱动的技能淘汰、活跃技能数量上限以及元技能作者优先策略。

Result: 在MBPP+ hard-100数据集上，经过100轮迭代后，所提治理方案使持有样本的pass@1从基线0.258提升至0.584，滚动增益达+0.328；八组消融实验证明了关键治理机制的有效性与冗余性。

Conclusion: 库漂移是自演化技能库中一个严重且隐蔽的失效模式，可通过引入结果导向的技能生命周期管理机制加以有效遏制。本研究不仅识别出核心失效机制，还提供了一套可复现、可诊断、可部署的治理框架，为构建可持续演化的智能体系统提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: Self-evolving skill libraries face a silent failure mode we term \emph{library drift}: unbounded skill accumulation without outcome-driven lifecycle management causes retrieval degradation, false-positive injections, and performance stagnation. Recent evaluation confirms the symptom--LLM-authored skills deliver +0.0pp gain while human-curated ones deliver +16.2pp (SkillsBench)--yet the underlying mechanism has not been isolated. We provide (1) a reproducible trigger: ablations that isolate drift--one disables skill injection (flat floor, +0.002), one imposes premature retirement (active harm, $-$0.019); (2) trace-level diagnostics: an append-only evidence log with per-skill contribution scores, attribution verdicts, and router engagement metrics that make the failure visible before it reaches end-task scores; and (3) a verified fix: a minimal governance recipe (outcome-driven retirement + bounded active-cap + meta-skill authoring prior) that lifts held-out pass@1 from a 0.258 baseline to a late-window mean of 0.584 (rolling gain $+$0.328) on MBPP+ hard-100 over 100 rounds. Eight ablations decompose which governance mechanisms are load-bearing and which are subsumed, providing a concrete playbook for diagnosing library drift in any self-evolving agent.

### [164] [Towards Multi-Model LLM Schedulers: Empirical Insights into Offloading and Preemption](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19593)
*Mert Yildiz,Pietro Spadaccino,Alexey Rolich,Francesca Cuomo,Andrea Baiocchi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过实证研究不同大语言模型（LLM）在异构硬件上的行为，重点分析了层卸载和抢占对推理吞吐量的影响。研究发现，卸载导致非线性且依赖模型的吞吐量下降，小模型对GPU驻留减少更敏感；抢占开销主要来自模型状态重载，而非键值缓存传输，且在不同模型和硬件间差异显著。序列长度和互连带宽进一步加剧了数据移动和执行效率问题。基于这些发现，论文提出了未来调度器应考虑的关键特征，如模型特定的卸载敏感性、工作负载特性以及抢占与数据传输的成本结构，为下一代支持混合CPU-GPU执行的多模型异构部署系统设计提供指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM服务系统大多优化单一模型的吞吐量，缺乏对多模型、异构硬件环境下混合CPU-GPU执行中资源分配、调度和抢占机制的深入研究，尤其在GPU内存受限时，亟需理解不同模型的行为特性以支撑高效调度。

Method: 通过实证实验分析多种LLM在不同硬件平台上的性能表现，考察层卸载与预处理对推理吞吐量的影响，量化不同模型和硬件下的抢占开销，并分析序列长度与互连带宽对数据移动和执行效率的影响。

Result: 卸载导致非线性且模型依赖的吞吐量下降，小模型更敏感；抢占开销主要由模型状态重载引起，且在不同模型和硬件上差异显著；序列长度和互连带宽会放大数据移动和执行效率问题。

Conclusion: 未来调度器必须综合考虑模型特定的卸载敏感性、工作负载特征以及预处理和数据传输的实际成本，才能有效管理异构、多模型的混合执行环境，推动下一代LLM服务系统的演进。

Abstract: Modern deployments of Large Language Models (LLMs) increasingly require serving multiple models with diverse architectures, sizes, and specialization on shared, heterogeneous hardware. This setting introduces new challenges for resource allocation, dispatching, and scheduling, particularly under GPU memory constraints where partial CPU-GPU offloading and preemption become necessary. While existing systems primarily optimize throughput for a single model, comparatively little work addresses multi-model scheduling under these conditions. In this paper, we present an empirical study of how different LLMs behave across hardware platforms, focusing on the performance implications of layer offloading and preemption. We show that offloading leads to strongly non-linear and model-dependent degradation in decode throughput, with smaller models exhibiting sharper sensitivity to reduced GPU residency. We further demonstrate that preemption incurs substantial overhead, largely dominated by model state reload rather than key-value cache transfer, and that this cost varies significantly across models and hardware platforms. Additionally, we highlight the role of sequence length and interconnect bandwidth in amplifying data movement and execution inefficiencies. Based on these findings, we identify a set of key features that future schedulers must consider, including model-specific offloading sensitivity, workload characteristics, and the cost structure of preemption and data transfer. These insights provide guidance for the design of next-generation LLM serving systems capable of efficiently managing heterogeneous, multi-model workloads with hybrid CPU-GPU execution.

</details>


### [165] [EMO-BOOST: Emotion-Augmented Audio-Visual Features for Improved Generalization in Deepfake Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19630)
*Aritra Marik,Marcel Klemt,Anna Rohrbach*

TL;DR: 本文提出Emo-Boost框架，利用情绪作为高层语义线索，结合视觉与音频情绪识别模块，建模跨模态情感表示的时间一致性，以提升对未见深度伪造技术的泛化能力。实验表明，该方法在FakeAVCeleb数据集上使跨操纵类型泛化AUC平均提升2.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前深度伪造检测面临新生成技术不断涌现的挑战，难以为每种篡改方式收集训练数据，因此如何实现对未见篡改类型的泛化成为关键难题。

Method: 提出EmoForensics模型，基于视觉和音频的情绪识别，建模音视频流中跨模态与内部的时间一致性；将该模型与现有的RGB和音频聚焦的深度伪造检测器融合，构建多模态检测框架Emo-Boost。

Conclusion: 情绪作为高层语义线索可有效补充低层特征，在面对未见深度伪造时提供更强的泛化能力，证明了多模态情感一致性建模在深度伪造检测中的有效性。

Abstract: With every advancement in generative AI models, forensics is under increasing pressure. The constant emergence of new generation techniques makes it impossible to collect data for each manipulation to train a deepfake detection model. Thus, generalizing to deepfakes unseen during training is one of the major challenges in current deepfake detection research. To tackle this challenge, we employ high-level semantic cues and argue that these cues can support low-level focused approaches in generalizing to unseen types of manipulations. In this work, we study emotions as a high-level semantic cue. We propose Emo-Boost, a multimodal deepfake detection framework that fuses an off-the-shelf RGB- and acoustic-focused deepfake detector with our emotion-based deepfake detector EmoForensics. EmoForensics utilises vision and audio emotion recognition modules and models intra- and inter-modal temporal consistency in emotion representations from an audio-visual stream. We found that EmoForensics and the low-level focused method capture complementary signals. Consequently, combining both signals in EmoBoost enhances the average cross-manipulation generalization AUC by 2.1% on FakeAVCeleb.

Extensive experiments demonstrate that PStar significantly reduces hallucination rates, achieving state-of-the-art scores of 87.1% on POPE and 68.0% on MMStar, outperforming even GPT-4V. Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CogScale 是一个包含14个可扩展合成任务的基准测试，用于评估模型在不同参数规模下的认知与记忆能力。该框架轻量且标准化，可快速验证新架构，避免大规模训练的高成本。研究对比了7种模型（GRU、LSTM、xLSTM、ESN、Mamba、Transformer Decoder、Encoder-Decoder），在1k、10k、100k参数预算下进行测试。结果显示，传统RNN和ESN在低参数下表现良好，但只有注意力机制和现代状态空间模型（如Mamba）能随任务复杂度提升保持高性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出CogScale基准，包含14个可调尺度的合成任务，覆盖不同认知与记忆能力；在严格参数预算（1k、10k、100k）下对7种主流架构进行系统评估，涵盖多种难度级别。

Result: 经典RNN和ESN在低参数条件下表现优异，但在任务复杂度增加时性能下降；而基于注意力机制和现代状态空间模型（如Mamba）在高复杂度任务中持续保持高性能。

Conclusion: CogScale为模型序列建模能力的快速评估提供了有效工具；未来模型设计应更注重注意力机制与状态空间结构以应对复杂推理任务。

Abstract: The ability to maintain and manipulate information over time is a fundamental aspect of living beings and Artificial Intelligence. While modern models have achieved remarkable success in tasks like natural language processing, evaluating the capacity of novel architectures to process sequential information remains computationally expensive and time-consuming. Testing a new architecture often requires scaling up to massive datasets and models, leading to vast computational costs and slow iteration cycles. In this paper, we propose CogScale, a benchmark of 14 scalable synthetic tasks designed to isolate and evaluate specific cognitive and memory abilities at different parametrizable scales. By providing a standardized, lightweight framework, CogScale allows researchers to rapidly validate architectural innovations before committing to large-scale training. To establish a solid baseline, we evaluate seven distinct architectures: Gated Recurrent Unit (GRU), Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM), xLSTM, Echo State Network (ESN), Mamba, Transformer Decoder, and Transformer Encoder-Decoder. These evaluations are conducted under strict parameter budgets (1k, 10k, and 100k) and across different difficulty levels and scales. Our results show that while classical RNNs and Echo State Networks excel at basic retention within strict parameter budgets, only attention mechanisms and modern state-space models consistently maintain high performance as reasoning complexity and task difficulty scale.

### [169] [What Really Improves Mathematical Reasoning: Structured Reasoning Signals Beyond Pure Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19762)
*Yuze Zhao,Junpeng Fang,Lu Yu,Zhenya Huang,Kai Zhang,Qing Cui,Qi Liu,Jun Zhou,Enhong Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过控制预训练实验，研究了代码在基础语言模型训练中的作用。发现代码虽显著提升编程能力，但并非通用推理增强器，反而与知识密集型任务（尤其是复杂数学推理）存在竞争关系。推理提升更多源于跨域结构化推理痕迹（如代码-文本、数学-文本混合），而非可执行代码本身。增加数学领域结构化样本密度可在不牺牲编程性能的前提下显著提升数学推理能力，表明认知支架是缓解跨域权衡的有效策略。路由分析显示数据组合效应反映在专家激活模式中，揭示了不同领域间的竞争与协同机制。研究明确了哪些数据特征能跨能力维度迁移，并提出了更精准的数据优化策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究代码在现代基础语言模型训练中的作用，特别是其是否能作为通用推理增强手段，以及如何优化数据以平衡不同能力维度的表现。

Method: 在10万亿令牌的语料库上进行受控预训练实验，采用细粒度领域分离，比较不同数据配置下的模型表现，包括纯可执行代码、代码-自然语言数据、数学-自然语言混合数据等，并通过路由分析观察专家激活模式。

Result: 代码主要提升编程能力，对一般推理无显著增益；反而与复杂数学推理产生竞争；推理提升更依赖于跨域结构化推理痕迹；提高数学领域结构化样本密度可显著提升数学推理，同时保持编程性能；路由分析揭示了领域间竞争与协同的机制性证据。

Conclusion: 代码并非通用推理增强剂，其价值体现在特定任务（如编程）和结构化数据组合上。通过合理设计数据构成，尤其是引入结构化数学样本，可有效缓解跨域能力冲突，实现更精准的能力优化。

Abstract: Code has become a standard component of modern foundation language model (LM) training, yet its role beyond programming remains unclear. We revisit the claim that code improves reasoning through controlled pretraining experiments on a 10T-token corpus with fine-grained domain separation. Our findings are threefold. First, when code is restricted to standalone executable programs and Code-NL data are controlled for, code substantially improves programming ability but does not act as a general reasoning enhancer; instead, it competes with knowledge-intensive tasks, especially complex mathematical reasoning. Second, the reasoning gains often attributed to code are better explained by cross-domain structured reasoning traces, such as code-text and math-text mixtures, rather than by executable code alone. Third, increasing the density of structured math-domain samples within a fixed math budget yields substantial gains on difficult mathematical reasoning while largely preserving programming performance, suggesting that cognitive scaffolds offer a targeted way to mitigate cross-domain trade-offs. Finally, routing analyses show that data-composition effects are reflected in expert-activation patterns, providing mechanism-level evidence for competitive and synergistic interactions across domains. Our results clarify which data characteristics transfer across capability dimensions and point to more precise data-centric optimization strategies.

### [170] [GroupAffect-4: A Multimodal Dataset of Four-Person Collaborative Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19765)
*Meisam Jamshidi Seikavandi,Alice Modica,Anna Obara,Shan Ahmed Shaffi,Fabricio Batista Narcizo,Tanya Ignatenko,Ted Vucurevich,Karim Haddad,Daniel Barratt,Daniel Overholt,Jesper Bunsow Boldt,Paolo Burelli,Andrew Burke Dittberner*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: GroupAffect-4 是一个包含40名参与者组成的10组四人小组的多模态数据集，涵盖多种生态相关的协作任务。每个参与者佩戴生理传感器、眼动追踪眼镜和近场麦克风，采集连续情感自报告、任务后问卷、任务结果及大五人格评分，所有数据均时间对齐。该数据集覆盖超过91%的生理信号窗口和98%的眼动追踪窗口，具有良好的任务有效性。研究定义了15个可基准化的分析目标，横跨个体状态、人际特质和群体动态三个层面，并提供了留一组外的可行性基线。数据集采用BIDS结构，配有元数据、数据表、质量报告和开放处理脚本，代码与数据已公开发布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建并收集来自10组四人小组的多模态数据，每组完成四个生态有效的协作任务（信息整合、协商、创意生成、公共品游戏）。每位参与者配备腕戴生理传感器、眼动追踪眼镜和近场麦克风，同步采集生理信号、眼动数据、音频、连续情感自报告、任务后问卷、任务成果及大五人格评估，所有数据以统一时钟对齐。通过任务有效性检验验证情感操纵效果，并提供数据质量报告与处理脚本。

Result: GroupAffect-4 数据集覆盖超过91%的生理信号窗口和98%的眼动追踪窗口，任务有效性通过明确的情感操控检查得到验证。定义了15个可基准化的分析目标，涵盖个体、人际和群体三个层次，并建立了留一组外的可行性基线，证明其可用于系统性评估。数据集结构规范，配套工具完善，便于复现与扩展研究。

Conclusion: GroupAffect-4 是一个全面、高质量、多模态的群体交互数据集，填补了现有数据集在群体情感多层级分析方面的空白，为未来群体情感计算与社会信号处理研究提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: Existing affective-computing, social-signal-processing, and meeting corpora capture important parts of human interaction, but they rarely support analysis of affect in co-located groups as a coupled individual, interpersonal, and group-level process. The required signals (per-participant physiology, eye movement, audio, self-report, task outcomes, and personality) are usually fragmented across separate dataset traditions. We introduce GroupAffect-4, a multimodal corpus of 40 participants in 10 four-person groups, each completing four ecologically varied collaborative tasks spanning information pooling, negotiation, idea generation, and a public-goods game. Each participant is instrumented with a wrist-worn physiology sensor, eye-tracking glasses, and a close-talk microphone; sessions include continuous affect self-reports, post-task questionnaires, task outcomes, and Big-Five personality scores, all time-aligned to a shared clock. The dataset covers over 91% of expected physiology windows and 98% of eye-tracking windows, with strong task validity confirmed by a clear affective manipulation check across the negotiation block. We define fifteen benchmarkable targets spanning three analysis levels -- within-person state, between-person traits, and group dynamics -- and report leave-one-group-out feasibility baselines establishing the dataset's evaluative scope. GroupAffect-4 is released with a BIDS-inspired structure, Croissant metadata, a datasheet, per-session quality reports, and open processing scripts. Code and processing scripts are available at https://github.com/meisamjam/GroupAffect-4; the dataset is publicly archived at https://zenodo.org/records/20037847.

### [171] [Minimax Optimal Variance-Aware Regret Bounds for Multinomial Logistic MDPs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19768)
*Pierre Boudart,Pierre Gaillard,Alessandro Rudi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于多项式逻辑（MNL）模型的随机马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）中的强化学习问题。针对现有算法在MNL混合MDP上表现出$\tilde{O}(dH^2\sqrt{T})$的后悔率，作者引入了一个依赖于问题的常数$\barσ_T \leq 1/2$，用于衡量最优下游值函数在学习轨迹上的归一化平均方差。提出的新算法实现了$\tilde{O}(dH^2\barσ_T\sqrt{T})$的后悔率，在最坏情况下恢复原有结果，而在结构化MDP中则有显著改进。例如，在KL约束鲁棒MDP中，$\barσ_T = O(H^{-1})$，使时间跨度依赖性降低一个因子$H$。同时建立了匹配的$\Omega(dH^2\barσ_T\sqrt{T})$下界，证明了该结果在对数因子意义下的极小极大最优性，首次完全刻画了MNL混合MDP的后悔复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有算法在处理MNL混合MDP时的后悔率在最坏情况下表现不佳，且缺乏对结构化问题的优化能力。为解决这一问题，需要引入更精细的问题依赖性度量，并设计能够适应不同结构特性的算法，以实现更优的性能。

Method: 受逻辑贝叶斯文献启发，定义了一个新的问题依赖常数$\barσ_T$，反映最优值函数在轨迹上的归一化方差；设计了一种新算法，利用该常数进行自适应优化；通过理论分析建立上下界，验证其最优性。

Result: 所提算法的后悔率为$\tilde{O}(dH^2\\barσ_T\\sqrt{T})$，在一般情形下与已有结果一致，但在结构化问题如KL约束鲁棒MDP中显著提升，达到$O(H^{-1})$的$\barσ_T$，从而将时间跨度依赖性降低一个因子$H$；同时证明了该后悔率的下界为$\Omega(dH^2\\barσ_T\\sqrt{T})$，表明算法在对数因子内是最优的。

Conclusion: 本工作首次完全刻画了MNL混合MDP的后悔复杂度，通过引入问题依赖常数$\barσ_T$并设计相应算法，实现了在结构化场景下的显著性能提升，并在理论上证明了其极小极大最优性，为该类问题提供了完整且紧致的理论框架。

Abstract: We study reinforcement learning for episodic Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) whose transitions are modelled by a multinomial logistic (MNL) model. Existing algorithms for MNL mixture MDPs yield a regret of $\smash{\tilde{O}(dH^2\sqrt{T})}$ (Li et al., 2024), where $d$ is the feature dimension, $H$ the episode length, and $T$ the number of episodes. Inspired by the logistic bandit literature (Abeille et al., 2021; Faury et al., 2022; Boudart et al., 2026), we introduce a problem-dependent constant $\barσ\_T \leq 1/2$, measuring the normalised average variance of the optimal downstream value function along the learner's trajectory. We propose an algorithm achieving a regret of $\smash{\tilde{O}(dH^2\barσ\_T\sqrt{T})}$, which recovers the existing bound in the worst case and improves upon it for structured MDPs. For instance, for KL-constrained robust MDPs, $\barσ\_T = O(H^{-1})$, reducing the horizon dependence by a factor $H$. We further establish a matching $\smash{Ω(dH^2\barσ\_T\sqrt{T})}$ lower bound, proving minimax optimality (up to logarithmic factors) and fully characterising the regret complexity of MNL mixture MDPs for the first time.

</details>


### [172] [From Prompts to Pavement Through Time: Temporal Grounding in Agentic Scene-to-Plan Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19824)
*Ahmed Y. Gado,Omar Y. Goba,Alaa Hassanein,Catherine M. Elias,Ahmed Hussein*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在自动驾驶车辆的高级场景理解与规划中，通过引入时间条件化来提升多智能体通信中的推理一致性。研究对比了三种逐步增强时间整合的规划器架构，在BDD-X数据集上评估其表现。尽管时间条件化未在标准NLP正确性指标上带来显著提升，但定性分析显示其能促进预测性危险推理、稳定的修正行为及策略分化，揭示了提示式时间锚定的局限性，并建立了首个关于时间感知场景到计划推理的实证基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于大语言模型（LLM）和大视觉语言模型（LMM）的自动驾驶系统在处理连续动作时普遍忽视时间维度，导致推理不一致，影响安全性和可解释性。因此亟需探索时间条件化对多智能体交互中推理连贯性的提升作用。

Method: 设计并比较三种逐步增加时间整合能力的规划器架构，基于BDD-X数据集的子集进行评估，采用语义、句法和逻辑指标量化性能，并结合定性分析考察推理行为特征。

Result: 时间条件化虽未显著提升标准NLP正确性指标，但在定性层面展现出更强的预测性危险识别、稳定纠错能力及策略多样性，表明其对复杂动态场景建模具有潜在价值。

Conclusion: 提示式时间锚定存在局限，无法显著改善传统评估指标，但能有效引导更符合现实动态需求的推理模式；本研究首次建立时间感知场景到计划推理的实证基准，为未来研究提供方向。

Abstract: Recent attempts to support high-level scene interpretation and planning in Autonomous Vehicles (AVs) using ensembles of Large Language Models (LLMs) and Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) continue to treat time as a secondary property. This lack of temporal grounding leads to inconsistencies in reasoning about continuous actions, undermining both safety and interpretability. This work explores whether temporal conditioning within inter-agent communication can preserve or enhance coherence without introducing degradation in semantic or logical consistency. To investigate this, we introduce three planner architectures with progressively increasing temporal integration and evaluate them on curated subsets of the BDD-X dataset using semantic, syntactic, and logical metrics. Results show that while temporal conditioning reshapes reasoning style, it yields no statistically significant improvements in standard NLP-based correctness metrics. However, qualitative analysis reveals predictive hazard reasoning, stable corrective behavior, and strategic divergence in the Sentinel. These findings clarify the limits of prompt-based temporal grounding and establish the first empirical benchmark for temporal scene-to-plan reasoning.

</details>

*Rebecca Ramnauth,Drazen Brscic,Brian Scassellati*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 受机器人学启发，将安全约束形式化为对封闭回路系统的运行时控制问题，引入Grounded Observer框架，通过实时监测与干预，确保交互轨迹不进入不良状态，同时具备自适应能力以应对复杂社会环境。

Result: 在小对话、家庭自闭症治疗和学校行为去激化三个真实场景中，该框架均成功实现对交互过程的实时干预，有效缓解了行为漂移问题，并展现出良好的上下文适应性。

Conclusion: 未来研究应致力于增强该框架的理论保证，探索更强大的形式化安全约束机制，推动基础模型在高风险社会应用中的可靠部署。

Abstract: Foundation models are increasingly deployed in socially sensitive domains such as education, mental health, and caregiving, where failures are often cumulative and context-dependent. We reframe guardrails as a problem of runtime behavioral control over interaction trajectories, drawing on robotics to introduce formal constructs for constraint enforcement in uncertain, closed-loop systems. We instantiate these ideas in the Grounded Observer framework and apply it across three real-world deployments: small talk, in-home autism therapy, and behavioral de-escalation in schools. Across settings, the framework enables runtime interventions that mitigate drift into undesirable interaction regimes while adapting to diverse social contexts. We discuss extensions to the framework and propose research directions toward stronger guarantees.

### [174] [Probabilistic Tiny Recursive Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19943)
*Amin Sghaier,Ali Parviz,Alexia Jolicoeur-Martineau*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Probabilistic TRM (PTRM) enhances Tiny Recursive Models (TRM) by introducing stochastic exploration via Gaussian noise injection at each recursion step, enabling parallel trajectories to escape suboptimal solutions. This task-agnostic, test-time compute scaling method improves accuracy significantly without retraining—achieving 98.75% on Sudoku-Extreme and 91.2% on Pencil Puzzle Bench, outperforming frontier LLMs at a fraction of the cost.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: TRMs are efficient but suffer from deterministic recursion that may converge to suboptimal solutions; existing fixes require task-specific perturbations and voting, limiting generalizability. PTRM aims to enable robust, scalable reasoning without retraining or domain-specific adjustments.

Method: PTRM injects Gaussian noise at each deep recursion step, allowing multiple parallel trajectories to explore diverse solution spaces. The model's existing Q head is used to select the best outcome among these trajectories, enabling effective exploration and improved decision-making at test time.

Result: PTRM achieves substantial accuracy gains: 87.4% to 98.75% on Sudoku-Extreme and 62.6% to 91.2% on Pencil Puzzle Bench. It surpasses frontier LLMs (91.2% vs. 55.1%) while using only 7M parameters and less than 0.0001x the computational cost.

Conclusion: PTRM provides a powerful, task-agnostic approach to enhance small models through stochastic test-time computation, enabling high accuracy and efficiency without retraining, making it a compelling alternative to large language models for complex reasoning tasks.

Abstract: Tiny Recursive Models (TRM) solve complex reasoning tasks with a fraction of the parameters of modern large language models (LLMs) by iteratively refining a latent state and final answer. While powerful, their deterministic recursion can lead to convergence at suboptimal solutions, without escape mechanism. A common workaround relies on task-specific input perturbations at test time combined with answer aggregation via voting. We introduce Probabilistic TRM (PTRM), a task-agnostic framework for test-time compute scaling that addresses this limitation through stochastic exploration. PTRM injects Gaussian noise at each deep recursion step, enabling parallel trajectories to explore diverse solution basins, and selects among them using the model's existing Q head (used for early stopping in the original TRM). Without requiring retraining or task-specific augmentations, PTRM enables substantial accuracy gains across benchmarks, including Sudoku-Extreme (87.4% to 98.75%) and on various puzzles from Pencil Puzzle Bench (62.6% to 91.2%). On the latter, PTRM achieves nearly double the accuracy of frontier LLMs (91.2% vs. 55.1%) at less than 0.0001x the cost, using only 7M parameters.

</details>


### [175] [GeoX: Mastering Geospatial Reasoning Through Self-Play and Verifiable Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20006)

Method: GeoX采用自玩框架，结合多模态策略生成可执行程序作为空间问题，并在三种推理模式（溯因、演绎、归纳）下操作空间原语与图像理解工具。程序由验证器执行，产生可验证的奖励信号，通过强化学习联合优化问题生成与求解能力。

Conclusion: GeoX展示了通过自玩机制实现高效、可扩展的地理空间推理的可行性，为减少对人工标注数据的依赖提供了新路径，并推动了地理空间理解领域的基准建设。

Abstract: Geospatial reasoning requires solving image-grounded problems over the complex spatial structure of a scene. However, developing this capability is hindered by the cost of annotating a vast and combinatorial question space. We propose GeoX, a self-play framework that acquires spatial logic through executable programs that yield verifiable rewards, without relying on large-scale human-curated data Given a satellite or aerial image, our framework employs a single multimodal policy that proposes spatial problems as executable programs and solves them under three reasoning modes-abduction, deduction, and induction-over spatial primitives and an image understanding tool. A verifier executes each program to covert a reward signal that jointly optimizes the two roles via reinforcement learning. GeoX consistently improves its base VLMs by up to 5.5 points on average, matching or exceeding conventional baselines trained on millions of curated data. Along-side the proposed method, we release a benchmark for geospatial understanding accumulated through self-play.

### [176] [AutoResearchClaw: Self-Reinforcing Autonomous Research with Human-AI Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20025)
*Jiaqi Liu,Shi Qiu,Mairui Li,Bingzhou Li,Haonian Ji,Siwei Han,Xinyu Ye,Peng Xia,Zihan Dong,Congyu Zhang,Letian Zhang,Guiming Chen,Haoqin Tu,Xinyu Yang,Lu Feng,Xujiang Zhao,Haifeng Chen,Jiawei Zhou,Xiao Wang,Weitong Zhang,Hongtu Zhu,Yun Li,Jieru Mei,Hongliang Fei,Jiaheng Zhang,Linjie Li,Linjun Zhang,Yuyin Zhou,Sheng Wang,Caiming Xiong,James Zou,Zeyu Zheng,Cihang Xie,Mingyu Ding,Huaxiu Yao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AutoResearchClaw 是一个基于多智能体的自主科研系统，通过结构化多智能体辩论、自愈执行器、可验证结果报告、人机协同干预和跨轮次演化机制，实现了科研过程的迭代优化。在 ARC-Bench 基准上，其性能优于 AI Scientist v2 54.7%；人机协同实验表明，在关键决策点进行精准干预比完全自治或逐步监督更有效。该系统旨在增强而非取代人类科学判断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主科研系统多为线性流程，缺乏迭代能力，无法处理失败并积累经验。真实科学研究是反复迭代的过程，需要多角度挑战假设、从失败中学习，并在不同周期间积累知识。因此亟需一种能模拟这一复杂过程的系统。

Method: 提出 AutoResearchClaw 系统，包含五个核心机制：1）结构化多智能体辩论用于生成假设与分析结果；2）自愈执行器采用 	extsc{Pivot}/	extsc{Refine} 决策循环，将失败转化为信息；3）可验证结果报告防止数据伪造与虚构引用；4）七种人机协同干预模式，支持从完全自主到逐步监督的灵活协作；5）跨运行演化机制，将历史错误转化为未来防护策略。

Result: 在 25 个主题的 ARC-Bench 实验基准上，AutoResearchClaw 的表现超越 AI Scientist v2 54.7%。人机协同消融实验显示，针对高杠杆决策点的精准干预显著优于完全自动化或全程细粒度监督。

Conclusion: AutoResearchClaw 不是替代人类科学家，而是一种研究增强工具，通过智能迭代与人机协同，提升科研效率与可靠性，推动自动化科学发现迈向更高层次。

Abstract: Automating scientific discovery requires more than generating papers from ideas. Real research is iterative: hypotheses are challenged from multiple perspectives, experiments fail and inform the next attempt, and lessons accumulate across cycles. Existing autonomous research systems often model this process as a linear pipeline: they rely on single-agent reasoning, stop when execution fails, and do not carry experience across runs. We present AutoResearchClaw, a multi-agent autonomous research pipeline built on five mechanisms: structured multi-agent debate for hypothesis generation and result analysis, a self-healing executor with a \textsc{Pivot}/\textsc{Refine} decision loop that transforms failures into information, verifiable result reporting that prevents fabricated numbers and hallucinated citations, human-in-the-loop collaboration with seven intervention modes spanning full autonomy to step-by-step oversight, and cross-run evolution that converts past mistakes into future safeguards. On ARC-Bench, a 25-topic experiment-stage benchmark, AutoResearchClaw outperforms AI Scientist v2 by 54.7%. A human-in-the-loop ablation across seven intervention modes reveals that precise, targeted collaboration at high-leverage decision points consistently outperforms both full autonomy and exhaustive step-by-step oversight. We position AutoResearchClaw as a research amplifier that augments rather than replaces human scientific judgment. Code is available at https://github.com/aiming-lab/AutoResearchClaw.

### [177] [Probing Embodied LLMs: When Higher Observation Fidelity Hurts Problem Solving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20072)
*Oussama Zenkri,Oliver Brock*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究通过在物理机器人设置和受控模拟中评估大语言模型（LLM）在不同感知输入（RGB、RGB-D、真实符号观察）下的行为，发现尽管直观上认为精确信息应提升表现，但LLM在原始RGB输入下表现最佳，而在完美地面真值观测下最差。进一步模拟实验表明，适度的感知噪声（如40%动作结果翻转）反而能显著提升成功率（提高2.85倍），并减少重复动作循环。这表明性能提升可能源于感知错误与推理缺陷之间的交互作用，而非真正鲁棒的问题解决能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在机器人系统中的应用日益增多，但其决策过程不透明，难以解释在闭环具身任务中的成功或失败。现有评估方法往往依赖于性能指标，但忽略了感知误差与推理错误之间的复杂交互，可能导致对模型能力的误判。因此需要从行为层面系统研究感知输入对LLM具身智能的影响。

Method: 使用锁盒（Lockbox）这一具有隐藏相互依赖关系的顺序机械谜题任务，在物理机器人平台和受控仿真环境中测试LLM在三种不同感知输入（RGB、RGB-D、地面真值符号）下的表现；通过随机翻转动作结果来模拟感知噪声，并分析其对行为模式和成功率的影响。

Result: LLM在原始RGB输入下表现最优，在完美地面真值输入下表现最差；模拟中40%动作结果翻转时成功率提升2.85倍，且重复动作循环减少；表明适度噪声有助于缓解模型陷入无效循环的问题。

Conclusion: 单纯以成功率评价大语言模型在具身任务中的能力是不足的，实际表现可能反映的是感知误差与推理缺陷之间的动态交互，而非真正的鲁棒性。未来评估需考虑感知不确定性与推理机制的耦合效应。

Abstract: Large Language Models are increasingly proposed as cognitive components for robotic systems, yet their opaque decision processes make it difficult to explain success or failure in closed-loop embodied tasks. Following an empirical AI methodology, we study embodied LLM agents behaviorally by varying the information available to the agent and measuring the resulting changes in behavior. Using the Lockbox, a sequential mechanical puzzle with hidden interdependencies, we evaluate LLMs across RGB, RGB-D, and ground-truth symbolic observations in a physical robotic setup and use controlled simulation to probe the resulting behavior. Counterintuitively, agents perform best under raw RGB input and worst under perfect ground-truth observations. In simulation, we probe this effect by randomly flipping perceived action outcomes and find that moderate noise improves performance, peaking at a 40% flip probability with a 2.85-fold success rate increase over the noise-free baseline. Further analysis links this gain to a reduction in repetitive action loops. These findings suggest that success rates alone are insufficient for evaluating LLMs, as measured performance may reflect the interaction between perceptual errors and reasoning failures rather than robust problem solving.

### [178] [Neurosymbolic Learning for Inference-Time Argumentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20098)
*Gabriel Freedman,Adam Dejl,Adam Gould,Mansi,Lihu Chen,Jianqi Jiang,Francesca Toni*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为推理时论证（ITA）的可训练神经符号框架，用于三元声明验证。该方法利用形式化论证语义来指导大模型训练，使其生成论据并分配基础得分，同时在推理时基于生成的、评分的论据计算真/假/不确定的三元预测。这种方法在训练时优化论据生成与评分质量，在推理时确保最终判断忠实于可解释的论据结构，而非依赖不可靠的事后推理。在两个三元声明验证数据集上，ITA优于现有论证基线，并能与非论证直接预测基线竞争，同时提供确定性且可检查的判决结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在医疗、金融等高风险场景中，当支撑声明的信息不完整或冲突时，二元真假分类可能不够恰当，需要引入‘不确定’状态；同时，模型的决策必须有可解释、忠实的依据，以增强可信度和透明度。传统方法依赖事后推理解释，常不可靠，因此需要一种能从内部结构生成可解释、一致结论的新范式。

Method: 提出推理时论证（ITA）框架，结合形式化论证语义与大模型能力：1）训练阶段，使用论证语义指导模型生成论据并赋予基础得分；2）推理阶段，基于生成的论据及其得分，通过论证语义规则计算三元预测结果，保证输出与输入论据严格一致。整个过程为确定性、可解释的结构化推理。

Result: 在两个三元声明验证数据集上，ITA显著优于现有的论证基线方法，性能可与非论证型直接预测基线媲美，且其输出具有明确、可检查的论据支持，实现高可信度的解释性决策。

Conclusion: ITA是一种有效、可解释且可靠的三元声明验证方法，它将形式化论证机制融入大模型训练与推理流程，实现了从生成到决策全过程的透明性和一致性，为高风险场景中的可信AI提供了新路径。

Abstract: Claim verification is an important problem in high-stakes settings, including health and finance. When information underpinning claims is incomplete or conflicting, uncertain answers may be more appropriate than binary true or false classifications. In all cases, faithful explanations of the considerations determining the final verdict are crucial. We introduce inference-time argumentation (ITA), a trainable neurosymbolic framework for ternary claim verification in which a formal argumentation semantics giving the strength of claims is used both (i) to guide LLM training as models learn to generate arguments and assign them base scores (representing intrinsic strengths) and (ii) to compute ternary (true/false/uncertain) predictions from generated, scored arguments. As a result, at training time, argument generation and scoring can be optimised according to the quality of the induced argumentative predictions. Moreover, at inference time, the final prediction is faithful, by construction, to the arguments and scores determining the verdict, rather than being justified by a potentially unfaithful post-hoc reasoning trace as in conventional reasoning models. We finally show that, on two datasets for ternary claim verification, ITA improves upon argumentative baselines and can perform competitively against non-argumentative direct-prediction baselines, while providing verdicts that are computed deterministically from explicit, inspectable argumentative structures.

### [179] [Using Aristotle API for AI-Assisted Theorem Proving in Lean 4: A Formalisation Case Study of the Grasshopper Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20120)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索AI辅助定理证明在复杂数学问题中的实际能力边界，特别是当局部推理成功而全局组合逻辑仍未解决时的证据可靠性问题。

Method: 采用Lean 4进行形式化，对蚱蜢问题的广义版本进行建模，验证了四个关键辅助引理，并分析主定理中未完成的全局计数步骤。
