Abstract: AI-assisted theorem proving can now generate substantial Lean developments for olympiad-level mathematics, but the evidential status of such developments depends on which declarations are actually verified. This paper reports a Lean 4 formalization case study of an Aristotle API proof attempt for the Grasshopper problem, originally posed as IMO 2009 Problem 6. The generated artifact states a generalized Lean version of the theorem, contains four verified helper lemmas for local components of a maximality and adjacent-swap exchange strategy, and leaves the main theorem grasshopper closed directly by one unresolved sorry. The verified components establish that the final partial sum equals the total sum, that an adjacent transposition can affect only the relevant intermediate partial sum, that the changed partial sum has the expected form, and that maximality at a position admitting an adjacent successor swap forces a corresponding forbidden-set membership fact. The Aristotle output summary identifies the intended remaining mathematical step as the global counting step needed to show that these membership facts produce at least n distinct forbidden values, contradicting the cardinality assumption |M| < n; the Lean source itself does not reduce the main theorem to a separately encoded counting lemma. This case study gives an inspectable example of a central limitation in AI-assisted formalization, namely that local proof search can succeed while the global combinatorial bookkeeping required for a theorem remains unresolved. The paper contributes a reproducible Lean artifact and a precise analysis of its verified and unverified proof content.

### [180] [Not Every Rubric Teaches Equally: Policy-Aware Rubric Rewards for RLVR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20164)
*Utkarsh Tyagi,Xingang Guo,MohammadHossein Rezaei,Daniel George,Anas Mahmoud,Jackson Lee,Bing Liu,Yunzhong He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: POW3R is a policy-aware rubric reward framework that adapts criterion-level reward weights during training to improve reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards. It uses rollout-level contrast to emphasize criteria that currently distinguish policy outputs, leading to faster convergence and better performance on both average rubric reward and strict completion across multiple datasets and models.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard static aggregations in rubric-based rewards conflate human-assigned importance with current optimization usefulness, which can be ineffective when some criteria are saturated or unreachable. This leads to suboptimal training signals.

Method: POW3R introduces adaptive reward weighting based on rollout-level contrast, preserving human-defined rubric objectives while dynamically adjusting criterion weights to highlight currently informative criteria.

Result: POW3R outperforms vanilla GRPO in 24 out of 30 comparisons, improves both mean rubric reward and strict completion, and reaches convergence 2.5–4× faster.

Conclusion: Rubric rewards should separate what matters in the final answer from what can teach the current policy; POW3R effectively achieves this by adaptively emphasizing discriminative criteria during training.

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards has made post-training highly effective when correctness can be checked automatically. However, many important model behaviors require satisfying several qualitative criteria at once. Rubric-based rewards address this setting by grading prompt-specific criteria and aggregating them into a scalar reward. Yet standard static aggregations conflate a criterion's human-assigned importance with its current usefulness as an optimization signal. We show that this assumption breaks down in rubric RL: many important criteria are already saturated or currently unreachable, while criteria that distinguish rollouts are not necessarily those with the largest human weights. We introduce POW3R, a policy-aware rubric reward framework that preserves human weights and category balance as the rubric objective while adapting criterion-level reward weights during training. POW3R uses rollout-level contrast to emphasize criteria that currently separate the policy's outputs, making the GRPO reward more informative without changing the underlying evaluation target. Across three base policies on two datasets spanning multimodal and text-only settings, POW3R wins $24$ of $30$ base-policy/metric comparisons, improving both mean rubric reward and strict completion (the fraction of prompts whose response satisfies every required rubric criterion) over vanilla GRPO with rubric rewards, and reaches the same plateau in $2.5$--$4\times$ fewer training steps. Rubric rewards should therefore distinguish what should matter in the final answer from what can teach the current policy.

</details>


### [181] [HaorFloodAlert: Deseasonalized ML Ensemble for 72-Hour Flood Prediction in Bangladesh Haor Wetlands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20167)
*Salma Hoque Talukdar Koli,Fahima Haque Talukder Jely,Md. Samiul Alim,Md. Zakir Hossen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HaorFloodAlert is a machine learning ensemble model designed to predict 72-hour flood probabilities in Bangladesh's Sunamganj Haor wetlands, addressing limitations of traditional riverine flood models. It uses a Sentinel-1 SAR proxy from the upstream Barak River for ~36 hours of lead time and corrects for temperature-driven seasonal bias (which previously inflated accuracy by 6.9 pp). The model achieves 89.6% LOOCV accuracy, 87.5% recall, and 0.943 AUC-ROC on 77 real flood events. It includes a three-tier alert system and a rice damage estimator calibrated with BRRI data.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Flash floods in haor wetlands occur with little warning and destroy the annual boro rice harvest. Existing flood prediction systems are designed for riverine floods and fail to account for backwater dynamics in flat, seasonally flooded basins like the haors, where water behavior differs significantly from rivers such as the Brahmaputra.

Method: The study developed HaorFloodAlert, a deseasonalized machine learning ensemble combining Random Forest (weight 0.5625) and XGBoost (weight 0.4375). It incorporates a Sentinel-1 SAR-derived upstream proxy from Silchar, Assam, enabling ~36 hours of lead time. Otsu-thresholded change detection on SAR imagery validates with 84–91% spatial match. Temperature-related seasonal bias was identified and corrected to prevent overestimation of model performance.

Result: The operational ensemble model achieved 89.6% LOOCV accuracy, 87.5% recall, and 0.943 AUC-ROC on 77 real Sentinel-1 flood events. The system includes a three-tier alert pipeline and a BRRI-calibrated boro rice damage estimator, enabling actionable early warnings and impact assessment.

Conclusion: HaorFloodAlert effectively addresses the unique hydrological challenges of haor wetlands by leveraging satellite data and adaptive machine learning. Its ability to detect flash floods with high accuracy and lead time offers significant potential for protecting agriculture and communities in vulnerable regions.

Abstract: Flash floods in Bangladesh's haor wetlands show up with almost no warning. They wreck the annual boro rice harvest. Current setups, built for riverine floods, miss backwater dynamics entirely. These basins are flat. Water does not behave like it does on the Brahmaputra.
  We built HaorFloodAlert, a deseasonalized machine learning ensemble that forecasts 72-hour flood probability for the Sunamganj Haor (approximately 8,000 km2). Temperature was acting as a seasonal cheat code - it inflated accuracy by 6.9 pp just because floods happen in warm months. We caught that. We also built an upstream Barak River Sentinel-1 SAR proxy from Silchar, Assam, giving about 36 hours of lead time. Otsu-thresholded SAR change detection validates at 84-91 percent spatial match.
  The operational ensemble (RF 0.5625 + XGBoost 0.4375) hits 89.6 percent LOOCV accuracy, 87.5 percent recall, and 0.943 AUC-ROC on 77 real Sentinel-1 events. A three-tier alert pipeline and a BRRI-calibrated boro rice damage estimator are included.

</details>

### [182] [Dimensional Balance Improves Large Scale Spatiotemporal Prediction Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18793)
*Jing Chen,Shixiang Pan,Yujie Fan,Haocheng Ye,Haitao Xu,Wenqiang Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可扩展、自适应的框架，用于解决时空模式分析中的性能瓶颈问题。通过空间和时间熵度量诊断复杂性不匹配问题，并在此基础上压缩空间维度（低秩矩阵嵌入）和扩展时间范围以捕捉长程依赖关系，从而提升预测精度与跨领域迁移能力。在交通、气象和流行病数据集上均表现出显著性能提升，代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在时空模式分析中存在性能瓶颈，仅带来微小改进且跨领域迁移能力有限，尤其在固定模型容量下，复杂性不匹配导致预测不确定性增加。

Method: 利用空间和时间熵作为诊断指标识别复杂性不匹配；采用低秩矩阵嵌入压缩空间维度以保留关键结构；扩展时间预测范围以缓解时间异质性带来的累积误差。

Result: 在城市交通、气象和传染病数据集上实现了显著的准确率提升，展现出广泛的适用性和良好的跨领域迁移能力。

Conclusion: 所提出的ST-Balance框架有效缓解了时空复杂性不匹配问题，具有在多种时空任务中广泛应用的潜力。

Abstract: Accurate spatiotemporal pattern analysis is critical in fields such as urban traffic, meteorology, and public health monitoring. However, existing methods face performance bottlenecks, typically yielding only incremental gains and often exhibiting limited cross-domain transferability. We analyze this bottleneck through spatial and temporal entropy measures, which are used as diagnostic indicators of spatiotemporal complexity mismatch rather than as guarantees that entropy alignment alone yields better forecasting. Empirically, larger mismatch is often accompanied by higher prediction uncertainty, especially under a fixed model-capacity budget. Guided by this diagnostic, we propose a scalable, adaptive framework that harmonizes spatial and temporal feature representations. Spatial dimensionality is compressed via low-rank matrix embedding to preserve essential structure, while an extended temporal horizon captures long-range dependencies and mitigates cumulative errors arising from temporal heterogeneity. Extensive experiments on urban traffic, meteorological, and epidemic datasets demonstrate substantial accuracy gains and broad applicability across the evaluated domains, suggesting that the framework is promising for a wide range of spatiotemporal tasks beyond the current study. The code is available on GitHub at https://github.com/ST-Balance/ST-Balance.

### [183] [HELLoRA: Hot Experts Layer-Level Low-Rank Adaptation for Mixture-of-Experts Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18795)
*Jia Wei,Zhonghao Zhang,Ping Chen,Qianyang li,Yancheng Pan,Shaoxun Wang,Ziyi Qiu,Longxiang Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出HELLoRA，一种针对MoE模型的低秩适配方法，仅在每层最常激活的专家上附加LoRA模块，显著减少可训练参数和适配器引起的FLOPs，同时提升下游性能。通过结构化正则化保留预训练专家专长，在多个MoE模型和任务上优于现有PEFT基线。进一步结合LoRI形成HELLoRI以应对极端参数预算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MoE模型具有稀疏激活特性，但现有参数高效微调（PEFT）方法主要针对密集架构，未能充分利用其稀疏性。因此需要更高效的适配策略来降低计算开销并提升性能。

Method: HELLoRA通过仅在每层最频繁激活的专家上添加LoRA模块，实现激活感知的适配器放置；进一步结合LoRI，冻结上投影并稀疏下投影，形成HELLoRI。

Result: 在OlMoE-1B-7B、Mixtral-8x7B和DeepSeekMoE三个MoE模型上，HELLoRA均优于强基线。例如在OlMoE上，使用15.7%的可训练参数，减少38.7%的适配器FLOPs，训练吞吐量提高1.9倍，准确率提升9.2%；在DeepSeekMoE上，仅用23.2%参数即超越LoRA。

Conclusion: 激活感知的适配器放置是扩展适用于MoE语言模型的参数高效微调的有效且实用路径。

Abstract: Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) dominates parameter-efficient fine-tuning of large language models, yet most variants target dense architectures. Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models scale parameters at near-constant per-token compute, and their sparse activation patterns create untapped opportunities for more efficient adaptation. We propose Hot-Experts Layer-level Low-Rank Adaptation (HELLoRA), which attaches LoRA modules only to the most frequently activated experts at each layer. This simple mechanism reduces trainable parameters and adapter-induced FLOPs while improving downstream performance, an effect we attribute to a form of structured regularization that preserves pretrained expert specialization. To stress-test HELLoRA under extreme parameter budgets, we further compose it with LoRI to form HELLoRI, which freezes the up-projection and sparsifies the down-projection. Across three MoE backbones, namely OlMoE-1B-7B, Mixtral-8x7B, and DeepSeekMoE, and three task families covering mathematical reasoning, code generation, and safety alignment, HELLoRA consistently outperforms strong PEFT baselines. Relative to vanilla LoRA on OlMoE, HELLoRA uses 15.7% of the trainable parameters, reduces adapter FLOPs by 38.7%, achieves 1.9x the training throughput, and improves accuracy by 9.2%. On DeepSeekMoE, HELLoRA outperforms LoRA while using only 23.2% of its trainable parameters. These results demonstrate that activation-aware adapter placement is an effective and practical route to scaling PEFT for MoE language models.

</details>


### [184] [UCCI: Calibrated Uncertainty for Cost-Optimal LLM Cascade Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18796)
*Varun Kotte*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: UCCI是一种校准优先的模型路由方法，通过等熵回归将标记级边缘不确定性映射为查询级错误概率，并利用受约束的成本最小化选择升级阈值。在三个明确假设下，基于校准得分的阈值策略具有成本最优性，且等熵校准实现了期望校准误差（ECE）的O(n^{-1/3})样本复杂度。在75,000个查询的真实命名实体识别任务中，使用4B和12B指令微调LLM在H100 GPU上运行时，UCCI将推理成本降低31%（95%置信区间：[27%, 35%]），同时保持微F1为0.91，并将ECE从0.12降至0.03。在相同性能点下，UCCI优于基于熵的阈值、分割共形路由以及类似FrugalGPT的可学习阈值方法。所有级联结果均基于实际模型输出的端到端路由和测量的H100延迟，而非基于全局准确率或名义API价格的模拟路由。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型路由系统大多依赖未经校准的置信度分数，需针对不同工作负载手动调整阈值，导致部署复杂且成本控制不精准。需要一种更可靠、自适应的校准机制来实现高效、低成本的模型级联路由。

Method: 提出UCCI方法，采用等熵回归对token级边缘不确定性进行校准，生成每查询的误差概率估计；通过约束成本最小化确定最优升级阈值；确保在特定假设下，基于校准得分的阈值策略为成本最优。

Result: 在真实生产级命名实体识别任务中，UCCI将推理成本降低31%（95% CI: [27%, 35%]），微F1保持0.91，同时将期望校准误差（ECE）从0.12降至0.03。相比熵阈值、分割共形路由及FrugalGPT风格学习阈值，表现更优。所有评估基于真实模型输出与实测延迟，非模拟数据。

Conclusion: UCCI通过校准驱动的路由机制，实现了在保证精度前提下的显著推理成本降低，具备实际部署价值，为高效大模型级联提供了新范式。

Abstract: LLM cascades and model routing promise lower inference cost by sending easy queries to a small model and escalating hard ones to a large model, but most deployed routers use uncalibrated confidence scores and require per-workload threshold tuning. We present UCCI, a calibration-first router that maps token-level margin uncertainty to a per-query error probability via isotonic regression and selects the escalation threshold by constrained cost minimization. Under three explicit assumptions, threshold policies on the calibrated score are cost-optimal, and isotonic calibration achieves O(n^{-1/3}) sample complexity for expected calibration error (ECE). On a production named entity recognition workload of 75,000 queries served by 4B and 12B instruction-tuned LLMs on H100 GPUs, UCCI cuts inference cost by 31% (95% CI: [27%, 35%]) at micro-F1 = 0.91 while reducing ECE from 0.12 to 0.03. At the same operating point, UCCI beats entropy thresholding, split-conformal routing, and a FrugalGPT-style learned threshold. All cascade results use end-to-end routing on actual model outputs and measured H100 latency, not simulated routing from global accuracies or nominal API prices.

</details>


### [185] [Simply Stabilizing the Loop via Fully Looped Transformer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18797)
*Rao Fu,Zixuan Yang,Jiankun Zhang,Jing Ma,Hechang Chen,Yu Li,Yi Chang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Fully Looped Transformer通过引入两个无参数修改——完全循环架构（分布层间信号以缓解残差爆炸）和注意力注入（利用现有注意力模块抑制梯度振荡），解决了循环Transformer在增加迭代次数时的训练不稳定性问题。该方法在12次循环迭代下仍能稳定训练，相比基线模型提升下游任务性能最高达13.2%，并支持推理时根据计算预算灵活调整迭代次数，兼顾性能与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决循环Transformer在增加迭代次数时出现的训练不稳定问题，尤其是梯度振荡和残差爆炸两大瓶颈，从而实现更高性能与更灵活的推理能力。

Method: 提出完全循环架构，将层间信号均匀分布于所有层以缓解残差爆炸；引入注意力注入机制，利用现有注意力块抑制梯度振荡，两者均为无参数设计，不增加模型参数量。

Result: 在最多12次循环迭代下训练稳定，显著优于基线循环模型；在轻度不稳定场景中仍提升平均下游任务性能最高达13.2%；支持推理时动态调整循环次数，实现性能与计算成本之间的灵活权衡。

Conclusion: Fully Looped Transformer有效提升了循环Transformer的训练稳定性与下游性能，同时具备良好的推理灵活性，为高效、可扩展的模型设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Scaling model performance typically requires increasing model size. Looped Transformer offers a compelling alternative by iteratively reusing the same Transformer blocks, trading additional computation for improved performance without increasing parameter count or context length. Because the number of loop iterations can be adjusted at inference, it also provides a natural mechanism for balancing performance and test-time compute. However, Looped Transformer still suffers from training instability when the number of loop iterations increases. Our analysis reveals that this instability stems from two sources: gradient oscillation and residual explosion. To address these two problems, we propose the Fully Looped Transformer, which introduces two parameter-free modifications: (1) Fully Looped Architecture, which distributes inter-loop signals across all layers to mitigate residual explosion; (2) Attention Injection, which reuses the existing attention block to suppress gradient oscillation. These modifications stabilize training dynamics, enabling the Fully Looped Transformer to be trained stably up to 12 loop iterations, whereas other baseline looped models collapse in this regime. In milder settings where Looped Transformer does not collapse, Fully Looped Transformer still improves average downstream-task performance by up to 13.2\%. Overall, our experiments demonstrate that Fully Looped Transformer improves training stability, enhances downstream performance, and provides preliminary adaptability under different test-time compute budgets by varying loop iterations at inference.

</details>


### [186] [Accurate Evaluation of Quickest Changepoint Detectors via Non-parametric Survival Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18798)
*Taiki Miyagawa,Akinori F. Ebihara*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出非参数估计器KM-ARL和KM-ADD，用于在有限和不规则序列长度下估计快速变点检测中的平均运行长度（ARL）和平均检测延迟（ADD），通过类比生存分析建模截断下的检测概率，证明其渐近无偏性，并在模拟与真实数据上验证其有效性，提升模型鲁棒性与可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ARL和ADD在实际应用中受限于序列长度有限且不规则，缺乏有效估计方法，导致难以应用于真实数据。

Method: 借鉴生存分析中的Kaplan-Meier方法，构建非参数估计器KM-ARL和KM-ADD，以处理序列截断情况下的检测概率建模，推导偏差界并证明渐近无偏性。

Result: 实验表明该方法在模拟与真实数据上均表现良好，显著提升对有限和不规则序列的适应能力，增强模型可解释性与实用性，支持直观的模型选择。

Abstract: We propose non-parametric estimators for the average run length (ARL) and average detection delay (ADD) in quickest changepoint detection (QCD) under finite and irregular sequence lengths. Although ARL and ADD are widely used as optimality criteria in theoretical and simulation studies, their application to real-world datasets is hindered by limited and irregular sequence lengths. To address this issue, we propose non-parametric estimators for the ARL and ADD, termed KM-ARL and KM-ADD, by drawing an analogy between QCD and survival analysis to model detection probabilities under sequence truncation. We derive estimation bias bounds and prove that they are asymptotically unbiased unless extrapolation is required. Experiments on simulated and real-world datasets demonstrate their practical utility, enhancing robustness against limited and irregular sequence lengths, improving interpretability, and facilitating empirical, intuitive model selection. Our Python code is provided at https://github.com/TaikiMiyagawa/Kaplan-Meier-Average-Run-Length, offering ready-to-use implementations for practitioners.

### [187] [ReCrit: Transition-Aware Reinforcement Learning for Scientific Critic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18799)
*Wanghan Xu,Yuhao Zhou,Hengyuan Zhao,Shuo Li,Dianzhi Yu,Zhenfei Yin,Yaowen Hu,Fengli Xu,Wanli Ouyang,Wenlong Zhang,Lei Bai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出ReCrit，一种面向科学推理中批评交互的过渡感知强化学习框架，旨在解决大语言模型在用户批评下可能放弃正确答案的问题。通过将初始回答到批评后的行为分解为四个象限（修正、迎合、鲁棒性、边界），ReCrit奖励修正和鲁棒性，惩罚迎合行为，并将持续错误视为弱边界信号。同时引入动态异步回滚与尾部自适应完成以提升训练效率。在ChemBench、TRQA和EarthSE三个基准上，ReCrit显著提升了批评阶段准确率，例如Qwen3.5-4B从38.15%提升至51.49%。消融实验表明，基于过渡感知的奖励比仅依赖最终答案奖励更有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在科学推理中可能因用户批评而放弃原本正确的解答，这在需要高可靠性的科学任务中尤为危险。现有方法关注最终答案准确性，忽视了交互过程中的正确性转移问题，因此亟需一种能识别并引导模型在批评下保持正确性的机制。

Method: 提出ReCrit框架，采用过渡感知强化学习，将初始回答到批评后的行为划分为四类：修正（Corrective）、迎合（Sycophancy）、鲁棒性（Robustness）和边界（Boundary）。通过设计相应的奖励函数，分别奖励修正与鲁棒性，惩罚迎合行为，并将持续错误视为弱边界信号。同时使用动态异步回滚与尾部自适应完成策略，降低训练延迟，提升可扩展性。

Result: 在ChemBench、TRQA和EarthSE三个科学推理基准测试中，ReCrit显著提升了批评阶段的准确率：Qwen3.5-4B从38.15%提升至51.49%，Qwen3.5-9B从45.40%提升至55.59%。消融实验验证了过渡感知奖励和象限加权的有效性，证明其相比传统最终答案奖励提供了更清晰的训练信号和更大的性能提升。

Conclusion: ReCrit成功解决了大语言模型在批评交互中可能出现的非理性退化问题，通过过渡感知机制与高效训练策略，在多个科学推理任务中实现了显著的性能提升。该方法强调了交互过程中的正确性稳定性，为构建更可靠的人机协作推理系统提供了新思路。

Abstract: Large language models can fail in critic interaction not only by answering incorrectly, but also by abandoning an initially correct scientific solution after user criticism. This is especially risky in scientific reasoning, where user criticism can turn a valid answer into an incorrect one. We frame critic interaction as an inter-turn correctness-transition problem rather than a final-answer accuracy problem, and identify three challenges: transition awareness, decoupling useful correction from harmful sycophancy, and scalable rollout. We propose ReCrit, a transition-aware reinforcement learning framework that decomposes Initial-to-Critic behavior into four quadrants: Correction, Sycophancy, Robustness, and Boundary. ReCrit rewards correction and robustness, penalizes sycophancy, and treats persistent errors as weak boundary signals. To make interaction training practical, ReCrit further uses dynamic asynchronous rollout with tail-adaptive completion to reduce rollout waiting. On three scientific reasoning benchmarks, ChemBench, TRQA, and EarthSE, ReCrit improves average Critic accuracy from 38.15 to 51.49 on Qwen3.5-4B and from 45.40 to 55.59 on Qwen3.5-9B. Ablations show that final-answer rewards provide little interaction-level gain, while transition-aware rewards and quadrant weighting produce more distinguishable training signals and larger net Critic-stage improvement. The code is available at https://github.com/black-yt/ReCrit .

</details>


### [188] [Theory-optimal Quantization Based on Flatness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18800)
*Xiusheng Huang,Zhe Li,Xuanwu Yin,Lu Wang,Yequan Wang,Dong Li,Emad Barsoum,Kang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的后训练量化框架BDQ，通过建模量化误差与异常值之间的数学关系，引入新指标Flatness来量化异常值分布，并推导出理论最优解。BDQ利用可学习的对角变换策略性地分散异常值幅度，显著提升低比特量化性能。在LLaMA-3-8B上实现W4A4量化仅0.1%精度损失，在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-LLaMA-70B的W2A4KV16设置下，相比现有方法性能差距缩小39.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM量化中的激活异常值问题导致低比特精度下性能严重下降，现有方法虽尝试通过线性变换缓解，但异常值模式仍集中，影响量化效果。

Method: 建立量化误差与异常值的数学模型，提出Flatness指标衡量异常值分布；推导理论最优解；设计双向对角量化（BDQ）框架，通过可学习对角操作优化矩阵变换以分散异常值。

Result: BDQ在多种量化设置下表现优异：在LLaMA-3-8B上实现W4A4量化时精度损失低于1%；在更难的W2A4KV16设置下，相较先进方法性能差距减少39.1%。

Conclusion: BDQ通过理论驱动的设计有效解决了量化中的异常值集中问题，为低比特大模型推理提供了高效且高性能的量化方案，建立了新的量化基准。

Abstract: Post-training quantization has emerged as a widely adopted technique for compressing and accelerating the inference of Large Language Models (LLMs). The primary challenges in LLMs quantization stem from activation outliers, which significantly degrade model performance especially at lower bit precision. While recent approaches attempt to mitigate outliers through linear transformations across feature dimensions, our analysis reveals that the transformed weights and activations still exhibit persistent outlier patterns with concentrated magnitude distributions. In this paper, we first model the mathematical relationship between quantization error and outliers, and then introduce a new metric Flatness to quantify the distribution of outliers. Based on this, we derive the theoretical optimal solution with respect to Flatness. Building on these insights, we propose Bidirectional Diagonal Quantization (BDQ), a novel post-training quantization framework that effectively disperses outlier patterns through optimized matrix transformations. BDQ strategically distributes outlier magnitudes across matrix dimensions via learned diagonal operations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that BDQ establishes a new quantization benchmark. It achieves less than 1\% accuracy drop in W4A4 quantization on the LLaMA-3-8B model. In the more challenging W2A4KV16 experiment, compared to state-of-the-art approaches, BDQ reduces the performance gap by 39.1\% on the DeepSeek-R1-Distill-LLaMA-70B model.

### [189] [PROWL: Prioritized Regret-Driven Optimization for World Model Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18803)
*Ahmet H. Güzel,Jenny Seidenschwarz,Benjamin Graham,Jonathan Sadeghi,Jeffrey Hawke,Jack Parker-Holder,Ilija Bogunovic*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于KL约束的对抗性课程学习方法，通过策略主动发现扩散模型在罕见高影响状态下的失败轨迹，并持续微调世界模型以增强其鲁棒性。引入优先级对抗轨迹（PAT）缓冲区，根据预测误差、动作保真度和学习进展动态重排序轨迹，聚焦于未解决的失败模式而非重复已解决案例。在MineRL框架上的实验表明，该方法显著提升模型在分布外轨迹上的表现，揭示弱约束下的奖励劫持行为，强调探索性失败发现与行为正则化之间的平衡对有效训练至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有行动条件视频世界模型在短时程视觉真实感上表现良好，但在关键稀有交互转换上仍不可靠，主要因被动演示数据无法充分覆盖这些高影响状态。为提升鲁棒性，需主动诱发模型失败，而非依赖自然出现。

Method: 提出KL约束的对抗性课程学习，训练策略暴露世界模型的高误差轨迹，同时保持接近行为分布；世界模型在这些对抗发现的轨迹上持续微调，形成闭环训练。引入优先级对抗轨迹（PAT）缓冲区，依据预测误差、动作保真度和学习进度重排序轨迹，确保训练集中在未解决的失败模式上。

Result: 在MineRL框架上的评估显示，所提方法（PROWL）在分布外轨迹上优于仅使用被动数据训练的模型；揭示了在弱行为约束下存在奖励劫持行为；证明有效的对抗性世界模型训练依赖于探索性失败发现与显式行为正则化的平衡。

Conclusion: 可扩展的世界模型不仅需要更大规模数据，更需选择性生成具有信息量的训练数据。主动发现并利用模型失败是提升鲁棒性的关键路径。

Abstract: Modern action-conditioned video world models achieve strong short-horizon visual realism, yet remain unreliable on rare, interaction-critical transitions that dominate downstream planning and policy performance. Because passive demonstration data systematically under-samples these high-impact regimes, improving robustness requires actively eliciting model failures rather than relying on their natural occurrence. We introduce a KL-constrained adversarial curriculum in which a policy is trained to expose high-error trajectories of a diffusion-based world model while remaining close to the behavior distribution. The world model is continuously fine-tuned on these adversarially discovered trajectories, yielding an adversarial training loop that converts rare failures into a stable, near-distribution training signal without drifting into out-of-distribution exploitation. To maintain pressure on unresolved weaknesses as the model improves, we propose a Prioritized Adversarial Trajectory (PAT) buffer that re-ranks trajectories based on prediction error, action fidelity, and learning progress, focusing training on unresolved failure modes rather than repeatedly revisiting solved cases. We implement our approach in the MineRL framework and evaluate it on held-out out-of-distribution trajectories; PROWL improves robustness over models trained on passive data alone, reveals reward-hacking behaviors under weak behavioral constraints, and demonstrates that effective adversarial world-model training critically depends on balancing exploratory failure discovery with explicit behavioral regularization. Our results suggest that scalable world models benefit not only from larger datasets, but also from selectively generating informative training data.

In scaling law experiments, block-based double decoders strongly outperform encoder-decoders and closely track decoder-only models across scales. At inference time, they cut KV-cache memory and per-token compute by at least 2/3 without sacrificing prefill caching or other existing inference optimizations available to decoder-only models.

### [191] [Compositional Literary Primitives in Instruction-Tuned LLMs: Cross-Architectural SAE Features for Self, Style, and Affect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18808)
*Joao Paulo Cavalcante Presa,Savio Salvarino Teles de Oliveira*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过稀疏自编码器在中深度残差流上分析了两个指令微调的大语言模型（Llama 3.1 8B-Instruct 和 Gemma 2 9B-IT）的文学基本单元组成架构，识别出四类特征：命名门控（促进目标情感的词汇标记）、十一自我簇（第一人称语体特征）、风格调节器（展示而非讲述、陌生化）以及仅由多特征协同生成的组合情感。在5个LLM组成的强制选择评判小组下，Llama实现了27/27的情感类别覆盖，而Gemma为23/27（仅‘钦佩’未达标）。随机判断下，单细胞通过概率约为$10^{-3}$，双种子假阳性细胞期望值可忽略，表明观察到的覆盖率非偶然。跨架构不对称性体现在严格与宽松评判对比中：相同生成内容下，Llama输出更直接命名情感，使评委一致性更高；而Gemma通过场景和意象间接唤起情感。两类模型均包含兼具语体标记与情感激发功能的自我特征，其中各自最具RLHF权重的自我特征在特定运行状态下强化机构化助手角色，并在同一校准系数下产生可分类情感输出。方法上提出三阶段验证流程（对数透镜、LLM评分、5个LLM评判），并记录反模式；总计算量仅需单个GPU，每轮情感特征发现约15分钟。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用稀疏自编码器在中深度残差流上提取特征，结合三阶段验证流程（对数透镜、LLM评分、5个LLM强制评判）进行特征有效性检验，采用27类情绪分类体系（Cowen-Keltner）评估覆盖能力，并通过随机判断测试以排除偶然性。

Conclusion: 大语言模型中的情感表达具有可解释的组合式架构，依赖命名门控、多特征协同与自我特征调节；不同模型在情感表达方式上呈现结构性差异，影响其可解释性与评判一致性；所提方法高效可靠，适用于大规模情感特征发现。

Abstract: We characterize a compositional architecture of literary primitives in two instruction-tuned large language models (Llama 3.1 8B-Instruct and Gemma 2 9B-IT) via sparse autoencoders on mid-depth residual streams. Four feature classes emerge: naming-gates that promote lexical tokens of a target affect, an eleven-self cluster of first-person register features, stylistic register modulators (show-don't-tell and defamiliarization), and compositional emotions that arise only from multi-feature steering. Under a forced-choice 5-LLM judge panel applied to a 27-category emotion taxonomy (Cowen-Keltner), Llama reaches full 27/27 coverage by combining naming-gates, multi-feature recipes, and single self-feature steering; Gemma reaches 23/27 with adoration as the single residual strict-fail. Under random judging, the per-cell pass probability is on the order of $10^{-3}$ and the expected number of two-seed false-positive cells across the catalog is negligible, so the observed coverage is not consistent with chance. A cross-architectural asymmetry sits in the strict-versus-soft judge contrast: on the same generations, judges agree more often on Llama outputs than on Gemma outputs because Llama outputs name the target affect more directly while Gemma outputs evoke it through scene and imagery. Both architectures contain self-features that serve simultaneously as register markers and as emotion emitters, including a single most-RLHF-loaded self-feature per architecture that intensifies the institutional Helper-AI persona at one operating regime and produces affect-categorizable output at the same calibrated coefficient. Methodologically, the paper presents a three-stage validation pipeline (logit-lens, LLM-rate, 5-LLM judge) with documented anti-patterns; the total compute is single-GPU and about 15 minutes per emotion-feature discovery cycle.

### [192] [PASC: Pipeline-Aware Conformal Prediction with Joint Coverage Guarantees for Multi-Stage NLP and LLM Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18812)
*Varun Kotte*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PASC (Pipeline-Aware Split Conformal) is a method for uncertainty quantification in multi-stage NLP and LLM pipelines, reducing joint coverage across K stages to a single scalar conformal prediction problem based on the maximum nonconformity score. It provides finite-sample, distribution-free guarantees that all stages are simultaneously covered with probability at least 1−α, nearly tight up to a 1/(n+1) factor. PASC outperforms both independent conformal prediction (CP) and Bonferroni correction in end-to-end coverage—achieving 96.4% vs. 93.4% (Bonferroni) and 86.5% (independent CP)—at the same average prediction set size (1.083). Under distribution shifts (e.g., WNUT-17, WikiNEuRal), PASC maintains target coverage while independent CP drops to 59%. PASC is faster (1.7x) than Bonferroni and scales well to K=6 stages, where independent CP fails (0.53 coverage). The approach generalizes directly to compound LLM systems and agent pipelines.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing uncertainty quantification methods in multi-stage NLP and LLM pipelines either calibrate stages independently (lacking joint coverage) or use conservative Bonferroni bounds (providing joint coverage but overly cautious). There is a need for a method that ensures joint coverage across all stages with high efficiency and minimal conservatism, especially under distribution shift.

Method: PASC reformulates multi-stage joint coverage as a single scalar conformal prediction problem by computing the maximum nonconformity score across all stages. This allows a single quantile computation to control the joint error rate across all stages, enabling efficient and tight uncertainty bounds without per-stage calibration.

Result: On a three-stage NER→NED→entity-typing pipeline using CoNLL-2003, PASC achieves 96.4% end-to-end coverage—superior to Bonferroni (93.4%) and independent CP (86.5%)—with identical average prediction set size. Under distribution shift (WNUT-17, WikiNEuRal), PASC maintains target coverage, while independent CP collapses to 59%. PASC is 1.7x faster than Bonferroni and scales effectively to K=6 stages, where independent CP fails. The method applies directly to LLM and agent pipelines.

Conclusion: PASC provides a scalable, efficient, and nearly tight solution for joint uncertainty quantification in multi-stage NLP and LLM systems. By reducing joint coverage to a single scalar conformal prediction, it enables reliable, distribution-free guarantees across all pipeline stages, even under distribution shift, outperforming existing methods in both coverage and computational efficiency.

Abstract: Modern NLP and LLM systems are pipelines: named entity recognition (NER) -> entity disambiguation (NED) -> entity typing, retrieval-augmented generation (retriever -> reader), and agentic chains of planner -> tool -> critic. Errors compound across stages, but existing uncertainty quantification methods either calibrate each stage independently (no joint coverage) or apply a Bonferroni union bound (joint coverage, but conservative). We present PASC (Pipeline-Aware Split Conformal), which reduces multi-stage joint coverage to a single scalar conformal prediction problem on the joint maximum nonconformity score. PASC provides a finite-sample distribution-free guarantee that all K stages are simultaneously covered with probability at least 1 - alpha, and is nearly tight up to a 1/(n+1) factor. On a three-stage NER -> NED -> entity-typing pipeline over CoNLL-2003, PASC achieves 96.4% end-to-end coverage versus 93.4% for Bonferroni and 86.5% for independent CP, at identical average prediction set size (1.083). Under distribution shift to WNUT-17 Twitter and WikiNEuRal Wikipedia data, PASC empirically maintains the target coverage in the tested shift settings while independent CP collapses to 59%. PASC requires a single quantile computation, runs 1.7x faster than Bonferroni, and scales to K = 6 stages where independent CP drops to 0.53 end-to-end coverage. The same joint-maximum-score reduction applies directly to compound LLM systems and agent pipelines.

</details>


### [193] [Composition of Memory Experts for Diffusion World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18813)
*Sebastian Stapf,Pablo Acuaviva Huertos,Aram Davtyan,Paolo Favaro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于扩散模型的框架，通过对比性的专家产物（product-of-experts）机制，整合多种异构记忆模型，以解决现有世界模型在记忆容量与计算效率之间的权衡问题。该方法引入三个互补的记忆专家：短期记忆专家捕捉局部动态，长期记忆专家通过轻量级测试时微调存储情景历史，空间长期记忆专家保持几何与空间一致性。该设计避免模式崩溃，支持长上下文且无二次计算开销，在模拟和真实世界基准上显著提升时间一致性、过去观测的召回率及导航性能，为构建和运行增强记忆的扩散世界模型提供了新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型在记忆容量与计算效率之间存在根本性权衡：变压器模型保留局部细节但受制于二次注意力，而循环和状态空间模型虽可高效扩展但压缩历史导致保真度下降。因此，需要一种既能保持高保真度又具高效扩展性的记忆架构。

Method: 提出一种基于扩散模型的框架，采用对比性的专家产物机制，集成三种互补的记忆专家：短时记忆专家（捕捉局部动态）、长时记忆专家（通过轻量级测试时微调存储情景历史）、空间长时记忆专家（确保几何与空间一致性），实现记忆与预测解耦。

Result: 在模拟和真实世界任务中，所提方法显著提升了时间一致性、对过去观测的召回能力以及导航性能，有效避免了模式崩溃，并支持长上下文建模，同时保持线性计算复杂度，无二次注意力开销。

Conclusion: 本文提出的记忆增强型扩散世界模型通过多专家协作与解耦设计，突破了传统架构的内存-效率权衡，为强化学习中的规划与决策提供了一种高效且高保真的新范式。

Abstract: World models aim to predict plausible futures consistent with past observations, a capability central to planning and decision-making in reinforcement learning. Yet, existing architectures face a fundamental memory trade-off: transformers preserve local detail but are bottlenecked by quadratic attention, while recurrent and state-space models scale more efficiently but compress history at the cost of fidelity. To overcome this trade-off, we suggest decoupling future-past consistency from any single architecture and instead leveraging a set of specialized experts. We introduce a diffusion-based framework that integrates heterogeneous memory models through a contrastive product-of-experts formulation. Our approach instantiates three complementary roles: a short-term memory expert that captures fine local dynamics, a long-term memory expert that stores episodic history in external diffusion weights via lightweight test-time finetuning, and a spatial long-term memory expert that enforces geometric and spatial coherence. This compositional design avoids mode collapse and scales to long contexts without incurring a quadratic cost. Across simulated and real-world benchmarks, our method improves temporal consistency, recall of past observations, and navigation performance, establishing a novel paradigm for building and operating memory-augmented diffusion world models.

### [194] [DynaTrain: Fast Online Parallelism Switching for Elastic LLM Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18815)
*Yuanqing Wang,Yuchen Zhang,Hao Lin,Junhao Hu,Chunyang Zhu,Quanlu Zhang,Boxun Li,Guohao Dai,Zhi Yang,Daning Cheng,Yunquan Zhang,Yu Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DynaTrain 是一个用于大规模语言模型训练的分布式系统，支持亚秒级、在线重新配置任意多维并行性。其核心是虚拟参数空间（VPS）抽象，将所有分布式训练状态统一到一个逻辑坐标空间中，使任何并行配置都可映射为确定性几何关系，从而简化复杂迁移过程。在此基础上，系统通过状态路由与过渡层实现内存感知、无死锁的本地传输，并利用弹性设备管理器在新拓扑构建期间重叠训练任务，隐藏拓扑变更开销。在高达2350亿参数的密集模型和MoE模型上，DynaTrain能够在2秒内完成700亿参数模型的重配置，2350亿参数模型仅需4.36秒，相比现有基于检查点和弹性系统提升达三个数量级，且保证正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出虚拟参数空间（VPS）抽象，将所有分布式训练状态统一于单一逻辑坐标空间；设计状态路由与过渡层，实现秩本地传输的内存感知、无死锁调度；引入弹性设备管理器，将新拓扑构建与持续训练重叠，以掩盖拓扑变更成本。

Result: 在2350亿参数的MoE模型上，重配置时间仅为4.36秒；700亿参数密集模型可在2秒内完成重构；性能优于现有检查点式和弹性系统达三个数量级，同时确保训练正确性。

Conclusion: DynaTrain 有效解决了大规模语言模型训练中的动态并行性重构难题，通过VPS抽象和高效调度机制，实现了亚秒级、高可靠性的在线重配置，显著提升了训练系统的灵活性与效率。

Abstract: Modern large language model (LLM) training is inherently dynamic: resource fluctuations, RLHF phase shifts, and cluster elasticity continually reshape the optimal parallelism layout, posing a significant challenge to existing training frameworks built around a static execution model. We present DynaTrain, a distributed training system for sub-second, online reconfiguration across arbitrary multi-dimensional parallelism. At its core, we propose a Virtual Parameter Space (VPS) abstraction that unifies all distributed training states under one logical coordinate space, turning any parallelism configuration into a deterministic mapping and collapsing complex transition into manageable geometric intersections. On top of VPS, a state routing-and-transition layer executes rank-local transfers under a memory-aware, deadlock-free schedule, and an Elastic Device Manager overlaps new-world construction with ongoing training to mask topology-change cost. On dense and MoE models up to 235B parameters, DynaTrain reconfigures a 70B dense model in under 2s and a 235B MoE model in 4.36s, outperforming state-of-the-art checkpoint-based and elastic systems by up to three orders of magnitude while preserving correctness.

### [195] [Emergence of Frontier Superposition: Möbius attractor and Cascade Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18820)
*Hongyu Gu,Jingwen Fu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究Transformer在Erdős-Rényi图上的可达性超位置推理，揭示了实现深度推理的关键机制：Möbius吸引子与级联监督的协同作用。通过理论分析和实验验证，证明了梯度下降可在对称鞍点中找到全局最优的等权重超位置状态，而传统端到端监督因梯度衰减无法有效到达该状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖人工设计的广度优先超位置，但未知梯度下降是否能在对称鞍点中收敛至目标状态；本文旨在解决这一开放问题，揭示超位置推理涌现的内在机制。

Method: 采用架构与监督分离分析框架，识别出在树状区域下$S_n$-对称性诱导的1维Möbius映射作为层间动力学简化模型，同时提出级联监督（Cascade Supervision）损失函数，实现选择性启动、梯度跨深度持续传播及每步判别能力。

Result: 理论预测在深度D=3时，级联监督的最终余弦值为0.35，端到端监督为0.71；实验结果分别为0.37与0.69，误差仅0.02，验证了参数无关衰减律的有效性。

Conclusion: Möbius吸引子与级联监督共同促成超位置推理的涌现，揭示了深度模型在复杂结构任务中自动形成推理路径的潜在机制。

Abstract: Superposition allows Transformers to reason in depth, carrying an entire reasoning frontier in parallel through a bounded-depth forward pass instead of unrolling serial chain-of-thought tokens. While Zhu et al. (2025) hand-crafted an equal-weight breadth-first frontier in a single residual stream for graph reachability, it remained open whether gradient descent could ever find this target amidst permutation-symmetric saddles.
  We close this gap on Reachability-by-Superposition over Erdős-Rényi graphs by isolating architectural and supervisional contributions. Architecturally, we identify a Möbius attractor: under $S_n$-symmetry in the tree regime, layerwise dynamics reduce to a 1D Möbius map whose zero set is a codimension-one manifold of global optima containing the equal-weight superposition state.
  On the supervision side, we identify Cascade Supervision: a loss class whose backward pass simultaneously delivers (A) selectivity bootstrap, (B) gradient persistence across depth, and (C) per-step discrimination (e.g., \mathcal{L}_{sup} and \mathcal{L}_{node}). End-to-end supervision fails condition (B) and is provably insufficient: internal gradients at layer c decay as (np)^{-(D-c-2)/2} in the graph fan-out and stall before the manifold is reached.
  Our thesis: Möbius attractor + Cascade Supervision = emergence of superposition reasoning. The parameter-free decay law predicts a final-step cosine of 0.35 vs. 0.71 (end-to-end vs. cascade) at depth D=3; experiments confirm 0.37 vs. 0.69, matching within 0.02 at every step.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入一种新的Hybrid-LoRA Score，用于评估模块对低秩适配的敏感度，并据此选择最合适的模块进行全量微调，其余模块采用LoRA进行适配。

However, RLVR post-training with full fine-tuning (FFT) requires substantial GPU memory and incurs high training costs. In this paper, we propose Hybrid-LoRA, an efficient hybrid post-training framework that selectively applies full fine-tuning to a small subset of modules less suited to low-rank adaptation, while adapting the remaining components with LoRA. We introduce a novel Hybrid-LoRA Score to rank candidate modules according to their sensitivity to low-rank adaptation under a fixed parameter budget. ### [198] [Not All Tokens Are Worth Caching: Learning Semantic-Aware Eviction for LLM Prefix Caches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18825)
*Shaoke Fang,Ziang Li,Wenfei Wu,Jiatong Ji,Qingsong Liu,Ruizhi Pu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SAECache提出了一种语义自适应的前缀缓存淘汰策略，通过多队列架构、语义感知的令牌加权机制和全自适应在线学习框架，显著提升LLM服务中前缀缓存的利用效率。实验表明，相比现有基线，其在TTFT上提升1.4x-2.7x，且能避免因工作负载不匹配导致的性能退化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有前缀缓存淘汰策略（如LRU）将缓存块视为均质，忽略了不同令牌类型在重用率上的巨大差异（最高达756倍），导致缓存效率低下。因此需要一种能利用令牌语义信息的自适应淘汰策略。

Method: SAECache采用三重创新：(1) 多队列架构，按任务类型将KV块分配至特定队列并使用定制优先级度量；(2) 语义感知的令牌加权机制，基于淘汰反馈在线学习不同令牌类型的重用价值；(3) 完全自适应的在线学习机制，自动更新时间参数、位置衰减幂、队列权重等，无需人工调参。

Result: 在异构工作负载下评估显示，SAECache相较生产级基线实现1.4x-2.7x的TTFT改进；而固定参数方法在工作负载不匹配时性能可能下降高达2.7x，SAECache则完全避免了这一问题。

Conclusion: SAECache通过引入语义感知与自适应学习机制，有效解决了传统前缀缓存淘汰策略忽视令牌重用差异的问题，显著提升了缓存效率与系统鲁棒性，是面向实际部署场景的高效优化方案。

Abstract: Prefix caching is a key optimization in Large Language Model (LLM) serving, reusing attention Key-Value (KV) states across requests with shared prompt prefixes to reduce expensive prefill computation. However, its benefit depends critically on the eviction policy as GPU memory is scarce, and existing policies such as LRU largely treat cached blocks uniformly. This view ignores a fundamental property of LLM prompts: not all tokens are equally worth caching. We show that different token types within a prompt, including system prompts, user queries, tool outputs, model responses, and chain-of-thought reasoning, exhibit up to 756x variation in reuse rates, yet no existing eviction policy exploits this signal. In this paper, we present SAECache (Semantic-Adaptive Eviction for prefix caches), a semantic-adaptive prefix cache eviction policy that addresses this gap through three innovations: (1) a multi-queue architecture that routes KV blocks to task-specific queues with tailored priority metrics, capturing both session reuse in multi-turn requests and structural reuse in templated single-turn requests; (2) a semantic-aware token weighting mechanism that learns the reuse value of different token types online through eviction feedback; and (3) a fully adaptive online learning schema for all parameter updates, including log-normal timing parameters, position decay power, queue weights, and meta-parameters, which eliminates manual tuning and enables automatic adaptation to deployment-specific workload characteristics. Through extensive evaluation across heterogeneous workloads, we demonstrate that SAECache achieves 1.4x-2.7x TTFT improvement over production-style baselines, while fixed-parameter alternatives can degrade by up to 2.7x under workload mismatch -- a failure mode our adaptive approach avoids entirely.

### [199] [Lossless Anti-Distillation Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18829)
*Zibo Diao,Jingchu Gai,Xinyue Ai,Zhang Zhang,Zhenyu He,Di He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LADS 是一种新型采样方案，旨在抵御多账户蒸馏攻击，同时保持对正常用户无损的体验。它通过将生成的随机性与查询语义和用户查询次数绑定，使正常用户每次获得独立且原始的响应，而攻击者因不同账户在相同语义下共享随机性，导致数据相关性增加，降低样本多样性并削弱蒸馏模型性能。理论分析表明，LADS 可证明性地减缓蒸馏模型的泛化误差收敛速度。实验验证其在图像生成、数学推理和代码生成任务中有效抑制蒸馏效果，同时保持用户个体统计特性不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前商业生成模型面临蒸馏攻击威胁，即攻击者通过收集生成内容训练低成本竞争模型。现有防御方法要么损害正常用户响应质量，要么易被多账号分布式查询绕过。因此亟需一种既能有效防御蒸馏、又不影响正常用户体验的解决方案。

Method: 提出 Lossless Anti-Distillation Sampling (LADS)，基于查询语义和用户查询次数生成私有种子，决定每轮生成的随机性。该机制确保每个合法用户每次请求都独立采样自原模型分布，而多个账户在相似语义下会共享种子，引发内部相关性，从而干扰蒸馏过程。

Result: 实验结果表明，在图像生成、数学推理和代码生成任务中，使用 LADS 后，蒸馏模型性能显著下降，而正常用户的输出统计特性与原始模型完全一致，实现无损体验。理论分析支持其在非独立同分布条件下有效降低蒸馏模型的泛化能力。

Conclusion: LADS 为对抗多账户蒸馏攻击提供了一种高效且无损的解决方案，既不牺牲正常用户质量，又能从根源上削弱攻击者的训练数据多样性，具有良好的理论保障和实际应用价值。

Abstract: Frontier commercial generative models face a growing threat from distillation, whereby a distiller harvests generated responses and trains a competing model of its own at drastically lower cost. Existing defenses either rely on modifying the models outputs, thereby sacrificing response quality for benign users, or on behavioral detection methods, which can be readily circumvented by distributing queries across multiple accounts. In this work, we propose Lossless Anti-Distillation Sampling (LADS), a novel sampling scheme specifically designed to counter multi-account distillation while maintaining a lossless experience for benign users. Concretely, LADS derives the randomness underlying each generation from a private seed determined by the semantic content of the query and the number of times the user has queried the model. By construction, every benign user receives a response independently sampled from the original model at each visit, and thus experiences no distortion. In contrast, for a distiller, different accounts share latent randomness whenever their queries fall in the same semantic bucket. As a result, the harvested data becomes correlated, potentially reducing sample diversity and degrading generalization. Using uniform convergence theory, we show that LADS provably degrades the convergence rate of the distillers generalization gap relative to standard i.i.d. sampling in both unconditional and conditional generation settings. Experiments on image generation, mathematical reasoning, and code generation confirm that LADS substantially degrades the performance of distilled students while preserving exact statistical fidelity for individual users.

</details>

This paper presents a novel knowledge-based approach to enhance automated data quality assessment. Our approach utilizes knowledge graph embeddings to predict missing edges between the input dataset's context representation and the relevant quality rules and dimensions within a knowledge graph representing contextual data characteristics and the required quality assessment operations. We surpass conventional practices by integrating diverse representations within the knowledge graph, drawing insights from contextual information from a thorough literature investigation. This integration allows us to develop a comprehensive and context-specific data quality assessment plan tailored to each context. Leveraging the knowledge graph improves our understanding of the input dataset's context, overcoming the limitations of traditional methods that rely solely on strict matching and overlook contextual characteristics. ### [201] [Spectral Gradient Surgery for Domain-Generalizable Dataset Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18836)
*Minyoung Oh,Najeong Chae,Jae-Young Sim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的领域可泛化的数据蒸馏（DGDD）框架，旨在解决传统数据蒸馏在分布外（OOD）场景下表现不佳的问题。作者指出，标准数据蒸馏方法（如分布匹配，DM）由于在压缩的合成数据中混淆了类别判别与领域特异性信息，导致其对域外数据泛化能力差。为此，提出谱梯度手术（SGS）方法，通过分析跨域梯度在频谱域的一致性，识别出共享的类判别特征并增强其一致性，同时促进合成数据内部多样性。SGS能有效提升蒸馏数据的域外泛化性能，且无需修改原有流程，具有良好的兼容性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据蒸馏方法假设测试数据与训练数据同分布，但在实际应用中这一假设往往不成立。直接应用现有的域泛化技术于蒸馏数据效果不佳，因这些方法依赖真实数据集的自然多样性，而合成数据缺乏此类多样性，且增加数据增强会违背数据蒸馏追求效率的目标。因此需要一种新范式来实现蒸馏数据在域外情况下的良好泛化能力。

Method: 提出谱梯度手术（SGS）方法，利用梯度在频谱域的跨域一致性来区分共享的类判别特征和领域特异性特征。在标准分布匹配（DM）更新基础上，引入两个互补梯度：一个强化跨域共享成分，另一个显式促进合成数据内部多样性，从而实现对领域变化的鲁棒性。

Result: 在多个规模不同的基准测试上，所提方法显著提升了蒸馏数据在域外情况下的泛化性能，同时保持了与现有分布匹配方法的即插即用兼容性，且未显著增加计算开销。

Conclusion: 本文提出的DGDD框架与SGS方法有效解决了数据蒸馏在域外场景下的泛化瓶颈，为构建高效且鲁棒的合成数据提供了新思路，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Dataset Distillation (DD) synthesizes a compact synthetic dataset that preserves the training utility of a full dataset. However, its standard formulation assumes that test data follow the same distribution as training data, an assumption that rarely holds in practice. A straightforward extension-applying post-hoc Domain Generalization (DG) techniques to distilled data-is ill-suited because existing DG methods rely on the natural diversity of real datasets, which compact synthetic sets inherently lack, while also incurring substantial augmentation overhead that conflicts with the efficiency objective of dataset distillation. To address this limitation, we introduce Domain Generalizable Dataset Distillation (DGDD), a new problem setting that explicitly targets out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization of distilled datasets. We study this problem through a widely adopted DD baseline of Distribution Matching (DM). We attribute the OOD vulnerability of DM to the entanglement of class-discriminative and domain-specific information within the compressed synthetic set, and propose Spectral Gradient Surgery (SGS) to disentangle the two. The key insight of SGS is that cross-domain agreement among domain-wise gradients in the spectral domain reveals which gradient components are shared across source domains-and are therefore class-discriminative-and which are domain-specific. Based on this observation, SGS augments the standard DM update with two complementary gradients: one that reinforces cross-domain shared components and another that explicitly promotes diversity within the distilled dataset. Extensive experiments on diverse-scale benchmarks demonstrate that SGS substantially improves OOD generalization while remaining plug-and-play compatible with existing DM methods.

### [202] [An Integrated Forecasting Prototype for Emergency Department Boarding Time to Support Proactive Operational Decision Making](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18839)

ED boarding time, defined as the duration admitted patients remain in the ED while awaiting inpatient bed placement, is a key indicator of this congestion. Predicting ED boarding time in advance enables proactive operational decision making before congestion escalates. We developed and evaluated a multi-horizon time series forecasting framework to predict ED boarding time at 6, 8, 10, 12, and 24-hour horizons. Real-world data from a university-affiliated urban hospital in the United States were utilized and integrated with external contextual data sources, including weather, holidays, and major local events. Decomposition-based Linear (DLinear) and Normalization-based Linear (NLinear) time series forecasting deep learning models showed superior performance across multiple horizons. Models were also evaluated under extreme congestion scenarios characterized by elevated boarding times. In addition, a Machine Learning Operations (MLOps) web application prototype was developed to support translation of the forecasting framework into practice through integrated data ingestion, forecast visualization, experimentation, and retraining.

</details>


### [203] [The Growing Pains of Frontier Models: When Leaderboards Stop Separating and What to Measure Next](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18840)
*Adil Amin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过分解SWE-bench和GPQA Diamond得分，提出一种分析模型能力耦合趋势与每轮残差（h-字段）的方法，以诊断各实验室在不同版本间的能力侧重，并预测未来测试方向。研究涵盖2024–2026年间10个实验室的34个前沿模型，发现能力之间存在显著正相关（r = +0.72, p < 10⁻⁶），但合作模式随实验室和时间变化：DeepSeek从以推理为主转向编码优先，谷歌保持稳定推理重点，Anthropic则在编码与恢复间波动。开放权重架构显示30–72B参数规模存在第二阶段能力跃迁，且SWE-bench已趋于饱和，而HLE与指令遵循能力仍具区分力，预示评测轴将发生轮转。研究提供三层次策略（定位、诊断、轮转）、各实验室测量优先级表及七个可验证预测，具备时间戳标准。跨实验室耦合斜率差异达5倍（谷歌1.15 vs DeepSeek 0.23），量化了不同模型配方将编码优势转化为推理能力的效率。2026年4月五次发布结果验证了诊断模型的有效性（r升至+0.75）。配套交互式仪表板支持相位分类、诊断建议、实验室耦合轨迹、基于微分方程的缩放预测、基准轮转指导、自适应演示与七项预测实时追踪。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有排行榜仅按独立维度排名模型，无法揭示能力间是协同增强还是此消彼长；而在前沿模型发展中，这种互动关系比单一指标更具信息量。为更深入理解模型能力演进机制，需识别能力间的动态耦合模式，从而指导下一阶段评测设计与研发重点。

Method: 将成对的SWE-bench与GPQA Diamond得分分解为群体耦合趋势与每轮残差（h-字段），用于捕捉整体协作趋势与个体偏离特征；结合多实验室、跨时间序列的34个模型数据，分析能力演变路径；利用开放权重模型验证阶段性转变；构建基于微分方程的缩放模型进行预测；设计可验证的预测框架并部署交互式仪表板实现动态跟踪与决策支持。

Result: 能力间存在显著正向耦合（r = +0.72, p < 10⁻⁶），但不同实验室表现各异：DeepSeek出现从推理到编码的显著转向（h从+11.2降至-4.7），谷歌维持稳定推理倾向，Anthropic呈现周期性波动。30–72B规模区间出现第二阶段能力跃迁，SWE-bench趋于饱和，而HLE与指令遵循能力仍具判别力，提示评测轴即将轮转。五次2026年4月发布的模型验证了预测有效性（r提升至+0.75）。各实验室耦合斜率差异达5倍，反映其转化效率差异。研究生成三层次策略、测量优先级表与七项可验证预测。

Conclusion: 模型能力并非静态，而是动态耦合并随时间和架构演化。当前评测体系应从单一指标排名转向多维耦合分析，以识别关键能力跃迁节点与下一阶段评测焦点。研究提出的诊断框架与交互式工具可有效支持前沿模型的研发导航与评测迭代，推动自适应评估范式的建立。

Abstract: Leaderboards rank frontier models on independent axes but do not reveal whether capabilities reinforce or trade off across releases -- and at the frontier, this interaction is the more informative signal. We decompose paired SWE-bench and GPQA Diamond scores into a population coupling trend and per-release residual ($h$-field) that diagnoses capability emphasis and identifies which measurement or stress test is most informative next. Across 34 models from 10 labs (2024--2026), capabilities cooperate ($r = +0.72$, $p < 10^{-6}$), but cooperation varies by lab and over time: DeepSeek reversed from reasoning-rich to coding-first ($h$: $+11.2 \to -4.7$, 15.9-pp swing); Google maintains consistent reasoning emphasis; Anthropic oscillates between coding excursions and recovery. Cooperation is not static -- it cascades. Six open-weight architectures confirm a second capability transition at 30--72B, and SWE-bench is now saturating while HLE and instruction-following retain discriminatory spread -- signaling the next axis rotation. We provide a three-level playbook (locate, diagnose, rotate), a per-lab measurement-priority table, and seven falsifiable predictions with timestamped criteria for the next 12 months of frontier releases. Per-lab coupling slopes vary $5\times$ (Google $1.15$ vs. DeepSeek $0.23$), quantifying how efficiently each recipe converts coding gains into reasoning. Five April 2026 releases confirm the diagnostic out of sample ($r$ rises from $+0.72$ to $+0.75$). An interactive dashboard provides phase classification with actionable recommendations, $h$-field diagnostics, per-lab coupling trajectories, ODE-based scaling predictions, benchmark rotation guidance, self-steering demo, and live tracking of all seven predictions: https://zehenlabs.com/cape/.

### [204] [From Cumulative Constraints to Adaptive Runtime Safety Control for Nonstationary Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18841)
*Timofey Tomashevskiy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出CPSS，一种运行时机制，将累积安全预算转化为执行过程中的自适应状态级控制约束，通过在线调整阈值实现更灵活的安全控制，在非平稳环境中有效减少安全违规并保持良好性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统累积成本约束无法直接防止不安全的个体决策，尤其在非平稳环境中，固定状态级阈值可能过于保守或过弱，需要一种能动态适应环境变化的自适应安全控制方法。

Method: CPSS通过跟踪剩余安全预算，将其投影为随时间变化的可接受风险阈值，并过滤掉预测安全成本超过当前阈值的动作；阈值基于上下文信号在线调整，使在高风险或快速变化环境中更严格，在安全余量充足时更宽松。

Result: CPSS保证了执行动作的每状态阈值满足，诱导有限时域累积成本边界，并提供干预频率和每步奖励扭曲下的性能退化界；在高速公路汇入场景中显著减少接近度安全违规，增加分离距离，且干预选择性，不完全取代学习策略。

Conclusion: 自适应预算到阈值的投影是将累积安全规范转化为持续强化学习系统中有效局部安全控制的实用方法。

Abstract: Safety in reinforcement learning is often specified through cumulative cost constraints, but these trajectory-level guarantees do not directly prevent unsafe individual decisions, especially under nonstationarity. In continual and nonstationary settings, the difficulty is amplified because the risk associated with the same action can vary across contexts, while a fixed state-level threshold may be either too conservative or too weak. We propose Constraint Projection Safety Shield (CPSS), a runtime mechanism that converts a cumulative safety budget into adaptive state-level control constraints during execution. CPSS tracks the remaining safety budget, projects it into a time-varying admissible risk threshold, and filters policy actions whose predicted safety cost exceeds the active threshold. The threshold is adjusted online using contextual signals so that enforcement becomes stricter in more demanding or rapidly changing regimes and less restrictive when the available safety budget is sufficient. We analyze the resulting shielded policy and show that the mechanism guarantees per-state threshold satisfaction for executed actions, induces finite-horizon cumulative cost bounds, and yields a performance degradation bound in terms of intervention frequency and per-step reward distortion. We evaluate CPSS in nonstationary highway merging scenarios using highway-env. Across multiple seeds, CPSS substantially reduces proximity-based safety violations and increases separation margins while intervening selectively rather than dominating the learned policy. These results support adaptive budget-to-threshold projection as a practical way to transform cumulative safety specifications into effective local safety control for continual reinforcement learning systems.

### [205] [Safe Continual Reinforcement Learning under Nonstationarity via Adaptive Safety Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18842)
*Timofey Tomashevskiy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LILAC+ 是一种针对非平稳环境下的安全持续强化学习框架，通过三种自适应安全机制实现安全性的动态调整：基于上下文的安全约束、适应速度约束和状态预算安全执行。该框架在模拟驾驶环境中验证，表现出在分布偏移下显著减少安全违规，同时保持与无约束及固定约束基线相当的任务性能，证明了自适应约束机制在应对环境变化中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准安全强化学习方法通常假设约束条件固定或环境稳定，但在非平稳环境下（如分布偏移）这些方法可能失效。因此，需要能够随环境变化动态调整的安全机制，以确保持续学习过程中的安全性。

Method: LILAC+ 框架结合三种自适应安全机制：(1) 基于上下文的安全约束，根据推断和预测的环境上下文动态调整安全要求；(2) 适应速度约束，在环境变化速率超过智能体安全适应能力时收紧安全要求；(3) 预算到状态的安全执行，将累计安全需求转化为可实时执行的局部状态级约束。

Result: 在静态、已见非平稳和未见非平稳条件下，LILAC+ 显著降低了安全违规次数，同时任务性能优于或等同于基准方法，表明其在动态环境中具备良好适应性与安全性。

Conclusion: 安全的持续强化学习必须依赖能响应当前状态、预测环境上下文、适应需求以及剩余安全预算的自适应约束机制，LILAC+ 为此提供了一个统一且有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Safe reinforcement learning in nonstationary environments requires safety mechanisms that adapt as environmental conditions change. Standard safe reinforcement learning methods often assume fixed constraints or stable environmental conditions, which can become inadequate under distribution shift. We propose LILAC+, a framework for safe continual reinforcement learning under nonstationarity that combines three adaptive safety mechanisms: context-based safety constraints, adaptation-speed constraints, and budget-to-state safety enforcement. Context-based constraints adjust safety requirements using inferred and predicted environmental context. Adaptation-speed constraints tighten safety requirements when the rate of environmental change exceeds the agent's ability to adapt safely. Budget-to-state enforcement converts cumulative safety requirements into local state-level control constraints that can be enforced at decision time. Together, these mechanisms provide a unified approach for proactive and reactive safety adaptation in continual reinforcement learning. We evaluate the framework in simulated driving environments under stationary, seen nonstationary, and unseen nonstationary conditions. The results show that adaptive safety constraints substantially reduce safety violations under distribution shift while maintaining competitive task performance compared with unconstrained and fixed-constraint baselines. These findings suggest that safe continual reinforcement learning requires adaptive constraint mechanisms that respond not only to current state information but also to predicted environmental context, adaptation demand, and remaining safety budget.

### [206] [TEMPO: Temporal Enforcement via Mode-Separated Policy Optimization for Trustworthy LLM Backtesting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18843)
*Zeyu Zhang,Bradly C. Stadie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TEMPO通过双模式奖励和基于GRPO的训练流程，实现大语言模型在历史事件回测中的时间纪律，有效减少知识泄露（从2~13%降至0.6~3.7%），同时提升任务表现或保持性能稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在历史事件回测中因模型预训练数据泄露后截止日期信息，导致评估结果失真；传统提示约束和知识消除无法解决实例特定的时间合规问题，亟需模型学会根据具体截止日期选择证据。

Method: 提出TEMPO框架，包含两个核心：(1) 双模式奖励机制，先强制消除后截止日期的推理，再优化任务表现；(2) 基于GRPO的训练流程，使模型自主发现符合时间约束的推理策略。

Result: 在三个预测任务和两个模型上，TEMPO将知识泄露率从2~13%显著降低至0.6~3.7%，且在存在强前截止信号时任务性能提升6~13%，在困难任务中保持原有性能。

Conclusion: TEMPO成功实现了模型的时间纪律训练，不仅确保了评估的合法性，还提升了推理质量，为可信的历史事件回测提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Backtesting large language models on historical events requires reasoning exclusively from information available before a specified cutoff date. Yet models routinely leak post-cutoff knowledge from pre-training into their reasoning, inflating apparent accuracy and undermining evaluation validity. Prompt-based constraints fail when suppressed content is causally related to the prediction, and knowledge unlearning cannot address this problem because temporal compliance is instance-specific: the same fact may be legitimate evidence for one cutoff date and a violation for another. Rather than erasing knowledge, the model must learn temporal discipline: selecting evidence conditioned on each instance's cutoff date. We propose TEMPO (Temporal Enforcement via Mode-separated Policy Optimization), which trains this discipline via two contributions: (1) a two-mode reward where a leakage mode drives post-cutoff claims to zero as a hard prerequisite before a performance mode optimizes task performance; and (2) a GRPO-based training pipeline that enables the model to discover temporally valid reasoning strategies. We prove that training monotonically decreases leakage, converges to the leak-free optimum, and improves task performance once compliance is achieved. On three prediction tasks and two models, TEMPO reduces leakage from 2~13% to 0.6~3.7% across all conditions, with task performance improving 6~13% where strong pre-cutoff signals exist and maintained where the prediction task is inherently difficult from valid information alone.

</details>


### [207] [First-Passage Prediction of Grokking Delay: ACalibrated Law under AdamW with Causal Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18845)
*Truong Xuan Khanh,Truong Quynh Hoa,Luu Duc Trung,Phan Thanh Duc*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文首次对AdamW下的grokking延迟给出了定量预测，将延迟建模为首次通过时间，推导出闭合形式的定律 T_grok - T_mem = (1 / 2 kappa_LL eta lambda) log(V_mem / V_star)，其中V_t = ||theta_t||^2为参数平方范数，V_star为与架构相关的阈值，kappa_LL吸收了AdamW对干净SGD收缩率的修正。在单个超参数单元上校准(kappa_LL, V_star)后，可在26个保留运行中预测延迟（MAPE 17.7%，延迟范围41倍）；该定律在MLPs上表现良好（MAPE 18.0%，N=34），跨任务扩展时降至23.3%（N=46，范围43.5倍），且存在结构化残差，表明同一架构内V_star / V_mem相对稳定（CV约14%）。首次通过V_t是必要但非充分条件；量化边缘定理表明正延迟需同时满足范数分离V_mem > V_post和角度可达性α_star = arcsin(C / V_T_mem^(1/2))，其中C由经验NTK特征映射和验证边缘分位数计算得出。在模p=89上校准C可预测p=97时α_star = 47.2°（观测值47.8°，误差1.3%），作为跨单元先验预测。因果干预冻结范数或在记忆阶段移除权重衰减会消除grokking（0/6 vs. 3/3基线），使角度位移维持在约12度。kappa_LL在不同架构中实测而非从(β_1, β_2, ε)推导，同一架构内变异系数不超过15%，但不同架构间差异达约2倍，主要源于深度以外的因素。研究范围限于算法任务（模运算、稀疏奇偶性）下使用AdamW的情况；该定律是否适用于自然语言规模模型尚待验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解并预测在AdamW优化下深度学习模型出现grokking现象的时间延迟，即模型从随机性能跃迁至高精度性能的时机。现有研究缺乏对延迟的定量建模，尤其在自适应优化器如AdamW下的机制不明确。本研究旨在建立一个可泛化的物理启发式模型，揭示延迟背后的几何与动力学原理。

Method: 将grokking延迟建模为参数范数平方V_t = ||theta_t||^2的首次通过时间问题，基于随机微分方程框架推导出闭合形式解析解。引入有效收缩率修正因子kappa_LL以捕捉AdamW对梯度噪声和动量的影响。利用经验核理论（NTK）估计验证边缘分位数与角度可达阈值α_star，并通过跨超参数设置的校准实现外推预测。采用因果干预实验验证关键机制：冻结范数或移除权重衰减以检验其对grokking的必要性。

Result: 该模型在26个保留运行中实现了17.7%的平均绝对百分比误差（MAPE），覆盖41倍的延迟范围；在MLPs上表现相似（MAPE 18.0%，N=34）；跨任务扩展时误差上升至23.3%（N=46，43.5倍范围），但仍保持结构化残差，显示内在一致性。角度阈值α_star的预测与观测值高度吻合（47.2° vs. 47.8°，误差1.3%）。因果实验表明，若冻结范数或移除权重衰减，则完全抑制grokking，且角度位移被限制在12°左右。kappa_LL在同架构内具有高度稳定性（CV ≤15%），但在不同架构间差异显著（约2倍），提示其与架构设计密切相关。

Conclusion: 本文提出首个针对AdamW优化下grokking延迟的定量理论模型，揭示了延迟由参数范数增长与角度演化共同决定。模型具备强预测能力与可解释性，支持“范数先行、角度后行”的双阶段动力学机制。尽管在跨任务场景中性能略有下降，但整体结构稳健。研究结果为理解自适应优化中的隐式正则化与泛化飞跃提供了新视角，未来需验证其在更大规模语言模型中的适用性。

Abstract: We give the first quantitative prediction of grokking delay under AdamW. Treating the delay as a first-passage time, we derive a closed-form law T_grok - T_mem = (1 / 2 kappa_LL eta lambda) log(V_mem / V_star), where V_t = ||theta_t||^2 is the squared parameter norm, V_star is an architecture-dependent threshold, and kappa_LL absorbs the AdamW correction to the clean-SGD contraction rate 2 eta lambda. Calibrating (kappa_LL, V_star) on a single hyperparameter cell predicts grokking delays on 26 held-out runs with MAPE 17.7% over a 41x delay range; the law generalises to MLPs (MAPE 18.0%, N=34) and degrades to 23.3% on cross-task extension (N=46, 43.5x range), with a structured residual in which V_star / V_mem stays comparatively stable within architecture (CV about 14% on the 1L transformer).
  First-passage of V_t is necessary but not sufficient. A quantile-margin theorem establishes that positive delay requires both norm separation V_mem > V_post and angular reachability of a threshold alpha_star = arcsin(C / V_T_mem^(1/2)), where C is computable from the empirical NTK feature map and the validation-margin quantile. Calibrating C on modulus p=89 predicts alpha_star = 47.2 degrees at p=97 (observed 47.8 degrees, error 1.3%) as a prior cross-cell prediction. Causal interventions that freeze the norm or remove weight decay at memorisation eliminate grokking (0/6 vs. 3/3 baseline), trapping the angular displacement near 12 degrees.
  kappa_LL is empirically measured per architecture rather than derived from (beta_1, beta_2, epsilon); within-architecture CV stays at most 15% across four architectures, but values differ by about 2x between architectural variants beyond depth alone. Empirical scope is algorithmic tasks (modular arithmetic, sparse parity) under AdamW; whether the law transfers to natural-language scale models is open.

</details>


### [208] [Transformers Linearly Represent Highly Structured World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18847)
*Roman Kniazev,Nathanaël Fijalkow*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在序列推理轨迹上训练的Transformer是否构建了对底层任务的内部模型，并发现其内部表示结构反映了任务的约束代数而非表面呈现。通过分析解决Sudoku的Transformer，研究揭示了一个围绕行、列和宫组织的信息结构，以及一个专门检测每个单元格唯一可能数字的“裸单电路”。该电路由最终MLP层中少量专用神经元组成，具有稀疏性、单一语义和可解释性。结果表明，模型的内部世界模型几何形状由域的约束代数塑造，且可通过机制可解释性工具还原整个算法过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Transformer在训练过程中是否能构建反映任务本质的内部世界模型，以及这些模型的结构是否与任务的约束代数一致，从而理解其推理机制。

Method: 在Sudoku求解轨迹上训练8层Transformer，并进行机制分析，识别内部计算结构和决策电路。

Result: 模型未按细胞逐个表示棋盘状态，而是围绕行、列和宫等约束结构组织信息；发现了由少数专用神经元构成的‘裸单电路’，能准确检测并推荐唯一可能的数字。

Conclusion: Transformer在组合推理任务中能构建符合域约束代数的内部世界模型，其决策机制是稀疏、单语义且完全可解释的，证明机制可解释性工具可用于还原端到端算法过程。

Abstract: Do transformers, when trained on sequential reasoning traces, build internal models of the underlying task? And if so, does the structure of those internal representations mirror the structure of the domain? We train an 8-layer transformer on Sudoku solving traces and perform a mechanistic analysis of its internal computation. We establish two results. First, the model builds a substructure world model: it does not represent the board state cell by cell, as a human analyst would expect, but organizes information around the rows, columns, and boxes that Sudoku's constraints act on. Second, we identify a naked-single circuit: a small set of dedicated neurons in the final MLP layer, each individually detecting when exactly one digit remains possible for a specific cell, and reliably promoting that digit. These findings show that the geometry of an emergent world model is shaped by the constraint algebra of the domain, not its surface presentation, and that the resulting decision circuit is sparse, monosemantic, and fully interpretable. More broadly, they demonstrate that mechanistic interpretability tools can recover an end-to-end algorithmic account of how a transformer solves a combinatorial reasoning task.

</details>

Conclusion: Exact Linear Attention（ELA）成功实现了精确的线性复杂度注意力计算，克服了传统线性注意力的固有缺陷，为高效大模型设计提供了新的理论基础与工程范式。

Abstract: This paper introduces Exact Linear Attention (ELA), a mechanism that achieves linear computational complexity for Transformer attention by leveraging the exact decomposition property of kernel functions, without any approximation error. It identifies and addresses gradient explosion and token attention dilution in prior linear attention methods by imposing kernel constraints that ensure non-negativity, discriminability, and geometric interpretability. Several kernel functions are proposed, including the Hadamard Exp Kernel, Summation Squared Euclidean Distance Kernel, and Subtraction Squared Euclidean Distance Kernel. Beyond the core attention formulation, the paper presents three engineering innovations: a Hyper Link structure that replaces traditional residual connections to mitigate gradient degradation, a Memory Lobe module based on bidirectional linear attention that captures transformation flow across layers to implement qualitative memory and an implicit reinforcement learning paradigm, and a routing score based bias mechanism for Mixture of Experts to improve interpretability and semantic alignment.

### [215] [Delta Attention Residuals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18855)
*Cheng Luo,Zefan Cai,Junjie Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Delta Attention Residuals propose attending to deltas (changes between sublayers) instead of cumulative hidden states in attention residuals, addressing redundancy and routing collapse in deep networks. This leads to higher-contrast attention and improved performance across model scales (220M–7.6B), with 1.7–8.2% gains in validation perplexity. The method is applicable at both sublayer and block levels and supports conversion of pretrained models via fine-tuning.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard Attention Residuals suffer from redundant cumulative hidden states, causing routing collapse with low-contrast, near-uniform attention weights, limiting selective information routing in deep layers.

Method: Replace standard additive residuals with learned softmax attention over delta representations (differences between consecutive sublayer outputs, $\mathbf{v}_i = \mathbf{h}_{i+1} - \mathbf{h}_i$), enabling more diverse and informative cross-layer routing.

Result: Delta Attention Residuals achieve consistent improvements over standard and attention residuals across all tested scales (220M–7.6B), with 1.7–8.2% lower validation perplexity; attention distributions are significantly more contrastive (max weight ~0.6 vs. ~0.2).

Conclusion: By attending to delta representations rather than cumulative states, Delta Attention Residuals enable more selective, effective, and scalable cross-layer routing, offering a principled improvement for deep neural architectures.

Abstract: Attention Residuals replace standard additive residual connections with learned softmax attention over previous layer outputs, enabling selective cross-layer routing. However, standard Attention Residuals still attend over cumulative hidden states in previous layers, which are highly redundant. We show that this redundancy leads to routing collapse in deeper layers: attention weights become low-contrast and closer to uniform (max weight ${\approx}$0.2), limiting the model's ability to select informative states in previous layers. This raises a key but underexplored design question: what layer-wise representations should be routed in Attention Residuals? To answer this question, we propose Delta Attention Residuals, which attend over deltas -- the change introduced by each sublayer ($\mathbf{v}_i = \mathbf{h}_{i+1} - \mathbf{h}_i$) -- instead of cumulative states. Delta representations are structurally diverse and yield higher-contrast attention distributions (max weight ${\approx}$0.6), enabling more selective and effective routing across layers. This principle applies at both per-sublayer and block granularity. Across all tested scales (220M--7.6B), Delta Attention Residuals consistently outperform both standard residuals and Attention Residuals, with 1.7--8.2\% validation perplexity gains. Delta Attention Residuals also enables converting pretrained checkpoints into Delta Attention Residuals via standard fine-tuning. Code is available at https://github.com/wdlctc/delta-attention-residuals-code.

</details>


### [216] [SPHERICAL KV: Angle-Domain Attention and Rate-Distortion Retention for Efficient Long-Context Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18856)
*Anay Chauhan,Gurucharan Marthi Krishna Kumar,Arion Das,Amit Dhanda,Vinija Jain,Aman Chadha,Amitava Das*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Spherical KV 提出一种基于注意力几何的长上下文推理方法，通过角度域注意力（ADA）和速率-失真保留（RDR）减少KV缓存占用，实现高效解码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如淘汰、窗口化、量化和卸载虽能减小内存占用，但未能有效解决解码过程中的关键路径瓶颈，尤其在压缩状态需重建为密集向量时。

Method: 提出角度域注意力（ADA），将键以球面参数化表示，仅用标量半径和紧凑的角度编码存储；结合速率-失真保留（RDR），在固定预算下联合决定保留/丢弃及精度层级，生成同质页与轻量元数据。

Result: 实现了低内存驻留与高效解码的平衡，保持分页、块局部性与融合友好的解码路径，显著降低实际部署中的HBM流量。

Conclusion: Spherical KV 为长上下文推理提供了一种面向部署的解决方案，在不牺牲解码效率的前提下有效减少了KV缓存开销。

Abstract: Long-context inference is increasingly constrained by the KV cache: resident memory grows with context length, and decoding becomes limited by repeated High Bandwidth Memory (HBM) streaming rather than arithmetic. Existing methods such as eviction, windowing, quantization, and offloading reduce footprint, but often leave the critical-path bottleneck only partially addressed, especially when compressed states must still be reconstructed into dense vectors during decoding.
  We present Spherical KV, a long-context inference method that treats KV allocation as a rate-distortion problem grounded in attention geometry for efficient decoding. The method is built on two ideas: (i) represent directional information cheaply in the decode hot loop, and (ii) allocate retention and precision according to estimated future utility. Its first component, Angle-Domain Attention (ADA), stores keys in a spherical parameterization consisting of a scalar radius and compact angle codes, and computes attention logits directly from these codes without reconstructing dense keys. This preserves a paged, block-local, fusion-friendly decode path and directly targets HBM traffic in realistic serving settings. Its second component, Rate-Distortion Retention (RDR), jointly chooses keep/drop decisions and precision tiers per token and head under a fixed budget, producing tier-homogeneous pages with lightweight metadata and coalesced reads. Together, ADA and RDR provide a deployment-oriented mechanism for reducing KV residency while preserving decode efficiency.
