TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对医疗AI中多群体公平性的最差组等几率边缘正则化方法，旨在解决在固定推理操作点下不同人口群体间诊断行为不均的问题。该方法通过识别在真阳性与假阳性上表现最极端的子群体并施加统一惩罚，实现对多个社会属性（如年龄、性别、种族）的公平性优化，无需交集约束。在两个医学影像数据集上的实验表明，该方法显著降低了等几率和等机会的差异，同时保持了较高的诊断性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医疗AI的诊断性能在不同人口群体间存在系统性差异，而传统的子群体AUC可能掩盖临床中重要的不公平现象。在固定推理操作点下，某些群体可能出现过度诊断（高真阳率与假阳率），而其他群体则出现诊断不足（低真阳率与假阳率），这些相反趋势在整体AUC中相互抵消，但导致实际临床决策中的不公。因此需要一种能同时评估并缓解多维度人口特征下公平性问题的方法。

Method: 提出一种最差组等几率边缘正则化器，通过在每次更新中识别由显式人口属性（如年龄、性别、种族）定义的、边际偏差最大的子群体，并施加统一惩罚，从而在不引入显式交集约束的情况下实现跨多个社会维度的公平性优化。

Result: 在两个真实世界的多标签医学影像数据集上，所提方法在保持几乎不变的AUC值的同时，显著降低了等几率和等机会的群体差异，有效提升了模型在多人口属性下的公平性表现。

Conclusion: 本文提出的正则化方法能够在不牺牲诊断性能的前提下，有效缓解医疗AI模型在多人口群体间的诊断不平等，为实现可解释、可部署的公平医疗人工智能提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Diagnostic performance in medical AI varies systematically across demographic groups, yet subgroup AUC can mask clinically important disparities. At a fixed inference-time operating point, some groups may exhibit over-diagnostic behaviour, characterized by elevated true and false positive rates, while others show under-diagnostic patterns with reduced true and false positive rates. These opposing tendencies can cancel in aggregate AUCs while producing meaningful inequities in clinical decision-making. Motivated by the need to assess and mitigate such disparities at the operating point and across multiple demographic attributes simultaneously, we propose a worst-group equalized-odds margin regularizer. The proposed regularizer explicitly targets subgroup-level deviations on both the true positive and false positive sides at inference. At each update, the method identifies subgroups defined by explicit demographic attributes (e.g., age, sex, and race) that exhibit the most extreme margin deviations and applies a unified penalty, enabling fairness optimization across multiple demographic axes without requiring explicit intersectional constraints. Across two medical imaging datasets in realistic multi-label settings, our method consistently reduces disparities in Equalized Odds and Equalized Opportunity with minimal impact on AUC, preserving diagnostic performance while improving fairness.

### [262] [GAE Falls Short in Imperfect-Information Self-Play Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19235)
*Zhiyuan Fan,Gabriele Farina*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: VRPO introduces Q-boosting, a variance-reduced advantage estimator using a centralized action-value critic, to improve policy optimization in competitive multi-agent reinforcement learning. It replaces sampled multi-step backups with Expected SARSA(λ) traces to reduce noise from stochastic action sampling, while maintaining PPO's clipped objective and on-policy updates. Empirically, VRPO performs strongly across various games including Dou Dizhu and Heads-Up No-Limit Texas Hold'em.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard PPO's generalized advantage estimation suffers from high variance due to stochastic future actions in imperfect-information games, which is exacerbated in equilibrium self-play even with an exact critic. This variance hinders stable and effective learning.

Method: Proposes Variance-Reduced Policy Optimization (VRPO), incorporating Q-boosting—a new advantage estimator based on a centralized action-value critic. Uses multi-step Expected SARSA(λ) traces to compute policy expectations at each step, thereby averaging out action-sampling noise, while preserving PPO’s clipped objective and on-policy actor updates.

Result: VRPO consistently achieves strong performance in both mid-sized and large-scale competitive games, including Dou Dizhu and Heads-Up No-Limit Texas Hold'em, demonstrating improved stability and effectiveness over standard PPO.

Conclusion: Q-boosting and VRPO effectively reduce variance in advantage estimation for stochastic policies in multi-agent reinforcement learning, leading to superior performance in challenging imperfect-information games.

Abstract: Competitive multi-agent reinforcement learning in imperfect-information games requires agents to act under partial observability and against adversarial opponents, necessitating stochastic policies. While self-play reinforcement learning with Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) has achieved strong empirical success, its standard advantage estimator, generalized advantage estimation, suffers from additional variance due to the sampling of stochastic future actions. This variance is amplified in equilibrium self-play because of the stochastic nature of the equilibrium policy and persists even when the critic is exact. We address this bottleneck by introducing $Q$-boosting, a variance-reduced advantage estimator based on a centralized action-value critic, and propose Variance-Reduced Policy Optimization (VRPO), incorporating this new estimator. The algorithm replaces sampled multi-step backups with a multi-step Expected SARSA$(λ)$ trace, computing policy expectations at each step to average out action-sampling noise, while retaining PPO's clipped objective and on-policy actor updates. Empirically, VRPO consistently achieves strong performance from mid-sized to large-scale games including Dou Dizhu and Heads-Up No-Limit Texas Hold'em.

</details>


### [263] [Euclidean Embedding of Data Using Local Distances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19243)
*Dimitris Arabadjis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在仅有局部距离图的情况下恢复数据的全局一致欧几里得嵌入问题，提出一种仅基于邻接图权重的最优距离表示方法。该方法不依赖任何先验的数据向量表示，通过求解匹配局部图距离与嵌入函数微分诱导的欧几里得度量的变分问题获得嵌入。推导出坐标无关形式的欧拉-拉格朗日方程，可直接从距离图计算所有算子。尽管方程为非线性且无显式表达式，但可通过迭代更新的稀疏线性问题求解。主要贡献包括：(a) 推导了连续情况下最优欧几里得嵌入的泛函方程；(b) 提出仅需邻接距离图、无需特征向量的表示无关公式；(c) 基于纯局部图操作的估计过程。实验在合成流形和真实数据集上验证了该非参数算法能一致保持局部度量结构与邻近关系，并逼近全局等距嵌入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常依赖数据的向量表示或参数化模型，难以在缺乏全局信息时准确恢复数据的欧几里得结构。本文旨在解决仅给定局部距离图时如何构建全局一致且保留局部度量特性的嵌入问题，尤其适用于无显式特征表示的数据场景。

Method: 提出一种基于变分原理的方法，将局部图距离与嵌入函数微分诱导的欧几里得度量相匹配。推导出坐标无关的欧拉-拉格朗日方程，利用邻接图直接计算所有算子，通过迭代更新的稀疏线性系统求解非线性方程。整个过程仅依赖局部图操作，无需预先向量表示。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在合成流形和真实数据集上均能有效保持局部度量结构与邻近关系，近似实现全局等距嵌入，表现出良好的稳定性与一致性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的非参数方法能够在仅依赖局部距离图的前提下，实现对数据的全局一致欧几里得嵌入，具备表示无关性、局部操作性及良好保距性能，适用于复杂结构数据的低维嵌入任务。

Abstract: We study the problem of recovering a globally consistent Euclidean embedding of data, given only a local distance graph and propose a method that optimally represents these distances. The method operates solely on a neighborhood graph weighted by pairwise distances, without requiring any prior vector representation of the data. The embedding is obtained by solving a variational problem that matches local, on-graph distances to the Euclidean metric, induced by the differentials of the embedding functions. The resulting Euler-Lagrange equations are derived in a coordinate-free form, enabling direct evaluation of all operators from the distance graph alone. Though non-linear and missing an explicit expression for their non-linearity, these equations are shown to be resolved as an iteratively updated sparse linear problem. The main contributions of the proposed approach are (a) the derivation of the functional equations governing the optimal Euclidean embedding in the continuum, (b) a representation-free formulation that requires only a neighborhood distance graph and no feature vectors and (c) an estimation procedure based exclusively on local graph operations. We experimentally evaluate the resulting non-parametric algorithm on synthetic manifolds and real datasets, demonstrating consistent preservation of local metric structure and neighboring relations, while approximating the global isometric embedding.

Although ECG XAI has been extensively investigated and steadily improved, practical pipelines and reporting conventions vary across studies, hindering reuse and reproducibility. To address these issues, we present Explainable AI framework for ECG models (ExECG), a Python framework that provides a three-stage pipeline: Wrapper standardizes access across heterogeneous ECG formats and intermediate representations, Explainer unifies diverse XAI methods under a shared execution protocol, and Visualizer supports consistent cross-method comparison within a unified interface. ### [265] [Backdooring Masked Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19262)
*Daniel Yiming Cao,Chengzhong Wang,Sheng-Yen Chou,Chengyu Huang,Pin-Yu Chen,Shengwei An*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文首次系统研究了掩码扩散语言模型（MDLMs）在训练阶段的后门攻击，提出SHADOWMASK攻击方法，通过替换标准全掩码终端分布为触发器-掩码混合先验，创建从触发器污染状态到攻击者指定目标的专用去噪路径，同时保持正常去噪行为。该方法具有高攻击成功率、良好的清洁数据性能、对参数高效微调和防御机制的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有针对高斯扩散模型或自回归语言模型的后门攻击不适用于依赖离散状态污染和迭代去噪的MDLMs，因此亟需针对MDLMs的训练时后门攻击研究。

Method: 提出SHADOWMASK攻击，修改MDLM前向污染过程，使用触发器-掩码混合先验替代标准全掩码分布；建立后门前向过程的数学形式，推导反向时间后验，并获得连续时间训练目标。

Result: 在DiT-based MDLM和LLaDA-8B-Instruct上，基于WikiText-103、OpenWebText和Alpaca的数据集测试显示，SHADOWMASK达到近100%攻击成功率，显著优于传统数据投毒，基本保持清洁数据性能，对全模型和参数高效微调有效，且对主流防御手段具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: SHADOWMASK是首个针对MDLMs的系统性训练时后门攻击方案，证明了其有效性与隐蔽性，揭示了MDLMs在安全方面的潜在风险。

Abstract: Masked diffusion language models (MDLMs) are emerging as a compelling new paradigm for text generation, but their training-time security remains largely unexplored. Existing backdoor attacks on Gaussian diffusion models or autoregressive language models do not directly apply to MDLMs because MDLMs rely on discrete state corruption and iterative denoising rather than continuous noising or left-to-right prediction. In this work, we present the first systematic study of training-time backdoor attacks on MDLMs. We propose SHADOWMASK, a backdoor attack that modifies the MDLM forward corruption process by replacing the standard all-mask terminal distribution with a trigger-mask mixture prior. This creates a dedicated denoising pathway from trigger-corrupted states to attacker-specified targets while preserving clean denoising behavior. We further provide a principled mathematical formulation by defining the backdoored forward process, deriving the reverse-time posterior, and obtaining the continuous-time training objective. Evaluations on DiT-based MDLM and LLaDA-8B-Instruct across WikiText-103, OpenWebText, and Alpaca show that SHADOWMASK achieves near-100% attack success, substantially outperforms standard data poisoning, largely preserves clean utility, remains effective under full-model and parameter-efficient fine-tuning, and is robust against representative defenses.

### [266] [CODA: Rewriting Transformer Blocks as GEMM-Epilogue Programs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19269)
*Han Guo,Jack Zhang,Arjun Menon,Driss Guessous,Vijay Thakkar,Yoon Kim,Tri Dao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CODA 是一种 GPU 内核抽象，将 Transformer 中的内存密集型操作（如归一化、激活函数、残差更新等）重参数化为 GEMM 加后处理（epilogue）程序，从而减少数据移动开销，在不牺牲性能的前提下提升框架生产力与硬件效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer 训练系统中，尽管核心是密集线性代数运算，但大量时间消耗在内存绑定的操作上，如归一化、激活、残差更新等，这些操作频繁移动大尺寸中间张量，造成显著的数据移动瓶颈。因此需要一种既能保持高性能又能提高开发效率的解决方案。

Method: 提出 CODA 抽象，将多种 Transformer 操作重新表达为 GEMM 加后处理的形式；固定 GEMM 主循环，暴露一组可组合的后处理原语（如缩放、约简、成对变换和累加），使这些操作能在 GEMM 输出块仍在芯片上时执行，避免过早写入全局内存。

Result: 在典型 Transformer 工作负载下，人工编写和 LLM 辅助编写的 CODA 内核均达到高性能，表明 GEMM 加后处理编程范式能够有效结合框架易用性与硬件高效性。

Conclusion: CODA 通过将内存密集型操作融入 GEMM 执行周期，显著缓解了数据移动瓶颈，为构建高效且易于开发的 Transformer 训练系统提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Transformer training systems are built around dense linear algebra, yet a nontrivial fraction of end-to-end time is spent on surrounding memory-bound operators. Normalization, activations, residual updates, reductions, and related computations repeatedly move large intermediate tensors through global memory while performing little arithmetic, making data movement an increasingly important bottleneck in otherwise highly optimized training stacks. We introduce CODA, a GPU kernel abstraction that expresses these computations as GEMM-plus-epilogue programs. CODA is based on the observation that many Transformer operators exposed as separate framework kernels can be algebraically reparameterized to execute while a GEMM output tile remains on chip, before it is written to memory. The abstraction fixes the GEMM mainloop and exposes a small set of composable epilogue primitives for scaling, reductions, pairwise transformations, and accumulation. This constrained interface preserves the performance structure of expert-written GEMMs while remaining expressive enough to cover nearly all non-attention computation in the forward and backward pass of a standard Transformer block. Across representative Transformer workloads, both human- and LLM-authored CODA kernels achieve high performance, suggesting that GEMM-plus-epilogue programming offers a practical path toward combining framework-level productivity with hardware-level efficiency.

</details>


### [267] [EviTrack: Selection over Sampling for Delayed Disambiguation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19283)
*Omer Haq*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EviTrack 是一种在延迟消歧场景下进行序列预测的测试时推理框架，通过维护一组竞争的潜在轨迹假设，并基于证据和似然比选择策略延迟决策，直到数据支持为止。它在合成基准上显著优于基于采样的基线方法，在相同推理预算下实现了更快的后消歧恢复。结果表明，在延迟消歧情况下，适度的轨迹级选择比增加采样覆盖更有效，强调了选择优于采样的原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在延迟消歧场景中，早期观测模糊，多个潜在解释长期共存，传统基于边缘推断的方法要么过早坍缩不确定性，要么在信息充分后无法及时恢复，因此需要一种能有效管理不确定性的新方法。

Method: EviTrack 采用轨迹级别的推理机制，维护一组竞争的潜在轨迹假设，利用证据强度和似然比进行动态选择，延迟最终决策直至有足够数据支持，借鉴多假设跟踪与先检测后跟踪的思想。

Result: 在具有已知真实轨迹的合成基准上，EviTrack 在相同推理预算下显著优于采样基线，表现出更快的后消歧恢复速度，证明了轨迹级选择的有效性。

Conclusion: 在延迟消歧环境中，适度的轨迹级选择比扩大采样范围更为有效，表明选择优于采样是实现可靠序列推断的关键原则。

Abstract: Sequential prediction is challenging in regimes of delayed disambiguation, where early observations are ambiguous and multiple latent explanations remain plausible until sufficient evidence accumulates. Standard approaches based on marginal inference struggle in this setting, either collapsing uncertainty prematurely or failing to recover once informative evidence arrives.
  We introduce EviTrack, a test-time inference framework that operates over latent trajectories rather than marginal states. EviTrack maintains a set of competing trajectory hypotheses and applies evidence- and likelihood-ratio-based selection to delay commitment until supported by data, drawing inspiration from hypothesis management in multiple hypothesis tracking and track-before-detect.
  To evaluate this setting, we construct a controlled synthetic benchmark with known latent ground truth that explicitly exhibits delayed disambiguation. At matched inference budget, EviTrack substantially outperforms sampling-based baselines, achieving faster post-disambiguation recovery.
  These results show that, in delayed disambiguation regimes, moderate trajectory-level selection is more effective than increasing sampling coverage, highlighting selection over sampling as a key principle for reliable sequential inference.

This paper presents the first comprehensive study of bidirectional knowledge distillation between Random Forests (RF) and Deep Neural Networks (DNN), addressing critical gaps in ensemble learning and model compression for big data applications. ### [269] [An Objective Performance Evaluation of the LSTM Networks in Time Series Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19311)
*Sooraj Sunil,Balakumar Balasingam*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出一个性能评估框架，比较了LSTM分类器与基于模型的期望最大化（EM）分类器在二元时间序列分类任务中的表现。通过蒙特卡洛模拟，在两种线性高斯状态空间模型上评估了两类分类器，以真实参数下的卡尔曼滤波似然比检验作为最优性能参考。结果表明，当数据符合假设模型时，EM分类器表现优异；而LSTM分类器需要更大的噪声差异才能可靠分类，且在测量噪声差异较小时，其性能始终低于参考分类器，无论序列长度或训练数据量如何。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用两个仅在噪声统计特性上不同的标量线性高斯状态空间模型，构建基准问题。使用卡尔曼滤波似然比测试作为理论最优性能参考。通过蒙特卡洛仿真，对LSTM分类器和基于期望最大化（EM）的模型分类器进行多维度评估：任务难度（由过程/测量噪声分离度控制）、序列长度、训练数据集大小。

Abstract: The rapid adoption of deep learning has increasingly led to data-driven models replacing classical model-based algorithms, even in domains governed by well-understood physical laws. While data-driven models, such as long short-term memory (LSTM) networks, have become a popular choice for time-series analysis, their performance relative to model-based approaches in structured environments is rarely evaluated objectively. This paper presents a performance evaluation framework comparing an LSTM classifier against a model-based expectation maximization (EM) classifier for binary time-series classification. The evaluation is conducted on two scalar linear Gaussian state space models differing only in their noise statistics, where the Kalman filter likelihood ratio test with true parameters serves as a reference for the best achievable classification performance.Through Monte Carlo simulations, the classifiers are evaluated across three axes: task difficulty, controlled by the separation in process or measurement noise between the two models; sequence length; and training dataset size. The results show that the EM classifier, which exploits the known model structure, performs strongly when the data conform to the assumed model class. The LSTM classifier requires a larger separation in noise statistics to achieve reliable classification, and its performance saturates below the reference classifier when the models differ only in measurement noise, regardless of sequence length or training dataset size.

### [270] [Inference-Time Scaling in Diffusion Models through Iterative Partial Refinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19317)
*Taegu Kang,Jaesik Yoon,Sungjin Ahn*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为迭代局部精炼（IPR）的推理时扩展方法，用于序列化扩散模型，无需外部验证器即可实现更全局一致的生成。通过重新加噪并基于剩余区域条件重生成部分区域，模型可在更丰富上下文中修正早期决策，显著提升满足全局约束的任务性能，如在MNIST Sudoku任务中有效解率从55.8%提升至75.0%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出迭代局部精炼（IPR），从已生成样本出发，对部分区域重新加噪并基于未修改区域条件进行重生成，实现迭代式局部修正，从而在不依赖外部验证器的前提下提升生成结果的全局一致性。

Result: 在需要全局约束满足的推理任务上，IPR显著提升性能：在MNIST Sudoku任务中，有效解率由55.8%提升至75.0%，证明该方法可作为无需外部验证器的有效推理时扩展策略。

Conclusion: 迭代局部精炼（IPR）是一种无需外部验证器的高效推理时扩展方法，适用于序列化、混合噪声条件下的扩散模型，能有效提升生成样本的全局一致性与任务表现。

Abstract: Inference-time scaling has emerged as a major approach for improving reasoning capabilities, and has been increasingly applied to diffusion models. However, existing inference-time scaling methods for diffusion models typically rely on external verifiers or reward models to rank and select samples, limiting their scalability to settings where such evaluators are available and reliable. Moreover, while recent diffusion models perform sequential inference with region-wise, mixed-noise conditioning, inference-time scaling tailored to this setting remains relatively underexplored. We propose Iterative Partial Refinement (IPR), an inference-time scaling method for sequential diffusion that requires no external verifier. Starting from an already-generated sample, IPR re-noises a subset of regions and regenerates them conditioned on the remaining regions, enabling the model to revise earlier decisions under a richer context than was available during the initial generation. This iterative partial refinement produces more globally consistent samples without external verification. On reasoning tasks requiring global constraint satisfaction, IPR consistently improves performance: on MNIST Sudoku, the valid solution rate increases from 55.8% to 75.0%. These results show that iterative partial refinement alone can serve as an effective inference-time scaling strategy for diffusion models in sequential, mixed-noise settings. Code is available at: https://github.com/ahn-ml/IPR

</details>


### [271] [An Exterior Method for Nonnegative Matrix Factorization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19325)
*Qiujing Lu,Tonmoy Monsoor,Ehsan Ebrahimzadeh,Kartik Sharma,Vwani Roychowdhury*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的非负矩阵分解（eNMF）框架，通过将低秩近似与非负性约束分离，避免传统内点法在非凸优化中收敛慢或陷入次优解的问题。eNMF从无约束最优解出发，通过旋转操作将因子映射到最接近非负正交锥的外部点，实现快速收敛至满足KKT条件的边界驻点。该方法具有几何解释能力，揭示了因子分解在排列和正交变换下的等价类。大规模实验表明，99%情况下不同算法趋向等效解；在多个真实与合成数据集上，eNMF优于9种主流算法共81种组合，在同等时间下误差降低最多30%，同等误差下速度提升最高150%。下游任务如音频处理与推荐系统也验证了其优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统非负矩阵分解（NMF）依赖内点法强制非负约束，导致在非凸问题中收敛缓慢或陷入次优解。为克服这一瓶颈，本文旨在设计一种脱离约束驱动、更高效且能获得高质量解的外点优化框架。

Method: 提出eNMF框架，将低秩近似与非负性约束解耦：首先求解无约束最优分解，再通过旋转操作将解投影至最接近非负正交锥的外部点，从而实现快速迭代更新并收敛至满足KKT条件的边界驻点。同时引入几何视角分析因子分解的等价类。

Result: 在400次实验中，99%情况下不同算法收敛于等效解；在9个基准测试中，eNMF在同等时间下平均降低30%重建误差，同等误差下最快提速150%；音频与推荐任务中显著提升性能，验证了方法的实际有效性。

Conclusion: eNMF通过外点优化思想成功突破传统NMF的收敛瓶颈，兼具理论清晰性与实践优越性，为非负矩阵分解提供了新范式。

Abstract: Nonnegative matrix factorization (NMF) seeks a low-rank approximation $X \approx UV^T$ with nonnegative factors and is commonly solved using interior methods that enforce feasibility throughout optimization. We show that such constraint-driven approaches can impede progress in the nonconvex landscape, leading to slow convergence or convergence to suboptimal stationary points. We propose an exterior framework for NMF (eNMF) that separates low-rank approximation from nonnegativity enforcement. Our method initializes from the optimal unconstrained factorization and introduces a rotation procedure that maps unconstrained factors to an exterior point closest to the nonnegative orthant. This viewpoint yields an algorithmic framework in which simple iterative updates converge to KKT-satisfying stationary points on the boundary of the positive orthant. The exterior formulation also enables a geometric interpretation of NMF solutions, clarifying equivalence classes of factorizations under permutation and orthogonal transformations. An intriguing numerical result, involving 400 NMF experiments across both real and synthetic datasets, show that in 99% of the cases, different algorithms tend to converge towards equivalent factor matrices. We benchmark eNMF against 9 state-of-the-art NMF algorithms with 9 initialization schemes across 3 real-world and 2 synthetic datasets. eNMF consistently outperforms all 81 competitors, achieving up to 30% lower reconstruction error under equal-time settings and up to 150% speedup under equal-error settings. The downstream experiments further demonstrate substantial performance gains in audio processing and recommendation tasks, corroborating the practical benefits of the proposed exterior optimization framework. Code is available at https://github.com/roychowdhuryresearch/eNMF

### [274] [The Evaluation Game: Beyond Static LLM Benchmarking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19377)

Abstract: As jailbreaks, adversarially crafted inputs that bypass safety constraints, continue to be discovered in Large Language Models, practitioners increasingly rely on fine-tuning as a defensive strategy. Yet the theoretical foundations underlying this robustness fine-tuning remain underexplored. We introduce a game-theoretic framework in which the interaction between an evaluator (auditing the model for jailbreaks) and a trainer is formalized as a two-player game.
  A key feature of our approach is the use of group actions, a mathematical structure that captures symmetries and transformations, to formally represent data augmentation. The simplest non-trivial instance is the circle with cyclic translation groups, where we exhibit various regimes depending on the trainer's generalization range. Below a critical threshold, the evaluator maintains a constant miss ratio for linearly many rounds, whereas other settings can yield very different behaviors. We further provide empirical evidence supporting locality-dependence of the model: for the three model families we tested (Llama, Qwen and Mistral), we have significant evidence that fine-tuning on adversarial prompts induces only local generalization, with refusal rates on test examples highly correlated with the distance to the fine-tuning prompts. Our framework recasts the central object of adversarial evaluation: a benchmark is not a static set of prompts but an orbit under the evaluator's group action, and audit protocols that ignore trainer-side adaptation cannot distinguish a genuine fix from a memorized patch.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Continual Model Merging (CMM) enables rapid customization of foundation models across sequentially arriving tasks, offering a scalable alternative to repeated retraining. However, existing merging rules lack explicit controllability over the allocation of learning capacity between previously learned capabilities and newly merged models. Consequently, as tasks are merged sequentially, this deficiency accumulates into severe forgetting, particularly in scenarios with heterogeneous task importance, where performance allocation becomes highly inconsistent. The key reason can be attributed to the fact that previous methods treat each task model as an isolated parameter point and apply fixed algebraic combinations, rather than explicitly constructing a transition that respects how independently trained models can be connected in parameter space. Motivated by mode connectivity, we assume that desirable merged models lie on low loss connecting paths, and that continual merging should follow such paths without crossing loss barriers that induce forgetting. Grounded in these insights, we propose a novel ODE-driven Merging (ODE-M) tailored for CMM that traces such a path by integrating a time-dependent velocity field and enforcing barrier constraints to prevent loss-increasing steps. ### [277] [When to Stop Reusing: Dynamic Gradient Gating for Sample-Efficient RLVR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19425)
*Yuchun Miao,Sen Zhang,Yuqi Zhang,Yaorui Shi,Qi Gu,Xunliang Cai,Lefei Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为动态梯度门控（DGG）的新方法，用于提升基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在大语言模型中的样本效率。核心创新在于发现并利用‘不相称权重发散’（DWD）现象：当策略发生严重退化时，语言模型头部（lm_head）的权重变化会急剧上升，而中间层保持稳定。理论证明了有害梯度集中于lm_head，且其梯度范数下界控制策略偏差。基于此，DGG实时监控lm_head梯度范数，提前拦截有害梯度，避免优化器被污染。实验表明，DGG在数学、ALFWorld、WebShop和搜索增强问答任务中，实现最高2.93倍的样本效率提升和2.14倍的壁钟速度提升，显著优于单次使用基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RLVR在大语言模型中虽是主流推理范式，但其生成采样成本高，样本效率成为瓶颈。虽然重用每批采样数据进行多次梯度更新可提高效率，但在RLVR中会导致策略剧烈偏移，引发性能下降。目前缺乏有效机制及时检测并阻止这种退化，因此亟需一种能实时预警并干预的轻量级方法。

Method: 提出动态梯度门控（DGG），通过监测lm_head梯度范数作为信号，识别潜在的灾难性策略偏移；一旦检测到异常上升，则主动截断或抑制有害梯度，防止其影响优化过程。该方法建立在对DWD现象的实证与理论分析基础上，具有明确的可解释性和可操作性。

Result: DGG在多个任务（数学、ALFWorld、WebShop、搜索增强问答）上均表现优异，相比标准单次使用基线，实现最高2.93倍的样本效率提升和2.14倍的壁钟时间加速，且无需额外训练或复杂调整，具备良好的泛化能力与实用性。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了RLVR中性能退化的关键机制——不相称权重发散（DWD），并据此设计出高效、轻量的动态梯度门控（DGG）机制。该方法为提升强化学习在大语言模型中的样本效率提供了可验证、可部署的解决方案，推动了高效智能推理系统的发展。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become the dominant paradigm for advanced reasoning in Large Language Models (LLMs), but rollout samples are expensive to obtain, making sample efficiency a critical bottleneck. A natural remedy is to reuse each rollout batch for multiple gradient updates, a standard practice in classical RL. Yet in RLVR, this amplifies policy shift, leading to severe performance degradation. Detecting the onset of degradation early enough to stop reuse remains an open and challenging problem. We close this gap by identifying the \textit{Disproportionate Weight Divergence (DWD)} phenomenon: performance degradation is synchronized with a sharp surge in the \texttt{lm\_head} weight change, while intermediate layers remain stable. Empirically, we verify that DWD emerges consistently across diverse LLMs and tasks. Theoretically, we prove that (i) harmful gradients concentrate at the \texttt{lm\_head} while intermediate layers are structurally attenuated, and (ii) the \texttt{lm\_head} gradient norm lower-bounds the policy divergence. These results establish the \texttt{lm\_head} gradient norm as a principled, real-time signal of catastrophic policy shift. Guided by this insight, we propose \textit{Dynamic Gradient Gating (DGG)}, a lightweight intervention that monitors the \texttt{lm\_head} gradient norm in real time and intercepts harmful gradients before they corrupt the optimizer. DGG consistently matches or exceeds the standard single-use baseline, achieving up to $2.93\times$ sample efficiency and $2.14\times$ wall-clock speedup across math, ALFWorld, WebShop, and search-augmented QA tasks.

### [278] [When the Majority Votes Wrong, the Intervention Timing for Test-Time Reinforcement Learning Hides in the Extinction Window](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19444)
*Hongxiang Lin,Zhirui Kuai,Erpeng Xue,Lei Wang*

TL;DR: TTRL在数学推理基准上通过多数投票伪标签信号实现显著准确率提升，但本文指出这些提升主要源于对已可解问题的强化而非真正学习，且错误修正不可逆。提出TTRL-Guard框架，包含三种机制：基于翻转率的奖励缩放（FRS）、少数正确答案保留采样（MPS）和风险条件稀疏更新（RCSU），有效应对‘正确答案消失窗口’现象。实验表明，在多个模型和基准上表现优异，尤其在Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct和Qwen3-4B上取得最佳平均通过率，相较于TTRL在AIME 2025上提升54%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有TTRL方法依赖多数投票作为伪标签信号，但该机制在低能力问题中导致正确答案信号短暂激活后被永久压制，形成‘正确答案消失窗口’，造成不可逆的错误积累，因此需要一种能识别并缓解此问题的轻量级框架。

Method: 提出TTRL-Guard，包含三个核心机制：1）Flip-Rate-Aware Reward Scaling (FRS) 根据翻转率动态降低高风险样本的更新权重；2）Minority-Preserving Sampling (MPS) 保留少数正确答案的梯度信号；3）Risk-Conditioned Sparse Updatings (RCSU) 在极化问题上暂停更新，防止错误固化。

Result: 在三个模型和四个基准测试中，TTRL-Guard在Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct和Qwen3-4B上实现了最优平均pass@1性能，并在AIME 2025上相比TTRL相对提升54%，验证了其有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: TTRL-Guard成功缓解了因多数投票策略引发的正确答案消失窗口问题，显著提升了测试时强化学习在数学推理任务中的可靠性与准确性，为未来TTRL系统设计提供了重要改进方向。

Abstract: Test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL) reports substantial accuracy gains on mathematical reasoning benchmarks using majority vote as a pseudo-label signal. We argue these gains are systematically misinterpreted: most reflect sharpening of already-solvable problems rather than genuine learning, while problems corrupted from correct to incorrect outnumber truly learned ones, and this damage is irreversible once majority vote locks onto a wrong answer. Per-problem tracking reveals that correct-answer signals in low-ability problems are briefly active before being permanently suppressed, a phenomenon we term the \textit{Correct-Answer Extinction Window}, with Flip Rate (FR) as its leading indicator. We thus propose \textbf{TTRL-Guard}, a lightweight framework with three mechanisms targeting the extinction window: Flip-Rate-Aware Reward Scaling (FRS) down-weights at-risk updates as FR declines, Minority-Preserving Sampling (MPS) retains gradient signal from minority correct answers, and Risk-Conditioned Sparse Updatings (RCSU) suspends updates on polarized problems. Experiments across three models and four benchmarks show that TTRL-Guard achieves the best average pass@1 on Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct and Qwen3-4B, improves relatively over TTRL by +54\% on AIME 2025. \footnote{Our code and implementation details are available at https://github.com/linhxkkkk/TTRL-Guard.

</details>


### [279] [Sampling-Based Safe Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19469)

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于采样的安全强化学习（SBSRL）算法，通过在有限的动力学样本集合上联合施加约束来保证整个学习过程中的安全性，近似处理难以计算的最坏情况优化问题，在连续域中实现实际的安全保障。引入基于认知不确定性约束的探索策略，无需显式的探索奖励。在常规条件下，推导出学习过程中的高概率安全保证及恢复近优策略的有限时间样本复杂度界。实验表明，SBSRL在仿真和真实机器人硬件上均实现了安全高效的探索，并可扩展至高维连续控制问题的深度集成实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 安全探索是强化学习在现实世界中部署的核心挑战。现有方法往往难以在学习过程中持续保证安全性，尤其在连续状态-动作空间中。因此需要一种既能提供严格安全保证又能高效探索的新方法。

Method: SBSRL采用模型基方法，利用一组动态模型样本构建安全约束，通过联合优化这些样本上的约束来逼近最坏情况下的安全决策。同时设计基于认知不确定性的探索机制，避免依赖人工设定的探索奖励。理论分析建立在正则性假设基础上，推导出安全性和样本复杂度的高概率保证。

Result: SBSRL在多种仿真环境和真实机器人平台上验证了其安全性与探索效率，能有效应对高维连续控制任务。其深度集成版本表现出良好的可扩展性，且在不牺牲安全性的前提下快速收敛到近优策略。

Conclusion: SBSRL为强化学习中的安全探索提供了一个有效的解决方案，兼具理论保障与实际可行性，适用于复杂、高维的真实系统。

Abstract: Safe exploration remains a fundamental challenge in reinforcement learning (RL), limiting the deployment of RL agents in the real world. We propose Sampling-Based Safe Reinforcement Learning (SBSRL), a model-based RL algorithm that maintains safety throughout the learning process by enforcing constraints jointly across a finite set of dynamics samples. This formulation approximates an intractable worst-case optimization over uncertain dynamics and enables practical safety guarantees in continuous domains. We further introduce an exploration strategy based on constraining epistemic uncertainty, eliminating the need for explicit exploration bonuses. Under regularity conditions, we derive high-probability guarantees of safety throughout learning and a finite-time sample complexity bound for recovering a near-optimal policy. Empirically, SBSRL achieves safe and efficient exploration both in simulation and in real robotic hardware, and readily extends to practical deep-ensemble implementations that scale to high-dimensional continuous control problems.

Result: 成功从动态系统视角解释了生成模型中的记忆化现象，表明该现象源于训练过程中不同变量演化速度的差异所导致的双时间尺度行为，且与双下降现象存在潜在关联。

Conclusion: 本研究通过系统理论框架，揭示了生成模型记忆化现象的动态根源，强调了训练过程中的多尺度动力学作用，并为理解生成模型训练中的复杂行为提供了统一的理论视角。

Specifically, we use a result of Austin [2016] to motivate a stylized model for the loss function for stochastic gradient descent (SGD) wherein the loss function has a strong dependence on some variables and weak dependence on the rest in a precise sense. This naturally leads to two distinct time scales in the constant step size SGD that is commonly used in machine learning. This fact has been used to explain the double descent phenomenon in SGD in Borkar [2026]. [2024] in order to explain the phenomenon of memorization wherein a generative model that is concurrently being tuned yields the same or similar outputs for significant stretches of time. ### [281] [The Silent Hyperparameter: Quantifying the Impact of Inference Backends on LLM Reproducibility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19537)
*David Pape,Jonathan Evertz,Lea Schönherr*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 调研200种推理引擎，分析3.5万篇论文；在固定模型权重、解码参数和硬件条件下，对比vLLM、SGLang、llama.cpp等五个主流推理引擎在多个开源模型和基准上的表现，通过追踪执行流程识别关键优化组件的影响。

Result: 不同推理后端可导致基准分数差异达16.6个百分点，产生高频率输出分歧；系统级优化如前缀缓存、CUDA图、自定义内核及日志处理默认设置是主要诱因。

Conclusion: 推理后端是影响大模型评估结果的关键但常被忽略的超参数，应建立标准化报告机制，以提升基准测试的透明度、可复现性和公平性。

Abstract: Progress in LLMs is increasingly measured through standardized benchmarks, where state-of-the-art improvements are often separated by fractions of a percentage point. At the same time, the computational cost of evaluating modern LLMs has driven widespread adoption of specialized inference backends, software systems that execute trained models efficiently at inference time. While critical for scalability, system-level optimizations, such as custom CUDA kernels and reduced-precision arithmetic, can alter token probabilities and introduce non-determinism, possibly cascading into divergent generation. In this work, we first survey the inference landscape, identifying 200 distinct engines, and analyze 35,000 ML publications, finding that the specific inference stack is rarely reported despite this widespread diversity. We then present a systematic empirical study of how inference backends affect LLM benchmark results. Holding model weights, decoding parameters, and hardware constant, we evaluate five widely used inference engines, including vLLM, SGLang, and llama.cpp, across multiple open-weight models and established benchmarks. We show that the choice of backend alone can shift benchmark scores by up to 16.6 percentage points and induce high rates of output disagreement. By isolating backend optimizations and tracing the execution pipeline, we find this divergence is driven by system-level optimizations like prefix caching and CUDA graphs, custom kernels, and engine-specific defaults in logit processing. Our findings identify the inference backend as a previously unreported but consequential hyperparameter in the evaluation of LLM and advocate standardized reporting of inference stacks to improve the reproducibility and interpretability of benchmark comparisons.

### [282] [TORQ: Two-Level Orthogonal Rotation for MXFP4 Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19561)
*Zukang Xu,Xing Hu,Dawei Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出TORQ（Two-level Orthogonal Rotation for MXFP4 Quantization），一种无需训练的后训练量化（PTQ）框架，用于解决MXFP4格式在大语言模型激活量化中因结构失衡导致的精度下降问题。通过宏观层面的块间正交旋转与微观层面的熵引导块内旋转，有效缓解了块间方差不均和码本利用不均的问题，显著提升4比特浮点量化性能。在LLaMA3和Qwen3等主流模型上实验表明，其性能接近全精度（BF16），大幅缩小低比特量化与高精度之间的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MXFP4虽具高动态范围与硬件效率优势，但直接应用于LLM激活量化时会引发显著精度损失，根源在于激活分布与MXFP4块浮点格式之间的结构性失衡，亟需新的量化方法以实现高效且高精度的低比特推理。

Method: 提出TORQ框架，基于舒尔-霍恩定理进行块间正交旋转以均衡激活能量分布，防止高方差块主导缩放因子；同时采用最大熵引导的块内旋转，提升码本利用率，避免码本坍塌，从而优化激活空间的几何特性。

Result: 在Qwen3-32B上，WikiText perplexity降至8.43（对比BF16为7.61），平均准确率从直接RTN的38.40%提升至73.63%（对比BF16为74.82%），显著缩小4比特浮点量化与全精度之间的性能差距。

Conclusion: TORQ通过两层正交旋转有效解决了MXFP4激活量化中的结构性失衡问题，实现了无需训练的高性能低比特推理，在保持硬件效率的同时大幅提升了量化模型的精度，为下一代低比特大模型部署提供了有力支持。

Abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) advance toward practical deployment, the Microscaling FP4 (MXFP4) format has emerged as a cornerstone for next-generation low-bit inference, owing to its ability to balance high dynamic range with hardware efficiency. However, directly applying MXFP4 to LLM activation quantization inevitably leads to significant accuracy degradation. In this paper, we theoretically analyze the error structure of MXFP4 activation quantization, revealing that the root cause of this performance drop lies in two structural imbalances between activation distributions and the MXFP4 block floating-point format: (1) extreme inter-block variance imbalance and (2) intra-block codebook utilization imbalance. To address these challenges, we propose TORQ (Two-level Orthogonal Rotation for MXFP4 Quantization), a training-free Post-Training Quantization (PTQ) framework designed to reshape the geometric properties of the activation space through optimal coordinate transformations. At the macroscopic level, TORQ leverages the Schur-Horn theorem to redistribute activation energy via inter-block orthogonal rotation, preventing high-variance blocks from driving up shared scaling factors and thereby preserving the precision of small-magnitude elements. At the microscopic level, TORQ employs maximum-entropy-guided intra-block rotation to alleviate codebook collapse and maximize the MXFP4 codebook's information capacity. Experiments on mainstream LLMs such as LLaMA3 and Qwen3 show that TORQ significantly improves the accuracy of MXFP4 activation quantization compared to existing methods: on Qwen3-32B, the perplexity on WikiText is reduced to 8.43 (vs. 7.61 for BF16), and the average accuracy increases from 38.40% with direct RTN to 73.63% (vs. 74.82% for BF16), substantially narrowing the gap between 4-bit floating-point quantization and full-precision inference.

</details>


### [283] [Online Market Making and the Value of Observing the Order Book](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19584)
*Davide Maran,Marcello Restelli*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线学习模型假设完全掩盖反馈，而真实限价订单簿中，未成交时可获得供需信息，该信息对市场做市至关重要。本文旨在揭示此类部分反馈的价值，改进传统带宽反馈模型的性能局限。

Method: 提出行动依赖反馈模型；在随机设定下使用消除算法；在均值回归设定下引入新浓度不等式分析；在对抗性设定下设计探索-扰动算法。

Abstract: We study an online market-making problem in which a learner sequentially posts bid and ask prices for a single asset while interacting with traders holding private valuations. Unlike existing online learning formulations that assume fully censored feedback, we introduce an action-dependent feedback model inspired by real limit order books: when a trade occurs, the trader's valuation remains hidden, whereas when no trade occurs, informative feedback about supply and demand is revealed.
  We show that this additional information fundamentally changes the learnability of the problem. In the stochastic setting with i.i.d. market prices, we propose an elimination-based algorithm that achieves $O(\sqrt T)$ regret with high probability, without requiring any smoothness assumptions on the distribution of trader valuations. We then extend this result to a broad class of mean-reverting price processes by considering both local, autoregressive dynamics and a weaker global drift condition based on cumulative deviations from the mean. Under either assumption, we establish high-probability $O(\sqrt T)$ regret bounds, relying on a new concentration inequality of independent interest. Finally, in the adversarial setting with oblivious prices, we design an explore-then-perturb algorithm that guarantees $O(T^{2/3})$ regret in expectation.
  Our results quantify the value of observing the order book in online market making and demonstrate that even limited, action-dependent feedback can substantially improve regret guarantees compared to standard bandit feedback models.

### [284] [MiMuon: Mixed Muon Optimizer with Improved Generalization for Large Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19619)
*Feihu Huang,Yuning Luo,Songcan Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了Muon优化器的泛化误差，证明其为 $O\big(\frac{1}{Nκ^{T}}\big)$，并提出改进的MiMuon优化器，通过梯度正交化融合动量SGD，将泛化误差降低至 $O\big(\frac{1}{N}\big)$，同时保持相同的收敛速度 $O(\frac{1}{T^{1/4}})$。实验验证了MiMuon在Qwen3-0.6B和YOLO26m等大模型上的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究已关注Muon优化器的收敛性，但其泛化性能尚未建立。由于$κ$通常很小，原Muon的泛化误差随$T$指数衰减，但实际效果受限，因此亟需提升泛化能力。

Method: 基于算法稳定性与数学归纳法分析泛化误差，设计混合优化器MiMuon，结合梯度正交化与动量机制，实现更优泛化性能。

Result: 理论证明MiMuon具有更低的泛化误差 $O(\frac{1}{N})$ 和相同的收敛率 $O(\frac{1}{T^{1/4}})$；实验表明其在大模型训练中高效可靠。

Conclusion: MiMuon优化器通过合理引入梯度正交化，在不牺牲收敛速度的前提下显著提升了泛化性能，为大规模模型优化提供了新思路。

Abstract: Matrix-structured parameters frequently appear in many artificial intelligence models such as large language models. More recently, an efficient Muon optimizer is designed for matrix parameters of large-scale models, and shows markedly faster convergence than the vector-wise algorithms. Although some works have begun to study convergence properties (i.e., optimization error) of the Muon optimizer, its generalization properties (i.e., generalization error) is still not established. Thus, in this paper, we study generalization error of the Muon optimizer based on algorithmic stability and mathematical induction, and prove that the Muon has a generalization error of $O\big(\frac{1}{Nκ^{T}}\big)$, where $N$ is training sample size, and $T$ denotes iteration number, and $κ>0$ denotes minimum difference between singular values of gradient estimate. To enhance generalization of the Muon, we propose an effective mixed Muon (MiMuon) optimizer by cautiously using orthogonalization of gradient, which is a hybrid of Muon and momentum-based SGD optimizers. Then we prove that our MiMuon optimizer has a lower generalization error of $O\big(\frac{1}{N}\big)$ than $O\big(\frac{1}{Nκ^{T}}\big)$ of Muon optimizer, since $κ$ generally is very small. Meanwhile, we also studied the convergence properties of our MiMuon algorithm, and prove that our MiMuon algorithm has the same convergence rate of $O(\frac{1}{T^{1/4}})$ as the Muon algorithm. Some numerical experimental results on training large models including Qwen3-0.6B and YOLO26m demonstrate efficiency of the MiMuon optimizer.

### [285] [Optimal Reconstruction from Linear Queries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19625)
*Yuval Filmus,Shay Moran,Elizaveta Nesterova*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究从近似线性查询中重建 $\mathbb{R}^d$ 中未知点的问题，旨在刻画重构误差随查询次数 $T$、维度 $d$ 和噪声参数 $\delta$ 变化的最优性能。当 $T \to \infty$ 时，最优误差收敛至 $\sqrt{2d/(d+1)}\delta$，类似监督学习中的贝叶斯最优误差；固定维度下，超出该极限的误差以双指数速率衰减；维度增长时，需约 $\exp(d)$ 次查询才能实现可忽略的过剩误差。技术上，提出并证明了朱恩定理（Jung's theorem）的鲁棒推广，利用对称性和李群作用进行几何与动力学分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在低维遥感、信号恢复、高维数据分析及隐私敏感推断等应用中，如何从有限且带噪声的线性查询中高效重建未知点是一个核心问题。现有工作缺乏对最优重构误差与查询次数、维度和噪声之间关系的系统刻画，尤其在高维情形下的理论边界不明确。因此，亟需建立统一的理论框架来揭示此类问题的内在极限。

Method: 通过几何分析与动力系统方法，结合对称性与李群作用，提出并证明了经典朱恩定理的鲁棒版本。利用该工具，分析渐近行为（$T \\to \\infty$）与有限样本下的误差界，并引入非正则化变体以拓展适用范围。

Result: 确定了在 $T \\to \\infty$ 时最优重构误差为 $\\sqrt{2d/(d+1)}\\delta$；固定 $d$ 时，过剩误差呈双指数衰减；当 $d$ 增大时，需 $\\Theta(\\exp(d))$ 次查询才能使误差趋于零；同时，所提出的鲁棒朱恩定理为理解近极值集合提供了新视角。

Conclusion: 本研究不仅揭示了线性查询重建问题的理论极限，还通过推广经典几何定理建立了新的数学工具。结果表明，在高维情形下信息获取成本急剧上升，而算法设计必须考虑维度与噪声之间的权衡。该框架对实际系统的设计与性能评估具有重要指导意义。

Abstract: We study the problem of reconstructing an unknown point in $\mathbb{R}^d$ from approximate linear queries. This setting arises naturally in applications ranging from low-dimensional remote sensing and signal recovery to high-dimensional data analysis and privacy-sensitive inference. Our main goal is to characterize the optimal reconstruction error as a function of the number of queries $T$, the ambient dimension $d$, and the noise parameter $δ$.
  We first analyze the limit $T \to \infty$ and show that the optimal reconstruction error converges to the explicit value $\sqrt{2d/(d+1)} δ$, which plays a role analogous to the Bayes optimal error in supervised learning. When the dimension is fixed, we show that the excess error above this limit decays doubly exponentially fast as $T \to \infty$, a rate that is significantly faster than those typically encountered in learning curves. When the dimension grows, we show that a number of queries on the order of $\exp(d)$ is necessary and sufficient to achieve vanishing excess error. Finally, we introduce and analyze an improper variant of the reconstruction problem.
  From a technical perspective, our main contribution is a generalization of Jung's theorem (1901). The classical theorem bounds the maximum possible radius of a set of diameter 1 and characterizes extremal bodies. Our generalization provides a robust variant that characterizes near-extremal bodies and is proved via geometric and dynamical arguments exploiting symmetry and Lie group actions.

</details>

*Paul Krzakala,Gabriel Melo,Camille Lançon,Charlotte Laclau,Rémi Flamary,Etienne Thévenot,Florence d'Alché-Buc*

Result: MSAlign在多个基准上表现优于现有方法，具有简单易实现、训练速度快、性能稳定等优势；所提出的分布偏移度量有效揭示了不同划分策略的潜在偏差，为评估提供新视角。

Abstract: Accurately identifying metabolites i.e. small molecules from mass spectrometry data remains a core challenge in metabolomics, with broad applications in drug discovery, environmental analysis, and clinical research. We address the Molecule Retrieval task, which consists in recovering the chemical structure of a metabolite from its MS/MS spectrum given a set of candidate molecules. While the recent release of benchmark datasets such as MassSpecGym and Spectraverse has considerably accelerated the development of novel machine learning approaches, the complexity of data preprocessing pipelines and the lack of unified implementations make methods and results difficult to reproduce and compare. We make three contributions. First, we propose a unified framework encompassing recent approaches based on representation alignment and contrastive learning. Second, we introduce MSAlign, inspired by multimodal alignment in vision-language models, which learns a shared representation space by aligning two frozen foundation models (DreaMS for mass spectra and ChemBERTa for molecules) through lightweight MLP projections trained with a candidate-based contrastive objective. MSAlign is simple to implement, fast to train and consistently outperforms existing approaches across all benchmarks. Third, we investigate a long-standing evaluation problem: data splitting strategies in molecule retrieval implicitly trade off data leakage against domain shift. We formalize this tension by introducing a quantitative measure of distribution shift, and use it to evaluate splitting strategies in existing benchmarks. All datasets, splits, candidate sets, and a unified implementation of MSAlign and baselines are publicly released to support reproducible research.

### [287] [AR1-ZO: Topology-Aware Rank-1 Zeroth-Order Queries for High-Rank LoRA Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19767)
*Ziye Chen,Hongbin Lin,Chenyu Zhang,Xiangda Yan,Yongjie Yang,Yao Shu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出AR1-ZO方法，解决零阶（ZO）优化与LoRA结合时的秩悖论问题。通过配对交替的秩-1原子查询与拓扑感知缩放，实现无需额外基底、激活钩子或曲率估计的秩不变信号恢复，在标准双前向传递预算下显著提升高秩LoRA在零阶优化中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统两步零阶优化在与LoRA结合时面临秩悖论：增加LoRA秩虽提升适配器容量，但标准有限差分信号易因坐标扰动维度依赖或原子级更新导致信号不可观测。核心瓶颈在于测量拓扑而非需外部子空间。

Method: 提出基于匹配秩-1原子的交替查询策略，每步仅查询一个原子，保持适配器秩为r的同时降低单次查询扰动维度；引入拓扑感知缩放γ=αr，避免信号随秩衰减，防止方向坍塌。

Result: 理论证明了原子最小性、秩无关的活跃查询维度、方向坍塌与恢复机制，以及剩余秩依赖作为摊销覆盖成本；实验在OPT和Qwen3模型上验证信号机制，显示AR1-ZO在相同预算下优于其他零阶方法，使高秩LoRA有效可行。

Conclusion: AR1-ZO通过拓扑感知的原子级查询与缩放设计，突破了零阶优化中高秩LoRA的应用瓶颈，实现了无需额外开销的高效、稳定训练，为大规模模型微调提供了新范式。

Abstract: Zeroth-order (ZO) optimization enables large-language-model fine-tuning without storing backpropagation activations, while LoRA supplies compact trainable adapters. Combining them creates a rank paradox: increasing LoRA rank improves adapter capacity, but standard two-point ZO either perturbs a rank-dependent number of coordinates or, under atomwise updates, can make the finite-difference signal unobservable. This paper shows that the bottleneck is a measurement-topology problem rather than a need for an external subspace. LoRA already decomposes into matched rank-$1$ atoms, each a complete factor-coordinate block of dimension $d_\text{out}+d_\text{in}$. Querying one atom per step keeps the stored adapter rank $r$ while removing $r$ from the single-query perturbation dimension. The naive atomwise query is still miscalibrated: if it inherits canonical LoRA scaling $α/r$, the active finite-difference signal shrinks as $1/r$ and the active finite-difference signal-to-noise ratio (FD-SNR) as $1/r^2$, producing directional collapse under a fixed residual evaluation-noise floor. AR1-ZO pairs alternating rank-$1$ atom queries with topology-aware scaling $γ=αr$, restoring rank-invariant active signal without auxiliary bases, activation hooks, curvature estimates, or extra forward queries. Theory proves atom minimality, rank-independent active query dimension, directional collapse and restoration, and the remaining rank dependence as an amortized coverage cost. Experiments on OPT and Qwen3 models validate the signal mechanism and show that AR1-ZO makes high-rank LoRA effective among matched-budget ZO methods under the standard two-forward-pass query budget.

### [288] [Latent Laplace Diffusion for Irregular Multivariate Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19805)
*Zinuo You,Jin Zheng,John Cartlidge*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不规则多变量时间序列的长期预测面临挑战：离散方法因重采样会破坏时间结构，而连续时间模型通常需要逐步求解，易产生漂移。需一种既能保持时间连续性又避免逐步积分的方法。

Method: 提出 Latent Laplace Diffusion (LLapDiff)，将目标建模为低维潜在轨迹；采用基于随机端口-哈密顿动力学的稳定模态参数化；在拉普拉斯域中使用可学习的共轭极点表示均值演化；通过更新-平均分析将采样间隔映射为有效事件域极点，设计间隙感知历史摘要器。

Result: LLapDiff 在长期预测任务中表现优于现有基线方法；其连续时间生成特性支持在历史时间戳上查询以完成缺失值插补；代码已开源。

Conclusion: LLapDiff 有效解决了不规则多变量时间序列长期预测中的关键难题，兼具时间连续性和高效生成能力，为复杂动态系统的建模提供了新范式。

Abstract: Irregular multivariate time series impose a trade-off for long-horizon forecasting: discrete methods can distort temporal structure via re-gridding, while continuous-time models often require sequential solvers prone to drift. To bridge this gap, we present Latent Laplace Diffusion (LLapDiff), a generative framework that models the target as a low-dimensional latent trajectory, enabling horizon-wide generation without step-by-step integration over physical time. We guide the reverse process utilizing a stable modal parameterization motivated by stochastic port-Hamiltonian dynamics, and parameterize its mean evolution in the Laplace domain via learnable complex-conjugate poles, enabling direct evaluation over irregular timestamps. We also link continuous dynamics to irregular observations through renewal-averaging analysis, which maps sampling gaps to effective event-domain poles and motivates a gap-aware history summarizer. Extensive experiments show that LLapDiff improves over baselines in long-horizon forecasting, and its continuous-time generative nature supports missing-value imputation by querying the same model at historical timestamps. Code is available at https://github.com/pixelhero98/LLapDiffusion.

### [289] [LionMuon: Alternating Spectral and Sign Descent for Efficient Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19811)
*Arman Bolatov,Artem Riabinin,Nikita Kornilov,Andrey Veprikov,Samuel Horváth,Martin Takáč,Aleksandr Beznosikov*

TL;DR: LionMuon combines Lion's low-cost updates with Muon's strong directionality by alternating between them on a fixed period P, using a shared dual-EMA buffer. It achieves better performance than Muon, Lion, Signum, and AdamW at lower compute, with theoretical guarantees under heavy-tailed noise.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To combine the low computational cost of sign-based optimizers like Lion with the superior convergence properties of Muon, while maintaining efficient memory usage.

Method: Alternating between Lion and Muon updates every P steps, sharing a single dual-EMA momentum buffer; also introduces a simpler single-EMA variant, SignMuon.

Result: LionMuon outperforms Muon, Lion, Signum, and AdamW across multiple datasets and architectures (124M to 720M models), achieving lower validation loss with less compute. Theoretical bounds confirm its efficiency under heavy-tailed noise.

Conclusion: LionMuon provides a Pareto-optimal trade-off between update effectiveness and computational cost, making it highly effective for large-scale optimization.

Abstract: In large-scale optimization, the cheapness and effectiveness of update steps are the most crucial factors for a successful optimizer. Sign-based optimizers like Lion or Signum produce cheap per-step updates, whereas Muon's spectral matrix-sign update gives a much stronger direction at a substantially higher per-step cost. In this work, we propose LionMuon, which retains the effectiveness of Muon steps while considerably cutting the averaged iteration cost, similar to sign-based methods. It alternates between Lion's and Muon's updates on a fixed period P, sharing a single dual-EMA momentum buffer between them. The optimizer state memory therefore matches Lion and is exactly half of AdamW's. A simpler single-EMA variant, SignMuon, by itself already outperforms pure Muon. At P = 2, LionMuon Pareto-dominates Muon, Lion, Signum, and AdamW on every dataset and architecture we tested at 124M model size, reaching lower validation loss at lower compute, and the same advantage persists at 355M and 720M scale. On the theory side, we prove sharp complexity bounds under heavy-tailed noise which are governed by period-averaged smoothness and noise that interpolate between Muon's and Lion's constants. These bounds predict the compute-optimal period and the conditions under which LionMuon outruns Muon and Lion. Code: https://github.com/brain-lab-research/lion-muon

*Anya Fries,Jacob A Nelson,Martin Jung,Markus Reichstein,Jonas Peters*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FLUXtrapolation 是一个用于评估生态系统通量在日益严峻的分布偏移下外推性能的基准测试。该研究强调了通量上采样中的领域泛化挑战，包括协变量分布和条件分布的偏移，并通过时间、空间和温度等场景评估模型表现。初步研究表明，现有基线模型在中位数小时均方根误差下表现相似，但在尾部误差和多尺度评估中差异明显，凸显了新基准的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在初步研究中，现有基线模型在中位数小时均方根误差（RMSE）上表现相近，但在尾部误差和多尺度评估中表现出显著差异，表明传统评估指标不足以反映模型在极端或复杂条件下的真实性能。该基准揭示了当前方法在面对真实分布偏移时的局限性，为未来机器学习方法的发展提供了明确方向。

Conclusion: FLUXtrapolation 提供了一个现实且相关的挑战，推动机器学习方法在分布偏移下的改进，同时其进展将直接促进通量上采样的科学目标实现。该基准不仅具有技术价值，也具备重要的生态学应用意义。

Abstract: We introduce FLUXtrapolation, a benchmark for extrapolating ecosystem fluxes under progressively harder distribution shifts. Ecosystem fluxes are central to understanding the carbon, water, and energy cycles, yet they can only be measured directly at sparsely located measurement towers. Producing global flux estimates therefore requires training models on observed sites using globally available covariates and predicting in unobserved regions, that is, upscaling. Flux upscaling is a challenging domain generalization problem that is affected by a shift in covariate distribution across climates, ecosystem types, and environmental conditions, as well as by conditional shift: important drivers remain unobserved at global scale. We provide a quantitative analysis of both these shifts in $P_X$ and $P_{Y\mid X}$. FLUXtrapolation is designed based on domain expertise on flux upscaling: it defines temporal, spatial, and temperature-based extrapolation scenarios and evaluates performance across held-out domains, temporal aggregations, and tail errors. In a pilot study, we find that baselines perform similarly under median hourly RMSE, but separate under the proposed tail-focused and multi-scale evaluation. FLUXtrapolation therefore poses a realistic and thus relevant challenge for machine learning methods under distribution shift; at the same time, progress on this benchmark would directly support the scientific goal of improving flux upscaling.

The protocol may use any number of adaptive rounds, and each client's local samples may be reused across rounds. For parameter estimation under squared \(\ell_2\) loss, we establish a federated van Trees lower bound for every estimator satisfying a total clientwise sample-level zero-concentrated differential privacy (zCDP) constraint. ### [292] [Set-Valued Policy Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19830)

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种适用于多治疗场景的集合值策略学习范式，通过输出一组可能的治疗方案而非单一推荐，实现内在的不确定性量化。该方法结合了学习延迟框架与置信区间思想，引入了新的'最大下界'方法和'符合性策略学习'，并采用随机注入技术确保边际覆盖率，无需对黑箱最优治疗规则做假设。在合成数据和体外受精（IVF）真实案例上的实验表明，所提方法能生成稳健且可操作的策略，兼顾性能与可靠性。

Abstract: Conventional treatment policies map patient covariates to a single recommended intervention in order to maximize expected clinical outcomes. Although a rich body of causal inference methods has been developed to estimate such policies, point-valued recommendations can be highly sensitive to estimation uncertainty, model specification, and finite-sample variability, while typically providing little guidance about how confident one should be in the recommended action. In this work, we propose a set-valued policy learning paradigm for the multiple-treatment setting, in which policies output a set of plausible treatments rather than a single recommendation. This formulation enables intrinsic uncertainty quantification, with the size of the predicted set reflecting the degree of decision ambiguity. We extend the learning-to-defer framework to multiple treatments via a novel \textit{greatest Lower Bound} method, and introduce \textit{conformal policy learning}, which bridges the gap between unobserved ground-truth optimal treatments and estimated optimal treatment rules. Drawing on insights from the noisy-label literature, we develop a randomness-injection approach that guarantees marginal coverage without requiring assumptions on underlying black-box optimal treatment rules. Through experiments on synthetic data and a real-world application to In-Vitro Fertilization (IVF), we demonstrate that our methods produce robust and actionable policies that naturally incorporate clinical considerations while effectively balancing performance and reliability.

Abstract: The progression of reinforcement learning algorithms have been driven by challenging benchmarks. The rate in which a researcher can iterate on a problem setting directly impacts the speed of algorithm development. Modern machine learning has produced tools that allow for fast and scalable algorithm development like the JAX library. Most notably, the JAX reinforcement learning ecosystem does not have any benchmarks that test visual first-person tasks; these domains are crucial for testing both exploration and an agent's ability to overcome partial observability. Abstract: This work addresses the problem of learning directed acyclic graphs (DAGs) from nodal observations generated by a linear structural equation model. DAG learning is a central task in signal processing, machine learning, and causal inference, but it remains challenging because acyclicity is a global combinatorial property. Continuous acyclicity constraints have led to important algorithmic advances by replacing the discrete DAG constraint with smooth equality constraints. However, existing formulations still involve difficult non-convex optimization landscapes and may suffer from degenerate first-order optimality conditions. Here, we restrict attention to DAGs with non-negative edge weights and exploit this additional structure to obtain a simpler characterization of acyclicity. Building on this characterization, we formulate a regularized non-negative DAG learning problem and develop an algorithm based on the method of multipliers. We further analyze the benign optimization landscape induced by non-negativity. Numerical experiments on synthetic and real-world data show that the proposed method improves over state-of-the-art continuous DAG-learning alternatives.

Using the LLM system prompt to estimate a robust baseline, we standardize user-token entropies and apply a one-sided CUSUM statistic. The resulting detector, CPD Online (CPD), is model-agnostic, training-free, runs online, and localizes the adversarial suffix onset. ### [296] [Your Neighbors Know: Leveraging Local Neighborhoods for Backdoor Detection in Decentralized Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19969)
*Sayan Biswas,Antoine Boutet,Davide Frey,Romaric Gaudel,Rachid Guerraoui,Maxime Jacovella,Anne-Marie Kermarrec,Dimitri Lerévérend,François Taïani,Martijn de Vos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Argus is a decentralized backdoor detection framework for decentralized learning (DL) that operates without a central server or prior knowledge of triggers. It enables honest nodes to locally analyze model updates, collaboratively share potential triggers, and use structural similarity to distinguish true backdoors from false positives caused by data heterogeneity. The method ensures convergence with theoretical guarantees and significantly reduces attack success rates while preserving model utility.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Decentralized learning (DL) is vulnerable to backdoor attacks due to its collaborative nature, yet existing defenses often fail to account for DL's constraints like the absence of a central coordinator and lack of trigger knowledge. There is a need for a native, decentralized solution that can detect backdoors effectively under real-world conditions.

Method: Argus uses local analysis of model updates by honest nodes, followed by collaborative sharing of detected triggers among neighbors. A structural similarity metric identifies consistent patterns across participants, filtering out false positives caused by data heterogeneity. Malicious senders are evicted if they persistently fail the test.

Result: Argus reduces attack success rates by up to 90 percentage points compared to no defense, maintains model utility within 5 percentage points of an ideal oracle, and performs better as data heterogeneity increases. It provides the first theoretical convergence guarantees for DL-specific backdoor detection.

Conclusion: Argus offers a practical, scalable, and theoretically sound solution for backdoor detection in decentralized learning, effectively defending against attacks while maintaining system performance and adaptability to heterogeneous data environments.

Abstract: Decentralized learning (DL) is an emerging machine learning paradigm where nodes collaboratively train models without a central server. However, the collaborative nature of DL makes it vulnerable to backdoor attacks, where a model is taught to behave normally on standard inputs while executing hidden, malicious actions when encountering data with specific triggers. Backdoor attacks in DL remain understudied and existing defenses often overlook DL constraints. We introduce Argus, a novel backdoor detection framework native to DL that requires neither a central coordinator nor prior knowledge of the trigger. In Argus, honest nodes locally analyze received model updates to identify potential backdoor triggers. Nodes then collectively share their triggers with their neighbors and use a structural similarity metric to separate true backdoors from false alarms induced by data heterogeneity. A key insight is that false positive triggers exhibit inconsistencies across participants while true positive ones show consistent patterns. Model updates that fail this collaborative test are rejected, and persistently malicious senders are eventually evicted. We provide the first theoretical convergence guarantees for a DL-specific backdoor detection mechanism, showing that filtering out suspicious model updates with high probability preserves a convergence rate comparable to standard DL. We implement and evaluate Argus on three standard datasets and against three state-of-the-art baselines. Across settings, Argus reduces attack success rates by up to 90 points compared to no defense, while preserving model utility within 5 percentage points of an omniscient oracle. Furthermore, the effectiveness of Argus compared to baselines improves as data heterogeneity increases.

### [297] [Block-Sphere Vector Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19972)
*Heesang Ann,Joongkyu Lee,Min-hwan Oh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种统一的理论框架，用于比较现有的基于旋转的量化方法（如EDEN、RabitQ、TurboQuant），并揭示其性能优势依赖于具体的失真准则。进一步提出了新的块球面量化算法BlockQuant，通过在球面上对向量块进行量化，更忠实保留随机旋转后的嵌入几何结构，在重建均方误差和期望内积失真方面均表现出理论优势。实验结果表明，该方法在真实嵌入数据集和长上下文大模型推理任务中实现了与理论预测一致的实际性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有旋转基量化方法（如EDEN、RabitQ、TurboQuant）的比较缺乏统一标准，因使用不同失真度量、概率设定和实现假设而难以公平评估；同时，传统坐标式量化无法充分保留旋转后嵌入的几何特性，限制了性能优化空间。

Method: 提出统一理论分析框架，对比多种旋转基量化器的失真表现；设计基于球面几何的块量化算法BlockQuant，采用块级球面量化策略，以更好地保持旋转嵌入的结构特性，并从理论上证明其在均方误差和期望内积失真上的优越性。

Result: 理论分析显示，不同量化方法的优势取决于失真度量：EDEN和TurboQuant在均方误差下表现优；EDEN在期望内积失真下也有效；RabitQ在高概率控制上更强。实验验证了BlockQuant在真实数据集和长上下文大模型推理任务中的实际性能提升，且与理论预测一致。

Conclusion: BlockQuant通过引入块球面量化机制，显著提升了旋转基量化在几何保持与失真控制方面的性能，为高效、可扩展的机器学习系统提供了更优的量化方案。

Abstract: Vector quantization is a fundamental primitive for scalable machine learning systems, enabling memory-efficient storage, fast retrieval, and compressed inference. Recent rotation-based quantizers such as EDEN, RabitQ, and TurboQuant have introduced strong guarantees and empirical performance, but the surrounding comparisons have been difficult to interpret because they rely on different distortion criteria, probability regimes, and implementation assumptions. As our first contribution, we provide a unified theoretical comparison of these methods and show that their relative advantages are criterion-dependent rather than absolute: EDEN and TurboQuant are favorable for MSE distortion, EDEN is also effective for expected inner-product distortion, and RabitQ provides strong high-probability control. This comparison further clarifies that EDEN provides particularly strong guarantees for expected distortion measures. As our second contribution, we introduce Block-Sphere Quantization (BlockQuant), a new rotation-based block quantization algorithm designed around the spherical geometry of randomly rotated vectors. Unlike coordinate-wise quantizers, BlockQuant quantizes blocks on the sphere, preserving the geometry of rotated embeddings more faithfully. We prove that this block-spherical design theoretically improves over the baselines considered in this paper for both reconstruction MSE and expected inner-product distortion. Our experiments on real embedding datasets and long-context LLM inference tasks show practical gains that are consistent with our theoretical improvements.

### [300] [Fine-Tuning Without Forgetting via Loss-Adaptive Learning Rates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20005)
*Parjanya Prajakta Prashant,Jiongli Zhu,Aldan Creo,Babak Salimi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FINCH提出一种基于损失自适应的学习率调度策略，通过在高损失批次降低学习率、模型收敛时提升学习率，有效缓解大语言模型微调中的灾难性遗忘问题。该方法不修改原有微调目标，却在知识获取、科学问答和低资源语言适配等任务上显著减少遗忘（平均降低93%），同时保持与标准微调相当的任务性能，并在多个指标上改善模型的置信度校准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通过抑制高损失样本或序列来缓解灾难性遗忘，但这些样本对新任务学习至关重要，尤其在预训练覆盖不足的情况下。因此需要一种不抑制关键样本的学习率调整机制，以控制遗忘而不影响新知识获取。

Method: 提出FINCH方法，基于观察到的每步遗忘受学习率与当前训练损失平方根乘积限制的规律，设计损失自适应学习率调度：高损失批次降低学习率，随模型收敛逐步提高学习率。

Result: 在多个基准测试中，FINCH平均减少93%的遗忘；在Qwen3-4B知识获取任务中，将TruthfulQA性能下降降低5倍，并逆转HaluEval的性能退化，同时更好保持置信度校准。

Conclusion: 学习率调度是塑造模型微调行为的有效工具，不仅能优化目标任务表现，还能有效缓解灾难性遗忘，且无需改变原有微调目标。

Abstract: Fine-tuning large language models on new data improves task performance but degrades capabilities learned during pretraining, a phenomenon known as catastrophic forgetting. Existing methods mitigate this by modifying the fine-tuning objective to suppress high-loss tokens or sequences, but these tokens are essential for learning new tasks, especially those with poor pretraining coverage. In such settings, hard tokens should still contribute to learning, so forgetting must be controlled without suppressing them. We identify a simple mechanism for doing so: per-step forgetting is bounded by the product of the learning rate and the square root of the current training loss. This suggests that high-loss batches are especially prone to inducing forgetting. Motivated by this observation, we introduce FINCH, a loss-adaptive learning-rate schedule that reduces the learning rate on high-loss batches and increases it as the model converges, while leaving the fine-tuning objective unchanged. Across knowledge acquisition, science, and low-resource language adaptation benchmarks, FINCH reduces forgetting by 93% on average while matching the task performance of standard fine-tuning. On Qwen3-4B knowledge acquisition, FINCH cuts TruthfulQA degradation by 5x and reverses HaluEval degradation, while better preserving confidence calibration. Overall, our results show that learning-rate schedules are an effective tool to shape model behavior during fine-tuning, beyond just target-task optimization.

*Salil Parth Tripathi,Bertrand Chapron,Fabrice Collard,Nicolas Courty,Ronan Fablet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为意图控制的部分最优传输（IC-POT）的新方法，通过点对点的拒绝成本替代传统的全局拒绝机制，使拒绝决策能基于侧信息、可靠性或支持几何结构进行。该方法具有双重解释：局部接受阈值与扩展支持上的平衡Kantorovich问题，并在正-未标记学习和开放部分域适应中提升了基线性能。最后以多模态卫星海洋观测为例，展示了其在物理和传感器先验指导下的实际应用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统部分最优传输采用全局预算或统一拒绝规则，难以满足需要结构化、点对点拒绝决策的应用场景；当拒绝决策应依赖于侧信息、可靠性或外部知识时，现有方法不足。因此需要更灵活的拒绝机制来适应复杂实际需求。

Method: 引入意图控制的部分最优传输（IC-POT），用点对点的拒绝成本取代全局拒绝规则，将问题转化为在扩展支撑集上的平衡Kantorovich最优传输问题，并通过双重解释实现求解。

Result: IC-POT在正-未标记学习和开放部分域适应任务中优于基线方法；在多模态卫星海洋观测中，利用物理与传感器先验构建合理的拒绝机制，有效提取可比信号信息。

Conclusion: IC-POT提供了一种灵活且可解释的框架，用于建模基于上下文的点对点拒绝，在多种实际任务中表现出优越性，尤其适用于有明确先验信息指导匹配过程的场景。

Abstract: While optimal transport (OT) enforces a rigid constraint by requiring two measures to be matched exactly, partial optimal transport relaxes this requirement by allowing mass to remain unmatched through a global budget, scalar rebate, or uniform rejection rule. However, many applications call for more structured, pointwise rejection mechanisms, where the decision to leave mass unmatched depends on side-specific reliability, support geometry, or external information about which components should participate in the comparison. We introduce \emph{intent-controlled partial optimal transport} (IC-POT), a targeted generalization of partial transport that replaces the global rejection paradigm with pointwise rejection costs over both measures. We show that the resulting optimization problem admits a dual interpretation in terms of local acceptance thresholds and can be solved by recasting it as a balanced Kantorovich OT problem on an augmented support. Beyond theoretical analysis, we demonstrate the practical relevance of IC-POT in settings where rejection is driven by side information. In positive-unlabeled learning and open-partial domain adaptation, incorporating pointwise rejection rules that encode statistical structure improves fixed baseline pipelines. Finally, we motivate the use of IC-POT with a geophysical practical case: multi-modal satellite ocean measurements, for which physical and sensors priors naturally inform the rejection mechanism and define the retrieved comparable signal information.

</details>


### [303] [CAMERA: Adapting to Semantic Camouflage in Unsupervised Text-Attributed Graph Fraud Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20032)
*Junjun Pan,Yixin Liu,Yu Zheng,Lianhua Chi,Alan Wee-Chung Liew,Shirui Pan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 欺诈者通过模仿良性用户的文本响应来隐藏其恶意目的，这种语义伪装现象破坏了传统基于结构和属性线索的欺诈检测假设，使得无监督检测变得困难。

Method: 采用去中心化混合专家架构，每个专家专注于建模不同类型的欺诈线索；引入上下文感知门控模型，结合中心节点表示及其局部邻域上下文，自适应融合各专家学习到的线索；利用欺诈者稀有性支持无监督单类学习，鼓励建模主流良性模式。

Result: 在4个具有挑战性的数据集上实验表明，CAMERA consistently优于现有方法，对语义伪装的欺诈者具有良好的检测效果。

Conclusion: CAMERA框架能够有效应对语义伪装的欺诈行为，在无监督条件下实现可靠欺诈检测，具备较强的实用性和泛化能力。

Abstract: Text-attributed graph fraud detection (TAGFD) plays a critical role in preventing fraudulent activities on online social and e-commerce platforms. However, to evade detection, fraudsters continuously evolve their camouflaging strategies by deliberately mimicking textual responses of benign users, thereby concealing their malicious purposes. This phenomenon, referred to as semantic camouflage, fundamentally undermines commonly relied assumptions on how structural and attribute cues can be exploited to identify fraudsters, and makes it difficult to spot fraudsters with unsupervised TAGFD. To bridge the gaps, we propose a Case-Adaptive Multi-cue Expert fRAmework (CAMERA) for unsupervised TAGFD. CAMERA employs an ego-decoupled mixture-of-experts architecture, where each expert specializes in modeling a distinct type of fraud-indicative cue. A context-informed gating model is introduced to jointly consider the ego node representation and its local neighborhood context for adaptive integration of cues learned by different experts. Furthermore, CAMERA leverages the inherent rarity of fraudsters to support unsupervised one-class learning with expert-level objectives that encourage modeling dominant benign patterns, thereby enabling reliable unsupervised detection of camouflaged fraudsters. Experiments on 4 challenging datasets show that CAMERA consistently outperforms competitors, showing its effectiveness against semantically camouflaged fraudsters. Code available at https://github.com/CampanulaBells/CAMERA

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: D$^3$-Subsidy成功构建了一个可扩展、响应迅速且符合约束的城市级司机侧补贴控制系统，具备良好的工业部署潜力，为大规模出行平台的动态供需调节提供了有效解决方案。

These requirements rule out expensive per-order optimization, calling for a forward-looking, constraint-aware city-level controller for online sequential decision making. To meet these requirements, we introduce D$^3$-Subsidy (Dynamic Driver-side Diffusion-based Subsidy), a hierarchical diffusion-based framework for deployable city-wide subsidy control. To bridge the train-inference gap, D$^3$-Subsidy employs a prefix-conditioned diffusion model that samples plausible future trajectories from immutable historical observations, ensuring the training protocol aligns with the fixed-history nature of online deployment. These generated plans are then decoded by a context-conditioned inverse module into low-dimensional city-level control signals. For scalable execution, we bridge the gap between city-level planning and fine-grained dispatch via a Lagrangian-dual-derived mapping, which embeds subsidy-rate caps directly into order-driver incentives without iterative optimization. Additionally, a multi-city pretraining strategy with parameter-efficient fine-tuning enables robust transfer across heterogeneous cities. ### [305] [Active Context Selection Improves Simple Regret in Contextual Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20040)
*Mohammad Shahverdikondori,Jalal Etesami,Negar Kiyavash*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究具有有限上下文空间的上下文多臂赌博机问题，其中学习者为每个上下文推荐最优动作，并以上下文加权简单后悔率进行评估。在奖励分布最坏情况下，对上下文分布向量 $p$ 保持实例依赖性。允许学习者主动选择采样上下文，对于已知 $p$，通过被动采样（随机揭示上下文）获得 $\sqrt{n/T \, \lVert p \rVert_{1/2}}$ 的后悔率，而通过主动采样（分配比例 $q_j \propto p_j^{2/3}$）可达到紧致的 $\sqrt{n/T} \, \lVert p \rVert_{2/3}$ 后悔率，性能提升可达 $Θ(k^{1/4})$（$k$ 为上下文数量）。进一步分析了预算受限的主动采样，刻画了相应的紧致后悔率，并识别出何时有限主动预算即可恢复完全主动采样性能。当 $p$ 未知时，提出探索-再探索-承诺（EETC）算法，可最优平衡估计上下文分布与切换至主动采样所需时间，在长周期下达到与已知 $p$ 时主动采样相当的常数倍后悔率。实验结果支持理论发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在上下文多臂赌博机问题中，传统方法通常被动接受上下文样本，无法根据上下文分布动态调整采样策略。然而，实际应用中往往可以主动选择观察哪些上下文，从而更高效地获取信息。本文旨在利用这种主动采样能力，设计更优的策略，尤其在上下文分布 $p$ 已知或未知的情况下，实现更优的后悔率性能。

Method: 提出基于主动采样的上下文多臂赌博机算法框架，针对已知 $p$ 的情况，设计最优采样分配 $q_j \\propto p_j^{2/3}$ 以最小化后悔率；针对预算受限情形，引入资源约束下的优化采样策略；当 $p$ 未知时，提出 Explore-Explore-Then-Commit (EETC) 算法，通过两阶段探索过程估计 $p$ 并最终进入主动采样阶段。

Result: 已知 $p$ 时，主动采样可实现 $\sqrt{n/T} \\lVert p \\rVert_{2/3}$ 的紧致后悔率，优于被动采样的 $\sqrt{n/T \\lVert p \\rVert_{1/2}}$，性能提升可达 $\\Theta(k^{1/4})$。预算受限下仍可逼近完全主动性能。未知 $p$ 时，EETC 算法在长周期下达到与已知 $p$ 主动采样相当的常数倍后悔率。大量实验验证了理论分析的有效性。

Conclusion: 主动采样显著提升了上下文多臂赌博机问题的性能，尤其是在上下文分布 $p$ 已知或可通过有效算法估计时。本文提出的 EETC 算法在未知 $p$ 情况下实现了接近最优的后悔率，证明了主动采样在实际应用中的巨大潜力。

Abstract: We study the contextual multi-armed bandit problem with a finite context space (a.k.a. subpopulations), where the learner recommends a best action for each context and is evaluated by context-weighted simple regret. Our guarantees are worst-case over the reward distributions, while remaining instance-dependent with respect to the context distribution vector $p$. Akin to experimental design problems where the population of interest is fixed but the sampled subpopulation can be controlled, we allow the learner to actively choose which context to sample from. For a known $p$, we characterize tight regret rates: passive sampling where contexts are randomly revealed achieves regret of order $\sqrt{n/T \, \lVert p \rVert_{1/2}}$, whereas active sampling with allocation $q_j \propto p_j^{2/3}$ achieves the tight rate $\sqrt{n/T} \, \lVert p \rVert_{2/3}$. The resulting improvement can be as large as $Θ(k^{1/4})$, where $k$ is the number of contexts. We further extend the analysis to budgeted active sampling, characterize the corresponding tight rate, and identify when a limited active budget suffices to recover the fully active rate. When $p$ is unknown, we propose the Explore-Explore-Then-Commit (EETC) algorithm, which optimally balances estimating the context distribution and the time to switch to active allocation, such that for large horizons, it matches the known-$p$ active rate up to constants. Experiments on synthetic and real-world data support our theoretical findings.

</details>


### [306] [Smooth Partial Lotteries for Stable Randomized Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20069)
*Alexander Goldberg,Giulia Fanti,Nihar B. Shah*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出平滑性作为部分抽奖机制的设计原则，引入剪切线性抽奖（Clipped Linear Lottery），通过在上下阈值间线性调整入选概率，实现对评分微小变动的鲁棒性。理论证明其最坏情况下的后悔值接近平滑规则的下界，且在真实同行评审数据集（ICLR 2025、NeurIPS 2024、瑞士国家科学基金会）上验证了现有抽奖设计的不稳定性，并展示了所提方法在平滑性与实用性之间更优的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有部分抽奖机制对评分微小变化敏感，导致选择概率剧烈波动，削弱了抽奖机制降低细粒度评分差异影响的核心目标。因此需要一种更稳定的机制来保障公平性和可预测性。

Method: 提出平滑性作为设计原则，形式化为评分到入选概率映射的Lipschitz条件；设计剪切线性抽奖机制，其入选概率在上下阈值间线性变化，高于上限则必选，低于下限则必弃。

Result: 理论分析表明，剪切线性抽奖的最坏后悔值逼近平滑规则的理论下界（误差因子为(1 - k/n)）；实证结果表明，现有抽奖机制在真实数据中极不稳定，而所提方法在平滑性与实用性之间表现更优。

Conclusion: 剪切线性抽奖是一种稳定、高效且理论性能接近最优的局部抽奖机制，适用于需要减少评分敏感性的竞争性选拔场景。

Abstract: Competitive selection processes, from scientific funding to admissions and hiring, use evaluations to score candidates, and eventually choose a subset of them based on those scores. Recently, many organizations have adopted partial lotteries, which randomize selection based on evaluation scores. However, existing lottery designs are inherently unstable, as a small change to a single candidate's score can cause large shifts in their selection probabilities. This instability undermines a key goal of lotteries: reducing the influence of fine-grained score distinctions near the decision boundary. We propose smoothness as a design principle for partial lotteries, formalizing it as a Lipschitz condition on the mapping from review scores over candidates to selection probabilities. We introduce the Clipped Linear Lottery, a simple mechanism in which selection probabilities scale linearly with estimated quality between an upper threshold, above which we always accept, and a lower threshold, below which we always reject. We prove that the Clipped Linear Lottery's worst-case regret matches a lower bound for any smooth selection rule up to a factor of $(1 - k/n)$, where $k/n$ is the acceptance rate. We compare smooth selection to other stability notions like Individual Fairness and Differential Privacy, showing that the Clipped Linear Lottery achieves a better smoothness-regret tradeoff than alternatives. Experiments on real peer review data from ICLR 2025, NeurIPS 2024, and the Swiss National Science Foundation demonstrate that existing lottery designs are highly unstable in practice even under perturbations to a single score. Our experiments also confirm the tightness of our theoretical analysis and show that our proposed Clipped Linear Lottery achieves a better smoothness-utility tradeoff than alternatives in practice.
